ādi hita sādhanam iti atra tad abhāvāt āgamaḥ  asti iti ced na bhāvanā mātra mūla tvena tasya api anāśvāsa viṣaya tvāt eka deśa saṃvādena api pravṛttiḥ iti ced na svapna ākhyānavat anyathā api sambhavāt  na ca anupalabdhe bhāvanā api cora sarpādayaḥ  hi upalabdhā eva bhīrubhiḥ bhāvyante na ca karma yogayoḥ hita sādhana tvam kutaścid upalabdham na ca eta ca ta yoḥ sva rūpeṇa upalambhaḥ kvacid upayujyate bhāvanā asādhyaḥ  vā na ca asmin  anvaya vyatirekau sambhavataḥ deha antara yogya tvāt phalasya apratīta tayā tadanu dananu ṣṭhāne tad abhāvāt ca na ca kartṛ bhoktṛ rūpa ubhaya deha pratisandhānāt eva tad upapadyate tad abhāvāt na hi etasya pūrva karmaṇaḥ phalam idam anubhavāmi iti kaścid pratisandhatteḥ kecid tathā bhaviṣyanti iti sambhāvanā mātre api anāśvāsāt vinigamanāyām pramāṇa abhāvāt  pratipad ni śītha nidrāṇa prātar pratibuddha samasta upādhyāyavat  anyonya saṃvādāt  kapila ādiṣu samāśvāsa iti ced na eka janma pratisandhānavat janma antara pratisandhāne pramāṇa abhavāt  tathā api ca adhikāri viśeṣeṇa brāhmaṇatva ādi apratisandhāne anuṣṭhāna rūpasya āśvāsasya abhāvāt  na hi pūrva janmani mātā pitroḥ brāhmaṇyāt tad uttaratra brāhmaṇyam iti niyamaḥ yena sarga ādau varṇa ādi dharma vyavasthā syāt  īśvaravat  adṛṣṭa viśeṣa upanibaddha bhūta viśeṣā tabhedā nupalambhāt  atīndriya artha darśi tve ca anāśvāsasya ukta tvāt  etena brahmāṇḍa antara sañcāri varṇa vyavasthayā sampradāya pravartanam apāstam sañcāra śakteḥ abhāvāt  varṣa antara sañcaraṇam eva hi duṣkaram kutaḥ loka antara sañcāraḥ kutastarām ca brahmāṇḍa antara gamanam  aṇima ādi sampatteḥ evam api syā aditi ced na atra api pramāṇa abhāvāt  sambhāvanā mātreṇa samāśvāsa anupapatteḥ atha mahā jana parigrahāni atha anupapattiḥ eva atra pramāṇam iti ced na evambhūta eka kalpanayā eva upapattau bhūyas  kalpanāyāḥ  gaurava prasaṅgāt  videha nirmāṇa śkteḥ aṇima ādi vibhūteḥ ca avaśya abhyupagantavya tvāt astu eka eva iti ced  na tarhi īśvaram antareṇa anyatra samāśvāsa iti api ca janma saṃskāra vidyā ādeḥ śakteḥ svādhyāya karmaṇoḥ hrāsa darśanataḥ  hrāsaḥ sampradāyasya mīyatām pūrvam hi mānasyaḥ prajāḥ samabhavan tatas  apatya eka prayojana maithuna sambhavāḥ tatas  kāmā lā varjanīya sannidhi janmānaḥ idānīm deśa kāla ādi avasthayā paśu dharmāt eva bhūyiṣṭhāḥ pūrvam caru prabhṛtiṣu saṃskārāḥ samādhāyiṣata tatas  kṣetra prabhṛtiṣu tatas  garbha āditaḥ idānīm tu jāta iṣu laukika loka vyavahāram āśritya pūrvam sahasraśākhaḥ vedaḥ  adhyagāyi tatas  vyastaḥ tatas  ṣaḍaṅga ekaḥ tidānīm tu kvacid ekā śākhā iti pūrvam ṛta vṛttayaḥ  brāhmaṇāḥ prādya utiṣata tatas  amṛta śraddhā śama dama grahaṇa dhāraṇa ādi śakteḥ ahara har apacīyamāna tvāt  svādhyāya anuṣṭhāne śīryamāṇe kathañcid anuvartete viśva parigrahāt ca na sahasā sarva uccheda iti yuktam utpaśyāmaḥ gata anugati kaḥ  loka iti aprāmāṇika eva ācāraḥ na tu śākhā ucchedaḥ aneka śākhā gatā iti kartavyatā āpūraṇīya tvāt ekasmin  api karmaṇi anāśvāsa prasaṅgāt iti ced  na evam hi mahā jana parigrahasya upaplava sambhave plave vedā api gata anugatika tayā eva lokaiḥ parigṛhyanta iti na vedāḥ pramāṇam syuḥ tathā ca vṛścika bhiyā palāyamānasya āśīviṣa mukhe nipātaḥ etam eva ca kāla krama bhā vi śākhā uccheda bhāvi na mana aśvāsam āśaṅkamānaiḥ mahā ṛṣibhiḥ prativihitam atas  na ukta doṣaḥ  api na ca ayam ucchedaḥ  jñāna krameṇa yena ślāghyaḥ syāt  api tu pramāda madamānā alasya nāstikya paripāka krameṇa tatas ca uccheda antaram punar  pravāhaḥ tad anantaram ca punar uccheda iti sārasvatam iva srotaḥ anyathā kṛta hāna prasaṅgāt  tathā ca bhāvi pravāhavat  bhavan  api ayam uccheda pūrvaka iti anumīyate smarati ca bhagavān vyāsaḥ  gītāsu bhagavat vacanam  yadā yadā hi dharmasya glāniḥ bhavati bhārata abhyutthānam adharmasya tadā atmānam sṛjāmi aham paritrāṇāya sādhūnām vināśāya ca duṣkṛtām dharma saṃsthāpana arthāya sambhavāmi yuge yuge   gī      iti kaḥ punar ayam mahā jana parigrahaḥ hetu darśana śūnyaiḥ gahaṇa dhāraṇa artha anuṣṭhāna ādiḥ sa hi atra na syāt  ṛte nimittam na hi atra ālasya ādiḥ nimittam duḥkha maya karma pradhāna tvāt  na api anyatra siddha prāmāṇye abhyupāye anadhikāreṇa asmin  ananya gatika tayā anupraveśaḥ paraiḥ pūjyānām api atrā praveśāt  na api bhakṣya peyāt yad vaita rāgaḥ tad vibhāga vyavasthā paratvāt na api kutarka abhyāsa āhati vyāmohaḥ ākumāram pravṛtteḥ na api sambhavat vipralambha pāṣaṇḍa saṃsargaḥ pitṛ ādi krameṇa pravartanāt  na api yoga abhyāsa abhimānena avyagra tā abhisandhiḥ prāthamikasya karma kāṇḍe kāṇḍa eva sutarām vyagra tvāt  na api jīvikā prāk uktena nyāyena dṛṣṭa phala abhāvāt na api kuhaka vañcanā prakṛte tad asambhavāt  sambhavati tu ete hetavaḥ  bauddha ādi āgama parigrahe tathā hi bhūyas tatra karma lāghavam iti alasāḥ itas  patitānām api anupraveśa iti ananya gatikāḥ bhakṣya ādi aniyama iti rāgiṇaḥ sva icchayā pari yārtha pari graha iti kutarka abhyāsinaḥ pitṛ ādi krama abhāvāt pravṛttiḥ iti pāṣaṇḍa saṃsargiṇaḥ  ubhayoḥ antaram jñātvā kasya śaucam vidhīyate  ityādi śravaṇāt avyagra tā abhimāninaḥ sapta ghaṭikā bhojana ādi siddheḥ jīvikā iti ayogyāḥ āditya stambhanam pāṣāṇa pāṭanam śākhā bhaṅgaḥ bhūta āveśaḥ pratimā jalpanam dhātuvāda ityādi dhandhanāt  vañcanāt  kuhaka vañcitāḥ tān parigṛṇhanti iti sambhāvyate atas  na te mahā jana parigṛgītā iti vibhāgaḥ syāt etad  yadi evam sarva karmaṇām vṛtti virodhaḥ na kiñcid utpadyate na kiñcid vinaśyati iti stimita ākāśa kalpe jagati kutaḥ viśeṣāt  punar  sargaḥ prakṛti pariṇateḥ iti sāṅkhyānām śobhate brahma pariṇateḥ iti bhāskara gotre yujyate vāsanā paripākāt iti saugata matam anudhāvati kāla viśeṣāt iti ca upādhi viśeṣa abhāvāt ayuktam asatām ca upalakṣaṇānām na viśeṣaka tvam sarvadā tulya rūpa tvāt  na ca jñāna dvārā anityasya tasya tadānīm abhāvāt nityasya ca viṣayataḥ svarūpataḥ ca aviśeṣāt iti ced  na śarīra saṅkṣobha śrama janita nidrāṇām prāṇinām āyuḥ paripāka krama sampādana eka prayojana śvāsa santāna anuvṛttivat  mahābhūta samplava saṅkṣobha labdha saṃskārāṇām paramāṇūnām mandataratamādi bhāvena kāla avaccheda eka prayojanasya pracaya ākhya saṃyoga paryantasya karma santānasya īśvara niḥśvasitasya anuvṛtteḥ kiyāna sau  iti atra avirodhāt  āgama prasiddhim anatikramya tāvantam eva kālam iti anumanyate brahmāṇḍa antara vyavahāraḥ  vā kāla upādhiḥ tad avacchinne kāle punar  sargaḥ yathā khalu alābula tāyām vitatāni phalāni tathā parameśvara śaktau  anusyūtāni sahasraśas  aṇḍāni iti śrūyate evam viccheda sambhave kasya kena parigrahaḥ yatas  prāmāṇyam syāt  jñāpakaḥ ca ayam arthaḥ na kārakaḥ tatas  kāraka abhāvāt nivartamānam kāryam jñāpaka abhimataḥ kathaṅkāram āsthāpayet na ca karma yogayoḥ hita sādhana tvam kutaścid upalabdham na ca eta ca ta yoḥ sva rūpeṇa upalambhaḥ kvacid upayujyate bhāvanā asādhyaḥ  vā na ca asmin  anvaya vyatirekau sambhavataḥ deha antara yogya tvāt phalasya apratīta tayā tadanu dananu ṣṭhāne tad abhāvāt ca na ca kartṛ bhoktṛ rūpa ubhaya deha pratisandhānāt eva tad upapadyate tad abhāvāt na hi etasya pūrva karmaṇaḥ phalam idam anubhavāmi iti kaścid pratisandhatteḥ kecid tathā bhaviṣyanti iti sambhāvanā mātre api anāśvāsāt vinigamanāyām pramāṇa abhāvāt  pratipad ni śītha nidrāṇa prātar pratibuddha samasta upādhyāyavat  anyonya saṃvādāt  kapila ādiṣu samāśvāsa iti ced na eka janma pratisandhānavat janma antara pratisandhāne pramāṇa abhavāt  tathā api ca adhikāri viśeṣeṇa brāhmaṇatva ādi apratisandhāne anuṣṭhāna rūpasya āśvāsasya abhāvāt  na hi pūrva janmani mātā pitroḥ brāhmaṇyāt tad uttaratra brāhmaṇyam iti niyamaḥ yena sarga ādau varṇa ādi dharma vyavasthā syāt  īśvaravat  adṛṣṭa viśeṣa upanibaddha bhūta viśeṣā tabhedā nupalambhāt  atīndriya artha darśi tve ca anāśvāsasya ukta tvāt  etena brahmāṇḍa antara sañcāri varṇa vyavasthayā sampradāya pravartanam apāstam sañcāra śakteḥ abhāvāt  varṣa antara sañcaraṇam eva hi duṣkaram kutaḥ loka antara sañcāraḥ kutastarām ca brahmāṇḍa antara gamanam  aṇima ādi sampatteḥ evam api syā aditi ced na atra api pramāṇa abhāvāt  sambhāvanā mātreṇa samāśvāsa anupapatteḥ atha mahā jana parigrahāni atha anupapattiḥ eva atra pramāṇam iti ced na evambhūta eka kalpanayā eva upapattau bhūyas  kalpanāyāḥ  gaurava prasaṅgāt  videha nirmāṇa śkteḥ aṇima ādi vibhūteḥ ca avaśya abhyupagantavya tvāt astu eka eva iti ced  na tarhi īśvaram antareṇa anyatra samāśvāsa iti kāram kāramalaukikā adbhuta mayam māyā vaśāt saṃharan hāram hāram api indra jālam iva yaḥ kurvan jagat krīḍati tam devam niravagraha sphurat abhidhyāna anubhāvam bhavam viśvāsa eka bhuvam śivam prati naman bhūyāsamantyeṣu api nanu etad api katham tatra bādhaka sadbhāvāt  tathā hi yadi syāt  upalabhyeta ayogya tvāt  san  api na upalabhyata iti ced  evam tarhi śaśa śṛṅgam api ayogya tvāt na upalabhyata iti syāt  na etad evam śṛṅgasya yogya tayā eva vyāpta tvāt iti ced  cetanasya api yogyā upādhi mat tayā eva vyāpta tvāt  tad bādhe saḥ  api bādhita eva iti tulyam vyāpaka sva artha ādi anupalambhena api anumīyate nīsti iti kaḥ  hi prayojanam antareṇa kiñcid kuryāt iti ucyate yogyā dṛṣṭiḥ kutaḥ ayogye pratibandiḥ kutastarām kva ayogyam bādhyate śṛṅgam kva anumānam anāśrayam sva ātmā eva tāvat  yogyā anupalabdhyā pratiṣiddhum na śakyate kutas tu ayogyaḥ para ātmā paramātmā tathā hi suṣupti avasthāyām ātmānam anupalabhamānaḥ na asti iti avadhārayet kasya aparādhenapunar  yogyaḥ  api ātmā tadānīm na upalabhyate sāmagrī vaiguṇyāt  jñāna ādi kṣaṇika guṇa upadhāne hi ātmā gṛhyata iti asya svabhāvaḥ jñānam eva kutaḥ na jāyata iti cintyate paścāt vā katham utpatsyata iti ced  manasaḥ  anindriya pratyāsanna tayā jananāt tad pratyāsattau ca paścāt jananāt  manaḥ vaibhava vādinām idam asaṃmatam tathā hi manaḥ  vibhu sarvadā sparśa rahita dravya tvāt sarvadā viśeṣa guṇa śūnya dravya tvāt nitya tve sati anārambhaka dravya tvāt jñāna asamavāyi kāraṇa saṃyoga ādhāra tvāt ityāde riti ced  na sarveṣām āpātatas  svarūpa asiddha tvāt tathā hi yadi rū yadā hi rū pādi upalabdhīnām kriyā tvena karaṇa tayā manaḥ  anumitiḥ na tadā dravyatva siddhiḥ adravyasya api karaṇa tvāt  atha āsām eva sākṣātkāritaya indriya tvena tad anumātavyam tathā api vyāpakasya nirupādheḥ na indriya tvam iti upādhiḥ vaktavyaḥ tatra yadi tad yadi karṇa śaṣkulīvat  nipata śarīra avayavasya upādhi tvam tadā tāvat mātre vṛtti lābhaḥ tad doṣe ca vṛtti nirodhaḥ śrotravat  prasajyeta tatas  śarīra mātram upādhiḥ abhidheyaḥ ravaseyaḥ tathā ca tad avacchedena vṛtti lābhe  śirasi me vedanā pāde me sukha am iti ādya vyāpya vṛttitva pratīti virodhaḥ asamavāyi kāraṇa anurodhena vibhu kāryāṇām prādeśikatva niyamāt  śarīra tad avayava ādi paramāṇu paryanta upādhi kalpanāyām kalpanā gaurava prasaṅgaḥ niyama anupapattiḥ ca iti tatas  anya t eva ekam sūkṣmam upādhi tvena atīndriyam kalpanīyam tathā ca tasya eva indriya tve svābhāvike adhika kalpanāyām pramāṇa abhāvāt  dharmi grāhaka pramāṇa bādhaḥ atha jñāna krameṇa indriya sahakāri tayā tad anumānam tatas  sutarām prāc ukta doṣaḥ yadi ca manasaḥ  vaibhave api adṛṣṭa vaśāt krama upapādyeta tadā manasaḥ  asiddheḥ āśraya asiddhiḥ eva vaibhava hetūnām iti atha yatra adṛṣṭasya dṛṣṭa kāraṇa upahāreṇa upayogaḥ tatra tad pūrṇa tāyām kāryam utpadyata eva anyathā antya tantu saṃyogebhyaḥ  api kadācid  paṭaḥ na jāyota jātaḥ  api vā kadācid nirguṇaḥ syāt  balavat tā kulālena dṛḍha daṇḍa nunnam api cakram na bhrāmyeta yatra tu dṛṣṭa anupahāreṇa adṛṣṭa vyāpāraḥ tatra tad vaiguṇyāt  kāryān udayaḥ yathā paramāṇu karmaṇaḥ tad iha api yadi viṣaya indriya ātmanām samavadhānam eva jñāna hetuḥ tadā tad sadbhāve sadā eva kāryam syāt  na hi etad atiriktam api adṛṣṭasya upaharaṇīyam asti na ca sadā eva jñāna udayaḥ tatas  atiriktam apekṣitavyam tad ca yadi apisarvāṇi eva indriyāṇi vyapnoti tathā api karaṇa dharma tvena kriyā kramaḥ saṅgacchate akalpite tu tasmin  āyam nyāyaḥ pratipad tuḥ akaraṇa tvāt  cakṣuḥ ādīnām aneka tvāt  iti ced  nanu evam api yugapad jñānāni mā bhūvan yugapad jñānam tu kena vāryate bhavati eva samūha ālambanam ekam jñānam iti ced na eka indriya grahyeṣu iva nānā indriya grāhyeṣu api prasaṅgāt  teṣu api bhavati eva iti ced na vyāsaṅga kāle jñāna krameṇa vivāda viṣaye krama anumānāt  bubhutsā viśeṣeṇa vyāsaṅge kriyā krama iti ced  mai nai vam na hi eṣa bubhutsāyā mahimā yad  abubhutsite viṣaye jñāna sāmagryām satyām api na jñānam api tu na tatra saṃskāra atiśaya ādhāyakaḥ pratyayaḥ syāt  yadi tu abubhutsite viṣaye sāmagrīm eva sā nirundhyāt  ghaṭāya unmīlitam cakṣuḥ paṭam na eva darśayet  tasmāt  bubhutsā api indriya antarāt ākṛṣya bubhutsita artha grāhiṇī indriye manaḥ  niveśayantī yugapad jñāna anutpattau  upayujyate na tu svarūpataḥ vibhunaḥ  api manasaḥ  vyāpāra kramāt  krama iti ced na tasya saṃyoga atiriktasya karma rūpa tve vaibhava virodhāt  guṇa rūpa tve nityasya krama anupapatteḥ anityasya ca nitya eka guṇasya avibhu dravya saṃyoga asamavāyikāraṇaka tvena tad antareṇa anupapatteḥ tad api kalpayiṣyata iti ced  tad eva tarhi manaḥ sthāne niveśyatām lāghavāya tasmāt aṇu eva mana iti tathā ca tasmin  anindriya pratyāsanne nirupadhāna tvāt ātmanaḥ suṣupti avasthāyām anupalambhaḥ etad eva manasaḥ śīlam iti kutaḥ niścir ṇī tam iti ced  anvaya vyatirekābhyām na kevalam tasya kim tu sarveṣām eva indriyāṇām na hi viśeṣa guṇam anapekṣya cakṣuḥ ādi apidravye pravartate svapna avasthāyām katham jñānam iti ced  tad tad saṃskāra udbodhe viṣaya smaraṇena svapna vibhramāṇām utpatteḥ udbodha eva katham iti ced  mandataratamādi nyāyena bāhyānām eva śabda ādīnām upalambhāt  antatas  śarīrasya eva ūṣma ādeḥ pratipatteḥ yadā ca manaḥ tvacam api parihṛtya purītati vartate tadā suṣuptiḥ syāt etad  para ātmā tu katham parasya ayogyaḥ na hi sākṣātkāri jñāna viṣaya tām eva ayam na prāpnoti svayam api adarśana prasaṅgāt na api grahītuḥ eva ayam aparādhaḥ tasya api hi jñāna samavāyi kāraṇa tā eva tad yoga tā na api karaṇasya sādhāraṇa tvāt  na hi āsaṃsāram ekam eva mana ekam eva ātmānam gṛhṇāti iti atra niyāmakam asti svabhāva iti ced  tarhi muktau niḥsvabhāvattva prasaṅgaḥ tad eka artha tāyā apāyāt iti na bhojaka adṛṣṭa upagrahasya niyāmaka tvāt  yad hi manaḥ  yad śarīram yāni indriyāṇi yasya adṛṣṭena ākṛṣṭāni tāni tasya eva iti niyamaḥ tad uktam prāk   pratyātma niyamāt  bhukte ariti etena para buddhi ādayaḥ  vyākhyātāḥ tad evam yogyā anupalabdhiḥ parātmā ādau na asti tad itarā tu na bādhikā iti tava api saṃmatam atas  kim adhikṛtya pratibandiḥ na hi śaśa śṛṅgam ayogya anupalabdhyā kaścid niṣedhati na ca prakṛte yogyā anupalabdhim kaścid manyate atha ayam āśayaḥ ayogya śaśaśṛṅga ādau  anupalabdhiḥ na bādhikā syāt  iti tatas  kim tad siddhyet iti ced  evam astu yadi pramāṇam asti paśutva ādikam iti ced  para sādhane pratibandiḥ tarhi na tad bādhane tatra eva bhaviṣyati iti ced  tad  kim tatra pratibandiḥ eva dūṣaṇam atha kathañcid tulya nyāyatayā yogyā eva parātma buddhi ādayaḥ te ca bādhitā eva iti apahṛta viṣaya tvam na prathamaḥ avyāpteḥ na hi paśutva ādeḥ śaśaśṛṅga sādhaka tvena kāryatva ādeḥ kartṛ mattva sādhaka tvam pyāptam yena tasmin  asati tad  pratiṣiddhyeta na dvitīyaḥ mithas  anupalabhyamāna tvasya vādi prativādi svīkārāt tathā api paśutva ādau kaḥ  doṣa iti ced  na jīnīmaḥ tāvat  tad vicāra avasare cintayiṣyāmaḥ syāt etad  yad pramāṇa gamyam hi yad  tad abhāva eva tasya abhāvam āvedayati yathā rūpa ādi prati patteḥ abhāvaḥ cakṣuḥ ādeḥ abhāvam kāya vāc vyāpāra eka pramāṇa kaśya para ātmā tad abhāva eva tasya abhāve pramāṇam aṅkura ādiṣu tad na tad eka pramāṇakatva asiddheḥ anyathā suṣuptaḥ  api na syāt  śvāsa santānaḥ  api tatra pramāṇam iti ced na niruddha pavanaḥ  api na syāt  kāya saṃsthāna viśeṣaḥ  api tatra pramāṇam iti ced na viṣa mūrcchitaḥ  api na syāt  śarīra uṣmā api tatra pramāṇam iti ced na jala avasikta viṣa mū sikta mū rcchitaḥ  api na syāt  tasmāt  yad yad kāryam upalabhyate tad tad anuguṇaḥ cetanaḥ tatra tatra siddhyati na ca kārya mātrasya kvacid vyāvṛttiḥ iti na ca tvad abhyupagatena eva pramāṇena bhavitavyam na anyena iti niyamaḥ  asti na ca prameyasya pramāṇena vyāptiḥ sā hi kārtsnyena vā syāt  eka deśena vā syāt  na prathamaḥ pratyakṣa ādi anyatamā ma sadbhāve api tad prameya avasthiteḥ na dvitīyaḥ puruṣa niyamena sarva pramāṇa vyāvṛttau  api prameya avasthiteḥ aniyamena asiddheḥ na hi sarvasya sarvadā sarvathā atra pramāṇam na asti iti niścayaḥ śakya iti katham tarhi cakṣuḥ ādeḥ abhāvaḥ  niścayaḥ vyāpaka anulabdheḥ carama sāmagrī niveśinaḥ hi kāryam eva vyāpakam tad nivṛttau tathābhūta anyā api nivṛttiḥ yogyatā mātrasya kadācid  kāryam tad nivṛttau tathābhūtasya api nivṛttiḥ anyathā tatra api sandehaḥ prakṛte api vyāpaka anupalabdhyā tad pratiṣedhaḥ  astu na āśraya asiddha tvāt na hi īśvaraḥ tad jñānam vā kvacid  siddham ābhāsa pratipannam iti ced na tasya āśrayatva anupapattaḥ pratiṣedhyatva anupapatteḥ ca vyāvartya abhāvavat tā eva bhāvikī hi viśeṣyatā abhāva viraha ātma tvam vastunaḥ pratiyogitā na ca etad ābhāsa pratipannasya asti iti kutas tasya niṣedha adhikaraṇa tvam niṣedhyatā ce ve ti katham tarhi śaśaśṛṅgasya niṣedhaḥ na kathañcid  sa hi abhāva pratyaya eva na ca ayam apāramārthika pratiyogikaḥ parama artha abhāvaḥ  nāma tathā apā na cāpā ramārthika viṣayam pramāṇam nāma iti api ca duṣṭa upalambha sāmagrī śaśaśṛṅga ādi yogya tā na tasyām na upalambhaḥ  asti na asti sa anupalambhane kena ca śaśa śaṅgam pratiṣiddhyate sarvathā anupalabdhasya yogyatva asiddheḥ tad itara sāmagrī sākalyam hi tad  nanu uktam ābhāsa upalabdham hi tad  ata eva aśakya niṣedham iti uktam anupalambha kāle ābhāsa upalambha sāmagryāḥ abhāvāt  tad kāle ca anupalambha abhāvāt iti kaḥ tarhi śaśa śṛṅgam na asti iti asya arthaḥ śaśe adhikaraṇe viṣāṇa abhāvaḥ  asti iti syāt etad  yadi api īśvaraḥ  na avagataḥ yadi api ca na ābhāsa siddhena pramāṇa vyavahāraḥ śakya sampādanaḥ tathā api ātmanaḥ siddhāḥ teṣām sārvajñyam niṣiddhyate kṣiti ādi kartṛ tvam ca iti tathā hi mad itare na sarva jñāḥ cena tvāt aham iva na ca te kṣiti ādi kartāraḥ puruṣa tvāt aham iva evam vastutva ādeḥ api iti tad etad api prāk eva parihṛtam tathā hi iṣṭa siddhiḥ prasiddha īśe hetu asiddhiḥ agocare na anyā sāmānyatas  siddhiḥ jātau  api tathā eva sā pramāṇa ṇena pratītānām cetanānām pakṣīkaraṇe siddha sādhanam tatas  anyeṣā masiddhau hetoḥ āśraya asiddha tvam ātmatva mātreṇa saḥ  api siddha iti ced  kaḥ  asya arthaḥ kim ātma tvena upalakṣitā sā eva vastu gatyā sarvajña viśva kartṛ vyaktiḥ atha tad anyā ātma mātram ātmatva mātra mā iva vā pakṣaḥ sarvatra pūrva doṣa an ativṛtteḥ ttiḥ atha ayam āśayaḥ ātma tvam na sarvajña sarva kartṛ vyakti samavetam jāti tvāt  gaḥ tvavat  iti tad asat  niṣedhya asiddheḥ niṣedhasya aśakya tvāt tathā ca aprasiddha viśeṣaṇaḥ pakṣa iti āśraya āsiddhiḥ iti sa eva doṣaḥ tvad upagata āgama loka prasiddhasya eva īśvarasya asarvajña tvam akartṛ tvam ca sādhyata iti ced na āgama ādeḥ pramāṇa tve bādhanāt aniṣedhanam ābhāsa tve tu sā eva syāt āśrayā siddhiḥ uddha tā nigadavyākhyātam etad  cārvākaḥ tu āha kim yogya tā viśeṣā ṣaṇā graheṇa yad na upalabhyate tad na asti viparītam asti na ca īśvara ādayaḥ tathā tatas  na santi iti etad eva jyāyaḥ evam anumāna ādi vilopa iti ced  na idam aniṣṭam tathā ca loka vyavahāra uccheda iti ced na sambhāvanā mātreṇa tad siddheḥ saṃvādena ca prāmāṇya abhimānāt  iti atra ucyate dṛṣṭi adṛṣṭyoḥ kva sandehaḥ  bhāva abhāva viniścayāt adṛṣṭi bādhite hetau pratyakṣam api durlabham sambhāvanā hi sandeha eva tasmāt ca vyavahāraḥ tasmin sati syāt  sa eva tu kutas  darśana daśāyām bhāva niścayāt  adarśana daśāyāma bhāva avadhāraṇāt tathā ca gṛhāt bahis ga nnirga taḥ ca arvākaḥ  varākaḥ  na nivartate pratyuta putra dāra dhana ādi bhāva avadhāraṇāt sa uraḥ tāḍam śoka vikalaḥ  vikrośet  smaraṇa anubhavān na evam iti ced na pratiyogi smaraṇa eva abhāva paricchedāt parāvṛttaḥ  api katham punar āsādayiṣyati sattvāt iti ced  anupalambha kāle api tarhi santi iti na tāvat mātreṇa abhāva avadhāraṇam tadā eva utpannā iti ced na anupalambhena hetūnām bādhāt  abādhe vā sa eva doṣaḥ ata eva pratyakṣam api na syāt  tad hetūnām cakṣuḥ ādīnām anupalambha bādhita tvāt  upalabhyanta eva golaka ādi rūpa tvāt teṣām iti ced na tad upalabdheḥ pūrvam teṣām anupalambhāt  na ca yaugapadya niyamaḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāvāt iti etena na paramāṇavaḥ santi anupalabdheḥ na te nityā niravayavā vā pārthiva tvāt  ghaṭa ādivat  na pāthasīya paramāṇu rūpādayaḥ  nityāḥ rūpa ādi tvāt  dṛśyamāna rūpa ādivat  na rūpatva pārthiva tu ādi nitya akārya ati indriya samavāyi jāti tvāt  śṛṅga tvavat  na indriyāṇi santi yogyā anupalabdheḥ ayogyāni ca śaśaśṛṅga pratibandi nirasanīyāni iti evam svarga apūrva devatā nirākaraṇam nāstikānām nisanīyam mīmāṃsakaḥ ca toṣayitavyaḥ  bhīṣayitavyaḥ ca iti yadi evam anupalambhena adṛśya pratiṣedhaḥ  na iṣyate anupalabhya upādhi pratiṣedhaḥ  api naiṣṭavyaḥ tathā ca katham tathābhūta artha siddhiḥ api anumāna bīja pratibandha asiddheḥ tad abhāve śabda ādeḥ api abhāvaḥ prāmāṇya asiddheḥ sā iyam ubhayatas  pāśā rajjuḥ atra kaścid āha mā bhūdupādhi vidhū nanam catur pañca rūpa sampatti mātreṇa eva pratibandha nirvāhāt  tasya āśya sa pakṣa āsa pakṣa darśana adarśana mātra pramāṇaka tvāt  yatra tu tad bhaṅgaḥ tatra pramāṇa bhaṅgaḥ  api āvaśyakaḥ na hi asti sambhavaḥ  darśana adarśanayoḥ aviplave hetu rūpa viplavaiti aprayojakaḥ  api tarhi hetuḥ syāt iti ced  bhūyas darśana aviplave kaḥ  ayam aprayojakaḥ  nāma na tāvat  sādhyam pratyakāryam akāraṇam vā sāmānyatas  dṛṣṭa anumāna svīkārāt na api sāmagryām kāraṇa eka deśaḥ pūrvavat abhyupagamāt  na api vyabhicārī tad anupalambhāt  vyabhicāra upalambhe vā sa eva doṣaḥ na ca śaṅkita vyabhicāraḥ nirbīja śaṅkāyāḥ sarvatra sulabha tvāt  na api vyāpya antara saha vṛttiḥ ekatra api sādhye aneka sādhana upagamāt na api alpa viṣayaḥ dhūma ādeḥ tathā abhāve api thābhūtasya api hetu tvāt  nanu dhūmaḥ  maḥ api vahni mātre aprayojaka eva tad nivṛttau  api tad anivṛtteḥ ārdra indhanava tvam vahni viśeṣam prati tu prayojakaḥ tad nivṛttau tasya eva nivṛtteḥ iti etad api ayuktam sāmānya prayojaka tāyām viśeṣa sādhakatva ayogāt tad asiddhau tasya asiddhi niyamāt siddhau vā sāmānya viśeṣa bhāva anupapatteḥ na api kḷpta sāmarthye anyasmin kalpanīya sāmarthyā prayojakaḥ nāśe kāryatva sāvayava tvayoḥ api hetu bhāvāt iti tad etad apeśalam katham hi viśeṣa abhāvāt kaścid vyabhicarati kaścid ca na iti śkayam avagantum tatas  nirṇāyaka abhāve sati sāhitya darśanam eva śaṅkā bījam iti kva asau nirbījā evam sati atiprasaktiḥ api cārvāka nandinī na upālambhāya svabhāvāt eva kaścid  kiñcid vyabhicarati kaścid ca na iti svabhāva eva viśeṣa iti ced  kena cihnena punar asau nirṇeya iti nipuṇena bhāvanīyam bhūyas darśanasya śataśas  pravṛttasya api bhaṅga darśanāt  yatra bhaṅgaḥ  na dṛśyate tad  tathā iti ced  āpātataḥ na dṛśyate iti sarvatra kāla krameṇa api na drakṣyata iti kaḥ  niyantā iti tasmāt upādhi tad virahau  eva vyabhicāra avi abhicāra nivandhanam tad avadhāraṇam ca aśakyam iti nanu yaḥ sarvaiḥ pramāṇaiḥ sarvadā asmad ādibhiḥ yadvat tayā na upalabhyate na asau tadvān yathā bakaḥ śyamikayā na upalabhyate ca vahnau dhūma upādhimattayā iti śkyam iti ced na asya api anumāna tayā tad apekṣāyām anavasthānāt sarva adṛṣṭeḥ ca sandehāt  svādṛṣṭeḥ vyabhicārātaḥ sarva dā itya siddheḥ tādātmya tad utpattibhyām niyama iti anye tatra tādātmyam vipakṣe bādhakāt  bhavati tad utpattiḥ ca paurvāparyeṇa pratyakṣa anupalambhābhyām na hi evam sati śaṅkā apiśācī avakāśam āsādayati āśaṅkyamāna kāraṇa bhāvasya api piśāca ādeḥ etad lakṣaṇa avirodhena eva tattva nirvāhāt iti na evam api ubhaya gāminaḥ  avyabhicāra nibandhanasya ekasya avivecanāt  pratyekam ca avyāpaka tvāt  kutas ca kārya ātmānau kāraṇam ātmānam ca na vyabhicārata iti atra ucyate śaṅkā ced anumā asti eva na ced śaṅkā tatas tarām vyāghāta avadhiḥ āśaṅkā tarkaḥ śaṅkā avadhiḥ mataḥ kāla antare kadācid vyabhicariṣyati iti kālam bhāvinam ākalayya śaṅkyeta tadā akalanam ca na anumānam avadhīrya kasyacid  mūhūrtayāmāhorātra pakṣa māsa ṛtu ayana saṃvatsara āt ayaḥ  hi bhāvinaḥ  bhavat muhūrta ādi anumeyā eva anavagateṣu smaraṇasya api anāśaṅkanīya tvāt anākalane vā kam āśritya vyabhicāraḥ śaṅkyeta raśaṅka iti tathā ca sutarām anumāna svīkāraḥ evam ca deśa antare api vaktavyam svīkṛtam anumānam suhṛd bhāvena pṛcchāmaḥ katham āśaṅkā nivartanīya iti ced  na yāvat āśaṅkam tarka pravṛtteḥ tena hi vartamānena upādhi koṭau tad ā āyatta vyabhicāra koṭau vā aniṣṭam upanayatā icchā vicchidyate vicchanna vipakṣa icchaḥ ca pramātā bhūyas darśana upalabdha sāhacaryam liṅga gamana ākulaḥ  adhitiṣṭhati adhiṣṭhitāt ca karaṇāt  kriyā pariniṣpattiḥ iti kim anupapannam nanu tarkaḥ  api avinābhāvam apekṣya pravartate tatas  anavasthayā bhavitavyam na śaṅkāyāḥ  vyāghāta  adhitvāt tad eva hi āśaṅkyate yasmin  āśaṅkyamāne sva kriyā vyāghātāt ayaḥ  doṣā na avataranti iti loka maryādā na hi hetu phala bhāvaḥ  na bhaviṣyati iti śaṅkitum api śakyate tathā sati śaṅkā eva na syāt  sarvam mithyā bhaviṣyati ityādivat  atha avyatīndriya upādhi niṣedhe kim pramāṇam i dhas  kiṃpramāṇaka i tyucyatām iti ced  na vai kaścid atīndriya upādhiḥ pramāṇa siddhaḥ  asti yasya abhāve pramāṇam anveṣaṇīyam kevalam sāhacarye nibandhana antara mātram śaṅkyate tatas  śaṅkā eva phalataḥ sva rūpataḥ ca nivartanīyā tatra phalam asyāḥ vipakṣasya api jijñāsā tarkāt āhanya nivartate tatas  anumāna pravṛttau śaṅkā svarūpam api iti sarvam sustham na ca etad anāgamam nyāya aṅga tayā tarkam vyutpādayataḥ sūtrakārasya abhimata tvāt  anyathā tad  vyutpādana vaiyarthyāt  tad ayam saṅkṣepaḥ yatra anukūla tarkaḥ  na asti saḥ  aprayojakaḥ sa ca dvividhaḥ śaṅkita upādhiḥ niścata upādhiḥ ca yatra idam ucyate  yāvat ca avyatireki tvam śata aṃśena api śaṅkyate vipakṣasya kutas tāvat  hetoḥ gamanikā balam tatra upādhiḥ tu sādhana avyāpaka tve sati sādhya vyāpakaḥ tad dharma bhūtā hi vyāptiḥ japā kusuma rakta tā iva sphaṭike sādhana abhimate cakāsti iti upādhiḥ asau  ucyata iti tad idam āhuḥ  anye para prayuktānām vyāptīnām upajīvakāḥ taiḥ dṛṣṭaiḥ api na eva iṣṭā vyapaka aṃśa avadhāraṇā   mī  ślaḥ  vā      iti tad anena vipakṣa daṇḍa bhūtena tarkeṇa sa nāthe bhūyas darśane kāryam vā kāraṇam vā tatas  anyat vā samavāyi vā saṃyogi vā anyathā vā bhāvaḥ vā abhāvaḥ  vā sa viśeṣaṇam vā nirviśeṣaṇam vā liṅgam iti niḥśaṅkam avadhāraṇīyam anyathā tad ābhāsa iti rahasyam tādātmya tad utpattyoḥ api etad eva bījam yadi hi kā yadi kār yātmānau kāraṇam ātmānam ca atipatetām tadā tayoḥ tattvam vyāhanyeta ata eva sāmagrī niveśinaḥ carama kāraṇāt api kāryam anumimate saugatā api tasmāt vipakṣa bādhakam eva pratibandha lakṣaṇam tathā hi śāka ādi āhāra pariṇati virahiṇi mitrātanaye na kiñcid aniṣṭam iti na asau tasya vyāpikā vyāpikā tu śyāmikāyāḥ kāraṇatva avadhāraṇāt kāraṇam ca tad  tasya tad atipatya bhavati ca iti vyāhatam evam anyatra api ūhanīyam iti kva punar aprayojakaḥ  antarbhavati na kvacid iti eke yathā hi siddha sādhanam na bādhita viṣayam viṣaya apahāra abhāvāt na api nirṇaye sati pakṣatvā ati pātāt apakṣa dharmaḥ kāla atīta vilopa prasaṅgāt  na ca anaikāntika ādiḥ vyabhicāra ādi abhāvāt  tathā ayam api sūtram tu upalakṣaṇa param iti tad asat  vibhāgasya nyūna adhika saṅkhyā vyavaccheda phala tvāt kva tarhi dvayoḥ antar niveśaḥ asiddhe eva tathā hi vyāptasya hi pakṣa dharma tā pratītiḥ siddhiḥ tad abhāvaḥ  asiddhi iyam ca vyāpti pakṣa dharma tā sva rūpāṇām anyatama apratītyā bhavantī yathāsaṅkhyam anyathā siddhiḥ āśrayā siddhiḥ svarūpa asiddhiḥ iti ākhyāyate madhyamā apya āśraya svarūpa apratītyā tad viśeṣaṇa pakṣatva apratītyā vā iti dvayī tatra carama asiddha sādhanam iti vyapadiśyate vyāpti sthitau pakṣatvasya ahatya vighaṭanāt  na tu evam bādhe vyāpteḥ eva prathamam vighaṭanāt iti viśeṣaḥ yadtva prayojakaḥ sandigdhā anaikāntika iti anaikāntike antar bhāvyate tad asat  vyāpti asiddhyā hi nimittena vyabhicāraḥ śaṅkanīyaḥ  anyathā vā prathame asiddhiḥ eva dūṣaṇam upajīvya tvāt  na anaikāntikam upajīvaka tvāt  anyathā śaṅkātva t ūṣaṇam eva nirṇīte tad anavakāśāt iti tṛtīya stabake īśvarasya upamāna abādhyatva nirūpaṇam upamānam tu bādhakamanāśaṅkanīyam eva viṣayān atirekāt iti kecid  tathā hi na tāvat asya viṣayaḥ sādṛśya vyapadeśyam padārtha antaram eva sambhāvanīyam paraspara virodhe hi na prakāra antara sthitiḥ na ekatā api viruddhānāmukti mātra virodhataḥ na hi bhāva abhāvābhyām anyaḥ prakāraḥ sambhāvanīyaḥ paraspara vidhi niṣedha rūpa tvāt na bhāva iti hi niṣedha mātreṇa eva abhāva vidhiḥ tatas tam vihāya katham sva vacanena eva punar sahṛdayaḥ  niṣedhet  na abhāva iti evam na abhāva iti hi niṣedha eva bhāva vidhiḥ tatas tam vihāya sva vācā eva anunmattaḥ katham punar niṣedhet  na bhāva iti ata evam bhūtānām eka tāpya śakya pratipattiḥ pratiṣedha vidhyoḥ ekatrā tvā sambhavāt  tasmāt bhāva abhāvau  eva tattvam bhāvat tve api guṇavat nirguṇam vā iti dvayam eva vā iti etad api pūrvavat  pūrvam dravyam eva uttarañca āśritam anāśritam vā iti dvayam eva pūrvavat  tatra uttaram samavāya eva anavasthā bhayāt  āśritam tu sāmānyavat niḥsāmānyañca iti pūrvavat dvayam eva tatra prathamam api spandaḥ  aspanda iti dvayam eva etad ca yathāsaṅkhyam karma guṇa iti vyapadiśyate niḥsāmānyam nirguṇam āśritam tu eka āśritam aneka āśritam vā iti prāk iva dvayam eva etad api yathāsaṅkhyam viśeṣaḥ sāmānyañca iti abhidhīyate tad  etad sādṛśyam etāsu ekām vidhāma āsādayat  na atiricyate anāsādayan  apadārthībhūya sthātum utsahate etena śakti saṅkhyādayaḥ  vyākhyātāḥ tatas  abhāvena saha sapta eva padārthā iti niyamaḥ atas  na upamāna viṣayor atha antaram iti syāt etad  bhavatu sāmānyam eva sādṛśyam tad eva tasya viṣayaḥ syāt  tad sa gaḥ sa dṛśaḥ  ayam iti hi pratyayaḥ na indriya janyaḥ tad āpāta mātreṇa anutpatteḥ iti ced  na pūrva piṇḍa anusandhāna rūpa sahakāri vaidhuryeṇa anutpatteḥ ṇa prāc ajananāt  saḥ  ayam iti pratyabhijñānavat iti nanu etad sadṛśaḥ sa iti na indriya janyam tena tasya asambandhāt nacedam smaraṇam tad piṇḍa anubhave api viśiṣṭasya ananubhavāt  naca etad api ayam sa iti viparīta pratyabhijñānavat upapādanīyam tad tedanta upasthāpana krama viparyaye api viśeṣyasya indriyeṇa sannikarṣa avirodhāt tasya sannihita vartamāna gocara tvāt prakṛte tu tad abhāvāt tasmāt  tad piṇḍa smaraṇa sahāyam etad piṇḍa varti sādṛśya jñānam eva tathāvidham jñānam utpādayat upamānam pramāṇam iti etad api na asti sādharmyam iva vaidharmyam mānam evam prasajyate arthāpattiḥ asau vyaktam iti ced  prakṛtam na kim yad  ā hi etad visadṛśaḥ  asau iti pratyeti tatra api tulyam etad  na hi tad  pratyakṣam asannikṛṣṭa viṣaya tvāt  na smaraṇam viśiṣṭasya ananubhavāt  na upamānam asādṛśya viṣaya tvāt nanu etad dharma abhāva viśiṣṭa tvam eva tasya vaidharmyam tad ca abhāva gamyam eva iṣyate na ca prakṛte api tathā astu sādṛśyasya bhāva rūpa tvāt iti ced  na itas  vyāvṛtta dharma viśiṣṭa tāyāḥ  api vaidharmya rūpa tvāt  tasya ca bhāva rūpa tvāt  syāt etad  tad dharmā iha na santi iti avagate arthāt āpadyate iha avidyamānāḥ tatra santi iti na hi tad vidharma tvam etasya upapadyate yadi etad vidharmā asau na bhavati iti ced  evam tarhi prakṛtam api artha āpattiḥ eva na hi tad sādṛśya viśiṣṭa tvam etasya pratyakṣa siddham api tasya etad sādṛśya viśiṣṭa tvam vinā upapadyate etena dṛṣṭā sannikṛṣṭa pratyabhijñānam vyākhyātam tatra api tad dharma śāli tvam tasya smaraṇa abhivyaktam anupapadyamānam tad idanta āspadasya ekatām vyavasthāpayati tasmāt na upamānam adhikam iti evam prāpte abhidhīyate sambandhasya paricchedaḥ dam sañjñāyāḥ sañjñinā saha pratyakṣa ādeḥ asādhya tvāt upamāna phalam viduḥ yath ā gauḥ tathā gavayaḥ iti śruta atideśa vākyasya gaḥ sadṛśam piṇḍam anubhavataḥ smarataḥ ca vākya artham ayam asau gavaya śabda vācya iti bhavati matiḥ sā iyam na tāvat  vākya mātra phalam anupalabdha piṇḍasya api prasaṅgāt  na api pratyakṣa phalam aśruta vākyasya api prasaṅgāt  na api samāhāra phalam vākya pratyakṣayoḥ bhinna kāla tvāt vākya tad arthayoḥ smṛti dvāra upanītau  api gavaya piṇḍa sambaddhena api indriyeṇa tad gata sādṛśya anupalambhe samaya pariccheda asiddheḥ phala samāhāre tu tad antarbhāve anumāna ādeḥ api pratyakṣatva prasaṅgaḥ tad  kim tad phalasya tad pramāṇa bahis bhāva eva antarbhāve vā kiyatī sīmā tad tad asādhāraṇa indriya ādi sāhityam asti tarhi sādṛśya ādi jñāna kāleviṣphāritasya cakṣuṣaḥ  vyāpāraḥ na upalabdha gosādṛśya viśiṣṭa gavaya piṇḍasya vākya tad artha smṛtimataḥ kāla antare api anusandhāna balāt samaya pariccheda upapatteḥ nanu ca vākyāt eva anena samayaḥ paricchinnaḥ gaḥ sadṛśasya gavaya śabdaḥ sañjñā iti kevalam idānīm pratyabhijānāti ayam asau  iti prayogāt va anumitaḥ yaḥ  yatra asati vṛtti antare vṛddhaiḥ prayujyate sa tasya vācakaḥ yathā gaḥ śabda eva goḥ prayujyate ca ayam gaḥ sadṛśe iti kim upamānena iti na sādṛśyasya animitta tvāt nimittasya apratītitaḥ samayaḥ  durgṛhaḥ pūrvam śabdena anumayā api vā na hi gavaya śabdasya sādṛśyam pravṛtti nimittam apratīta gūnām avyavahāra prasaṅgāt  na ca ubhayam api nimittam svayaṃpratīta samaya saṅkrāntaye ati deśa vākya prayoga anupapatteḥ gavayat tve hi ayam vyutpannaḥ  vṛddha vyavahārāt  na sādṛśye katham etad nirdhāraṇīyam iti ced  vastu gatiḥ tāvat iyam tad āpātatassandehe api na phala siddhiḥ gandhavat tvam iva pṛthivī tvasya gaḥ sādṛśyam gavaya śabda pravṛtti nimittasya upalakṣaṇam idam eva vā nimittam iti anirdhāraṇāt syāt etad  pūrvam nimitta anupalabdheḥ na phala siddhiḥ idānīntu tasmin  upalabdhe tad eva vākyam smṛti samārūḍham phaliṣyati adhyayana samaya gṛhīta iva vedarāśiḥ aṅga upāṅga paryavadātasya kāla antare na ca vācyam vākyena sva arthasya prāk eva bodhita tvāt  prāk eva paryavasitam iti gaḥ sādṛśyasya upalakṣaṇa nimitta tvayoḥ anyataratra tātparye sandehāt  idānīntu gavayatve avagate tarka puraskārāt sādṛśyasya upalakṣaṇa tāyām vyavasthitāyām gaṅgāyām ghoṣa itivat anvaya pratipattiḥ iti ced  na śruta anvayāt anā kāṅkṣam na vākyam hi anyat icchati padārtha anvaya vaidhuryāt tad ākṣiptena saṅgatiḥ gaḥ sadṛś aḥ  gavaya śabda vācya iti sāmānādhikaraṇya mātreṇa anvaya upapattau viśeṣa sandehe api vākyasya paryavasita tvena māna antara upanīta anapekṣaṇāt taktā rakta sandehe api ghaṭaḥ  bhavati iti vākyavat  anyathā vākya bheda doṣāt  na ca gaṅgāyām ghoṣa itivat  padārthā eva anvaya ayogyāḥ yena pramāṇa antara upanītena anvayaḥ syāt atha pratīta vākya artha bala āyātaḥ  api arthaḥ  yadi vākyasya eva divā bhojana niṣedha vākyasya api rātri bhojanam arthaḥ syāt tasmāt yathā gavaya śabdaḥ kasyacid vācakaḥ śiṣṭa prayogāt iti sāmānyatas  niścite api viśeṣe māna antara apekṣā tathā gaḥ sadṛśasya gavaya śabdaḥ  vācaka iti vākyāt niścitepi sāmānye viśeṣa vācaka tve asya māna antaram anusaraṇīyam iti astu anumānam tathā hi gavaya śabdaḥ  gavayasya vācakaḥ asati vṛtti antare abhiyuktaiḥ tatra prayujyamāna tvat  gavi gaḥ śabdavat iti ced  na asiddheḥ na hi asati vṛtti antare tad viṣaya tayā prayogaḥ saṅgatim avijñāya jñātum śakyate sāmāna adhikaraṇyāt iti ced na piṇḍa mātre siddha sādhanāt  nimitte ca asiddheḥ sādṛśyasya animitta tvāt iti uktam nanu vyāpti param idam vākyam syāt  yaḥ  gaḥ sadṛśaḥ sa gavaya padārtha iti tathā ca vākyāt avagata pratibandhaḥ  anuminuyāt  ayam asau gavayaḥ  gaḥ sadṛśa tvāditi deśa vākya avagata piṇḍavat iti na viparyayāt  na hi gaḥ sadṛśam buddhau  āropya anena pṛṣṭaḥ sa kim śabda vācya iti kintu sāmānyatas  gavaya padārtham avagamya sa kīdṛś iti tathā ca yad yoga prāthamyābhyām tasya eva vyāpya tvam tatas  kim tena prakṛta anupayogāt atha kiṃlakṣaṇa kaḥ  asau  iti praśna arthaḥ tadā vyatireki param syāt  lakṣaṇasya tathā abhavāt tathā ca gaḥ sadṛśaḥ  gavaya iti asya arthaḥ yaḥ  gavaya iti na vyavahriyate na asau gaḥ sadṛśa iti evañca prayoktavyam ayam asau gavaya iti vyavahartavyaḥ gaḥ sadṛśa tvāt  yaḥ tu na tathā gaḥ sadṛśaḥ yathā hastī na ca hasti ādīnām vipakṣa tve pramāṇam asti sarva aprayogasya duravadhāra ṇa tvāt  katipaya avi avahārasya ca anaikāntika tvāt  nanu liṅga mātre praśnaḥ  bhaviṣyati kīdṛś  kim liṅgam iti na na hi anena liṅgam avijñāya gavaya śabdasya vācaka tvam kasyacid vācya tvam vā avagatam yena tad artham praśnaḥsyāt pravṛtti nimitta viśeṣa liṅge praśnaḥ yena nimittena gavaya śabdaḥ pravartate tasya kim liṅgam iti ced na na hi tad avaśyam anumeyam eva iti anena niścitam yata idam syāt  jñāna upāya mātra praśne tad viśeṣeṇa uttaram iti ced na aviśeṣāt indriya sannikarṣam api uttarayet  paryāya antaram vā yathā gavayam aham katham jānīyām iti praśne vanam gataḥ  drakṣyasi iti yathā vā kaḥ pika iti atra kokila iti tasmāt nimitta bheda praśna eva ayam gavayaḥ  gavaya pada vācyaḥ kīdṛś  kena nimittena iti yuktam utpaśyāmaḥ tasya ca nimitta viśeṣasya sākṣāt upadarśayitum aśkya tvāt  pṛṣṭaḥ tad u lakṣaṇam kiñcid ācaṣṭe tad ca upamāna sāmagrī samutthāpanam eva tasya ca pramāṇasya sataḥ tarkaḥ sahāya tām āpadyate  sādṛśyasya eva nimitta tāyām kalpanā gauravam nimitta antara kalpane ca kḷpta kalpya virodha  iti tad eva nimittam avagacchati iti lakṣaṇantu asya anavagata saṅgati sañjñāsam abhivyāhṛta vākya arthasya sañjñinī anusandhānam upamānam vākya arthaḥ ca kvacid  sādharmyam kvacid vaidharmyam atas  na avyāpakam tasmāt niyata viṣaya tvāt eva na tena bādhaḥ na tu anatiḥ ekāt iti sthitiḥ ku    atra ucyate anekāntaḥ paricchede sambhave ca na niścayaḥ ākāṅkṣā sat tayā hetuḥ yogyā sattira bandhanā et e padārtha āmithaḥsarṅgavanta iti saṃsṛṣṭā eva iti niyamaḥ  vā sādhyaḥ sambhāvita saṃsargā iti vā na prathamaḥ anāpta ukta pada kadamba smāritaiḥ aneka antāt āpta uktyā viśeṣaṇīyam iti ced na vākya artha pratīteḥ prāk  tad asiddheḥ na hi avipralambhakatva mātram iha āpta śabdena vivakṣitam tad ukteḥ api padārtha saṃsarga vyabhicārāt api tu tad anubhava prāmāṇyam api na ca etad śakyam asarvajñe sarvadā sarva viṣaye satya jñānavān ayam iti niścetum bhrānteḥ puruṣa dharma tvāt  yatra kvacid āpta tvam anāptasya api asti iti na tena upayogaḥ tatas  asmin  arthe ayam abhra anta iti kenacid upāyena grāhyam na ca etad  saṃsarga viśeṣam apratītya śakyam buddheḥ arthaṃbhedam antareṇa nirūpayitum aśakyatvāt  padārtha mātre ca abhrāntatva siddhau na kiñcid  anāpta sādhāraṇyāt  eteṣām saṃsarge ayam abhra anta iti śakyam iti ced na eteṣām saṃsarge iti asyā eva buddheḥ asiddheḥ ananubhūta care smaraṇa ayogāt tad anubhavasya liṅga adhīna tayā tasya ca viśeṣaṇa asiddha tvena anupapatteḥ iti evam dvitīye api prayoge hetuḥ ākāṅkṣa ādimattve sati iti tatra kā iyam ākāṅkṣā nāma na tāvat viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāvaḥ tasya saṃsargar gaviśeṣa svabhāvatayā sādhya tvāt  na api tad yogya tā yogya tayā eva gata artha tvāt na api avinābhāvaḥ nīlam sarojam iti ādau tad abhāve api vākya artha pratyayāt tatra api viśeṣa ākṣipta sāmānyayoḥ avinā abhāvaḥ  asti iti vā upi ākāṅkṣa iti ced na ahaḥ vimalam jalam nadyāḥ kacche mahiṣaḥ carati ityādau vākya bheda anupapatti prasaṅgāt  na api pratipattuḥ jijñāsā paṭaḥ bhavati ityādau śukla ādi jijñāsāyām sayā raktaḥ paṭaḥ bhavati iti asya eka deśavat sarvadā vākya aparyavasāna prasaṅgāt   guṇa kriyā ādi aśeṣa viśeṣa jijñāsāyām api padasmārita viśeṣa jijñāsā ākāṅkṣā paṭa iti ukte kiṃrūpaḥ kutra kim karoti iti ādi rūpa jijñāsā tatra bhavati iti ukte kim karoti iti eṣa eva padasmārita viṣayā na tu kim rūpa ityādiḥ api yadā tu rakta iti ucyate tadā kiṃrūpa iti eṣā api smārita viṣayā syāt evambhūtaḥ  api ayam aikāntikaḥ  hetuḥ yadā hi ayam eti putraḥ  rājñaḥ puruṣaḥ  apasāryatām iti vaktā uccārayati śrotā ca vyāsaṅga ādinā nimittena ayam eti putra iti aśru tvā eva rājñaḥ puruṣaḥ ced  evam tarhi saṃsargaḥ  na siddhyet  āpta vākyeṣu setsyati iti ced na sarva viṣayā aptatvasya asiddheḥ yatra kvacid āpta tvasya anaikāntika tvāt  prakṛta viṣaye ca āptatva siddhau saṃsarga pramāṇa antara asaṅkīrṇa udāharaṇa abhāvāt ca padānām tu pūrva bhāva niyamena padārtha smaraṇa avāntara vyāpāravat tayā tad upapatteḥ vyāpārasya avyavadhāyaka tvāt iti kṛtam prasakta anuprasaktyā astu tarhi śabda eva bādhakam sarvajñe kartari tathā hi prakṛteḥ kriyamāṇāni guṇaiḥ karmāṇi sarvaśas  ahaṅkāra vimūḍha ātmā kartāham iti manyate g ī  ityādi paṭhanti asya ayam arthaḥ na pāramārthikam cetanasya kartṛ tvam asti ābhimānikam tu tad  na ca sarvajñasya abhimānaḥ na ca asarvajñasya jagatkartṛ tvam asti ucyate na pramāṇam anāpta uktiḥ na adṛṣṭe kvacid āpta tā adṛśya dṛṣṭau sarvajñaḥ  na ca nitya āgamaḥ kṣamaḥ yadi hi sarvajña kartṛ bhāvā avedakaḥ śabdaḥ  na āpta uktaḥ na tarhi pramāṇam atha āptaḥ  asya vaktā katham na tad artha darśī atīndriya artha darśī iti ced  katham asarva jñaḥ katham vā na kartā āgamasya eva praṇayanāt  na ca nitya āgama sambhavaḥ vicchedāt itya āveditam apica na ca asau kvacid ekāntaḥ sattvasya api pravedanāt  nirañjana avabodha arthaḥ  na ca san  api tad paraḥ na hi asattva pakṣa eva āgamaḥ  niyataḥ īśvara sadbhāvasya eva bhūyaḥsu pradeśeṣu pratipādanāt  tathā ca agre darśayiṣyāmaḥ tathā ca sati kvacid asattva pratipādanam anekāntam na bādhakam sattva pratipādanam api tarhi na sādhanam iti ced  āpātatas tāvat evam etad  yadā tu niḥśeṣa viśeṣa guṇa śūnya ātma svarūpa pratipādana artha tvam akartṛkatva āgamānām avadhārayiṣyate tadā na tad niṣedhe tātparyam am īṣām iti sattva pratipādakānām eva āgamānām prāmāṇyam bhaviṣyati iti na ca teṣām api anyatra tātparyam iti vakṣyāmaḥ astu arthāpattiḥ tarhi bādhikā tathā hi yadi abhaviṣyat na upādekṣyat na hi asau  anupadiśya pravartayitum na jānāti ata upadeśa eva anyathā anupapadyamānaḥ tathāvidhasya abhāvam audāsīnyam vā avedayati na anyathā eva upapatteḥ hetu abhāve phala abhāvāt pramāṇe asati na pramā tad abhāvāt pravṛttiḥ na u karma vāde api ayam vidhiḥ buddhi pūrvām hi pravṛttiḥ na buddhim anutpādya śakya sampādanā na ca prakṛte buddhiḥ api upadeśam antareṇa śakya siddhiḥ tasya eva tad kāraṇa tvāt bhūta āveśa nyāyena pravartayet iti ced  pravartayet eva yadi tathā phala siddhiḥ syāt  na tu evam kuta etad avasitam upadeśānyatha anupapattyā eva yasya api mate adṛṣṭa vaśāt eva bhūtānām pravṛttiḥ tasya api tulyam etad  yadi asti pravṛtti nimittam adṛṣṭam kim upadeśena tatas  eva pravṛtti siddheḥ na ced  tathā api kim upadeśena tad abhāve tasmin sati api apravṛtteḥ nityaḥ svatantra upadeśaḥ  na paryanuyojya iti ced  yūyam paryanuyojyāḥ ye tama mana vadhānataḥ  dhārayanti vicārayanti ca iti na ca arthāpattiḥ anumānataḥ  bhidyate loke tad asaṅkīrṇa udāharaṇa abhāvāt prakāra antara abhāvāt ca tathā hi aniyamyasya na ayuktiḥ na aniyantā upapādakaḥ na mānayoḥ virodhaḥ  asti prasiddhe vā api asau samaḥ jīvan  caitraḥ  gṛhe na asti iti anupapadyamānam asati bahis sadbhāve tam āpa māve dayati iti udaharanti tatra cintyate kim anupapannam jīvataḥ  gṛha abhāvasya iti na hi aniyama yasya aniyāmakam vinā kiñcid anupapannam atiprasaṅgāt  nanu svarūpam eva tad  na tāvat bahis  sattvena kartavyam tad akārya tvāt tasya sthitiḥ eva asya tena vinā na syāt iti asya svabhāva iti ced  evam tarhi tad niyata svabhāva eva asau vyāpteḥ eva vyatireka mukha nirūpyāyāḥ tathā avyapadeśāt katham vā ca bahis sattvam asya upapādakam na hi aniyāmakaḥ  bhavan  api aniyamyam upapādayati atiprasaṅgāt eva svabhāvaḥ  asya yad anena bahis sattvena geha asa tvam kroḍīkṛtya sthātavyam iti ced  sā iyam vyāptiḥ eva anvaya mukha nirūpyā tathā vyapadiśyate iti na vayam avinā abhāvam artha āpattau  apajānīmahe kintu tad jñānam na ca asau sattā mātreṇa tad anumāna tvam āpādayati iti ced  na anupapatti pratisandhānasya avaśya abhyupagantavya tvāt anyathā ātu ati prasaṅgāt  arthāpatti ābhāsān avakāśāt ca yadā hi anyathā eva u thāpyu papannam anyathā anupapannam iti manyate tadā asya viparyayaḥ na tu anyathā iti tathā api katham atra vyāptiḥ gṛhyeta iti ced  yadā aham iha tadā na anyatra yadā anyatra tadā na iha iti sarva pratyakṣā siddham etad  kā tatra api kathantā sarva deśa apratyakṣa tve tatra abhāvaḥ  duravadhāraṇa iti api na asti teṣām eva saṃsargasya ātmani pratiṣedhāt  ayogyānām pratiṣedhe kā vārtā iti ced  tad avayavānām tad saṃsarga pratiṣedhāt eva anumānāt anyeṣām na kācid  na hi akāraṇībhūtena paramāṇunā na idam saṃsṛṣṭam iti niścetum śakyam iti na ca na api vinā abhāva niścayena api gamayan  apakṣa dharmor atha āpattiḥ iti yuktam pakṣa dharma tāyā animittatva prasaṅgāt  aviśeṣāt  vyadhikaraṇena āvinābhāva niścaya ayogāt ca yad  yatra yadā iti prakāra anupapatteḥ pramāṇayoḥ virodhe arthāpattiḥ avirodha upapādikā na tu evam anumānam iti api na asti virodhe hi rajju sarpa ādivat ekasya bādha eva syāt  na tu ubhayoḥ pramāṇyam prāmāṇye vā na virodhaḥ sthūlam idam ekam itivat  saha sambhavāt  caitraḥ  ayam ayam tu maitra itivat vā viṣaya bhedāt  prakṛte kvāpi asti iti sāmānyatas  gehasya api praveśāt eka viṣaya tā api asti iti ced  yadi evam kvacid asti kvacid na asti itivat na virodhaḥ atra api virodha eva iti ced  ekam tarhi bhajyeta na bhajyeta arthāpattyā ubhayoḥ api upapādanāt iti ced  kim anupapadyamānam virodha eva anyathā anupapadyamānaḥ  vibhinna viṣaya tayā vyavasthāpayati iti ced  atha abhinna viṣaya tayā eva kim na vyavasthāpayet  vyavasthāpanam avirodha āpādanam eka viṣaya tayā eva ca anayoḥ virodhaḥ sa katham tayā eva śamayitavyaḥ na hi yaḥ  yad viṣa mūrcchitaḥ sa tena eva utthāpyate iti ced  eka viṣaya tayā anayoḥ virodha iti etad eva kutas  vibhinna deśa svabhāva tayā eva sarvatra upalambhāt iti ced  nanu iyam vyāptiḥ eva tathā ca ghaṭṭa kuṭyām prabhātam iti dhūma upi vā anupapadyamāna tayā eva vahnim gamayet  na hi tena vinā asau  upapadyate virodhaḥ  api dhūmāt vahninā bhavitavyam anupalabdheḥ ca na bhavitavyam iti tathā ca anu palabdheḥ arvāc bhāga vyavasthāpanam dhūmasya ca vyavadhānena anupalabhya vahni viṣayatva sthitiḥ arthāpattiḥ iti kutaḥ anumānam vahnim ān ayam iti am anumānam vyāpteḥ anyathā anumāna abhāve virodha asiddheḥ arvāc bhāga anupalabdhi virodhena para bhāge asya vahniḥ iti asya artha āpattiḥ eva iti ced  na vyāpti grāhakeṇa pramāṇena virodhasya ukta tvāt na api uttarā arthāpattiḥ anyathā pāṇḍara tvasya apālālatva virodhena pālālatva sthitiḥ api artha āpattiḥ eva syāt  tad viśiṣṭasya tena eva vyāpteḥ na evam iti ced  yadi evam arvāc bhāga anupalabhyamāna vanhi tvena matvena viśiṣṭasya dhūmasya tena eva vyāpteḥ katham evam bhaviṣyati iti tulyam kevala vyatirekya anumānam para abhimatam arthāpattiḥ anvaya abhāvāt iti ced  evam etāvatā viśeṣeṇa anumāner athāpatti vyavahāram na vārayāmaḥ tatra anumāna vyavahāraḥ kuta iti ced  avinābhūta liṅga samutpanna muttha tvāt  sādhya dharmeṇa vinā hi abhavanam anvayina iva vyatirekiṇaḥ  api aviśiṣṭam tad niścayaḥ ca anvaya vyatirekābhyām anyatareṇa vā iti tasmāt arthāpattiḥ iti anumānasya paryāyaḥ  ayam tad viśeṣa vacanam vā pūrvavat ādivat iti yuktam anupalabdhiḥ tu na bādhikā iti cintitam na ca pratyakṣa ādeḥ atiricyate tad ucyate pratipatteḥ apārokṣyāt indriyasya anupakṣayāt ajñāta karaṇa tvāt ca bhāva āveśāt ca cetasaḥ yā hi sākṣātkāriṇī pratītiḥ sā indriya karaṇikā yathā rūpa ādi pratītiḥ tathā iha bhū tale ghaṭaḥ  na asti iti api sākṣātkāri tvam asya asiddham iti ced na eka jātīya tve jñāta ajñāta karaṇatva anupapatteḥ na hi tasmin  eva kārye tad eva karaṇam ekadā jñātam ajñā tañca ekadā upayujyate liṅga indriyayoḥ api vyatyaya prasaṅgāt  jñānasya akāraṇatva prasaṅgāt ca na hi tad atipatyā api bhavataḥ tad kāraṇa tvam vyāghātāt  tasmāt  jñāta anupalabdhi janyasya sākṣātkāri tvāt  tad viparīta kāraṇakam idam tad viparīta jātīyam iti nyāyyām nanu kva nāma jñāta anupalabdhiḥ asākṣāt kāriṇīm abhāva pratītim janayati tad yathā nipuṇataram anusṛtaḥ  mayā mandire caitraḥ na ca upalabdha iti śrutyā śrotā anum inoti nūnam na āsīt eva iti etena prāk nāstitā api vyākhyātā nanu tathā api avāntara jāti bhedaḥ  astu ajñāta anupalabdhi janye sākṣātkāraḥ tu kuta iti ced  kāraṇa virodhāt  kārya virodhena bhavitavyam iti uktam eva ananyatra upakṣīṇa indriya vyāpāra anantara bhāvi tvāt ca adhikaraṇa grahaṇe tad upakṣīṇam iti ced na andhasya api tvac indriya upanīte ghaṭa ādau rūpa viśeṣa abhāva pratīti prasaṅgāt  asti hi tasya adhikaraṇa grahaṇam asti ca pratiyogi smaraṇam asti ca śyāmeraktatvasya yogyasya abhāvaḥ  anupalabdhiḥ ca adhikaraṇa grāhaka indriya grāhya abhāva vādinaḥ  api samānam etad iti ced na pratiyogi grāhaka indriya grāhyaḥ  abhāva iti abhyupagamāt  mama api pratiyogi grāhaka indriya gṛhīte adhikaraṇe anupalabdhiḥ pramāṇam iti abhyupagama iti ced na vāyau tvac indriya upanīte rūpa abhāva prati iti anudaya prasaṅgāt  tathā api tad tatra sannikṛṣṭam iti ced  hanta evam ananyatra carita artham indriyam avaśyam apekṣaṇīyam rūpa abhāva anubhavena syāt etad  tathā api vastu antara graha eva tasya upayoga iti ced na tasya tam pratyakāraṇa tvāt  kāraṇa tve vā mahā andhakāre kara parāmarśena sparśavat dravya abhāvam na pratīyāt  pratīyāt ca puras visphārita akṣaḥ pṛṣṭha lagnasya aśyāma tvam ārjava avasthānam api adhikaraṇasya upayujyate iti ced  tarhi nayana sannikarṣaḥ  api upayokṣyate tad eka sahakāri prabhā sannikarṣa apekṣaṇāt  vātāyana vivara visāri kara parāmṛṣṭe api adhikaraṇe tad upalambha prasaṅgāt ca tathā api yogya tā āpādana upakṣīṇañcakṣuḥ tad itara sāmagrī sākalye hi anupalabhyamānasya abhāvaḥ  niścīyate tad ca cakṣuṣi adhiḥ akaraṇa sannikṛṣṭe sati syāt iti ced  nanu paripūrṇāni kāraṇāni eva sākalyam tathā ca kim kutra upakṣīṇam atha anyonya melanam mithas  pratyāsatti ādi śabda vācyam tad upakṣaya viṣayaḥ na tarhi kvacid cakṣuḥ kāraṇam syāt iti na hi rūpa ādi upalabdhim api asannikṛṣṭam etad upajanayati atha adhikaraṇa samaveta kiñcit upalambhaḥ  api tad viṣaya abhāva grahe anupalabdheḥ apekṣaṇīyaḥ tatas tatra idam caritārtham vāyu ādiṣu tu rūpa ādi abhāva pratītiḥ ānumānikī tathā nupalabdhyā hi anumīyate ayam nīrūpaḥ  vāyuḥ iti na asiddheḥ na hi upalambha abhāvaḥ  bhavatām abhāva upalambhaḥ upalambhasya atīndriyatva abhyupagamāt prākaṭya abhāvena anumeya iti ced na vāyau rūpa vattā prākaṭya abhāvasya api asiddheḥ rūpa abhāvena samāna tvāt  vyavahāra abhāvena anumeya iti ced na kāya vāc vyāpāra abhāve api upekṣā jñāna bhāva abhyupagamāt mūka svapna upapatteḥ ca na ca vyavahāra abhāva mātreṇa anumātum api śakyate anaikāntika tvāt asiddheḥ ca tad viṣayaḥ tu vyavahāraḥ tad viṣaya jñāna janyaḥ  vā tad viṣaya jñāna jana kaḥ  vā tad āśraya dharma jana kaḥ  vā tad abhāvaḥ ca tad jñāna tad āśraya dharma abhāva antar bhūta  eva iti aśakya niścaya eva ātma āśraya ita retara āśraya cakraka pravṛtti prasaṅgāt  na ca ajñātasya upalambha ādi abhāvasya liṅga tā na ca prākaṭya abhāvaḥ sattā mātreṇa upalambha abhāvam āvedayati iti yuktam liṅga abhāvasya tathā tve ati prasaṅgāt  avinā abhāva balena tu niyame tad pratisandhānāpatteḥ na hi avinābhāvaḥ sattā mātreṇa jñāna hetum niyamayati dhūma ādau  api tathā abhāva prasaṅgāt iti jñāna pratyakṣa tvena tvad diśā bhaviṣyati iti ced na śabda dhvaṃsā ādinā ukta uttara tvāt apica pratiyogi grāhaka indriyeṇa adhikaraṇa dharma pratītiḥ anupalabdheḥ aṅgam iti tad rahitāyāḥ tasyāḥ kārya vyabhicārāt vyavasthāpyeta vyāpti balāt vā na tāvat ukta rūpa anupalabdhiḥ tām vinā abhāva pratyayam ajanayantī dṛśyate na api vyāpteḥ tathā sati vayau rūpa abhāva pratyayaḥ tām ākṣipet  evam bhūta tvāt anākṣepe vā na tad kāraṇa kaḥ  bhavet  na vā bhavet  tatas  na bhavati eva liṅgāt tad utpatti riti ced  nanu liṅgam api sā eva na tattva antaram yathā yoni sambandhaḥ aliṅga daśāyām indriya sannikarṣam apekṣate liṅgadaśāyām tu tad anapekṣa eva brāhmaṇya jñāne tathā etad  syāt iti ced na kārya jāti bhedāt tad upapatteḥ prakṛte ca tad anabhyupagamāt  pārokṣya apārokṣye vihāyāni athā api asau bhaviṣyati iti ced na anupalambhāt  sambhāvyate tāvat iti ced  sambhāvyatām na tu etāvatā api tam āśritya karaṇa niyama niścayaḥ ajñāta karaṇa tvāt ca yad ajñāyamāna karaṇa jam jñānam tad sākṣāt indriya jam yathā rūpa pratyakṣam tathā āca iha bhū tale ghaṭaḥ  na asti iti jñānam iti yathā vā smaraṇam ajñāyamāna karaṇa jam sākṣāt manaḥ janma kutas tarhi na sākṣāt kārī anubhava rūpam saṃskāra atirikta sannikarṣa abhāvāt iti vakṣyāmaḥ tathā api bhāva viṣaye iyam vyavasthā abhāva jñānam tu ajñāta karaṇa tve api na sākṣāt indriya jam bhaviṣyati iti ced na utsargasya bādhaka abhāvena saṅkoca anupapatteḥ anyathā sarva vyāptīnām bhāva mātra viṣayatva prasaṅgaḥ aviśeṣāt  tathā api vipakṣe kim bādhakam iti ced  nanu idam eva tāvat  anyat api ucyamānam ākarṇaya tad yathā akāraṇaka kārya prasaṅgaḥ rūpa ādi upalabdhīnām api vān indriya karaṇatva prasaṅgaḥ na hi anumiti ādibhiḥ upalabhyamāna karaṇikābhiḥ cakṣuḥ ādi vyavasthāpanam apitu anupalabhyamāna karaṇikābhī rūpa ādi upalabdhibhiḥ eva yadi api sākṣātkāritā api tatra eva paryavasyati tathā api prathamatas  anupalabhyamāna karaṇa tvam eva prayojakam cakṣuḥ ādi kalpane na hi upalabhyamāne karaṇa antare sākṣāt kāriṇīṣu api tāsu cakṣuḥ ādi anupalabhyamānam kaścid akalpayiṣyat ata eva asākṣātkāri tve api smṛteḥ mana eva karaṇam upāgaman dhīrāḥ saṃskāraḥ tu artha viśeṣa pratti āsattau  upayujyate indriyāṇām prāpya kāritva vyavasthāpanāt  bhāva āveśāt ca cetasaḥ sarvatra hi bāhya artha anubhave janayitavye bhāva bhūta pramāṇa āviṣṭam eva ceta upayujyate na atas  anyathā iti vyāptiḥ tathā eva śakteḥ avadhāraṇāt  na hi anupalabdhi mātra sahāyam tad  abhāve api anubhavam ādhātum utsahate śabda liṅga ādeḥ apekṣā darśanāt na ca yatra yad apekṣam yasya janaka tvam upalabdham tad eva tasya eva tad anapekṣam janakam iti nyāya saham ārda indhana sambandham antareṇa api dahanāt dhūma sambhāvana āpatteḥ tathā ca gatam kārya kāraṇa bhāva parigraha vyasanena api ca pratiyogini sāmarthyāt  vyāpāra avi avadhānataḥ akṣa āśraya tvāt doṣāṇām indriyāṇi vikalpanāt  yad hi pramāṇam yad bhāva avagāhi tad  tad abhāva gāhi yathā liṅgam śabdaḥ  vā ghaṭa ādi avagāhi ca indriyam iti anyathā hi śabda ādikam api na abhāvam āvedayet  bhāva eva sāmarthya avadhāraṇāt na ca evam eva nyāyyam devadattaḥ  gehe na asti iti śabdāt  mayā tatra jijñāsamānena api na dṛṣṭaḥ  maitra iti avagata anupalabdhyā anumānāt api avagateḥ grāhayatu vā aśrayam indriyam tathā api na tena idam vyavadhīyate vyāpāra tvāt  anyathā sarva sa vikalpakānām pratyakṣa tvāya dattaḥ  jala añcaliḥ syāt  nanu evam sati dhūma upalambhaḥ  api asya vyāpāraḥ syāt  tathā ca gatam anumānena api iti ced na yayā kriyayā vinā yasya yad kāraṇa tvam na nirvahati tam prati tasyāḥ  eva vyāpāra tvāt  na ca dhūma ādi upalabdhim antareṇa cakṣuṣaḥ  vanhi jñāna kāraṇa tvam na nirvahati saṃyogavat iti asti ca bhāva abhāva viparyayaḥ saḥ  ayam yasya doṣam anuvidhatte tad eva atra karaṇam iti nyāyyam na ca anupalabdhiḥ svabhāvataḥ  duṣṭā na api adhikaraṇa grahaṇam pratiyogi smaraṇam vā svabhāvataḥ  duṣṭam anupad patti daśāyām anutpatteḥ utpatti daśāyāñca sva artha prakāśana svabhāva tāyāḥ  aparāvṛtteḥ asaṃsṛṣṭayoḥ adhikaram apratiyoginoḥ saṃsṛṣṭa tayā pratimānam duṣṭam saṃsṛṣṭayoḥ ca asaṃsṛṣṭa tayā iti ced  nanu ayam eva viparyayaḥ tathā ācā atma āśrayaḥ  doṣaḥ tasmāt duṣṭa indriyasya tad viparyaya sāmarthye aduṣṭasya tad samīcīna jñāna sāmarthyam api tathā ca prayogaḥ indriyam abhāva pramākaraṇam tad viparyaya karaṇa tvāt yad  yad viparyaya karaṇam tad  tad pramākaraṇam yathā rūpa pramākaraṇam cakṣuḥ iti vikalpanāt khalu api aghaṭam bhū talam iti hi viśiṣṭa dhīra vaśyam indriya karaṇikā svīkartavyā pramāṇa antaram vā saptamam āstheyam yathā hi viśeṣya mātra upakṣīṇam indriyam akaraṇam atra tathā viśeṣaṇa mātra upakṣīṇa anupalabdhiḥ api na karaṇam syāt  sva sva viṣaya mātra pravṛttayoḥ pramāṇayoḥ samāhāraḥ kāraṇam iti ced na viṣaya bhede phala vaijātye ca tad anupapatteḥ na hi mṛtsu tantuṣu ca vyāpriyamāṇayoḥ kulāla kuvindayoḥ samāhāraḥ syāt  na api ghaṭa paṭa ādi kāriṇām cakravema ādīnām samāhāraḥ kvacid upayujyate tatra karbura kārya abhāvāt na tathā prakṛte tu viśiṣṭa pratyayasya parokṣa aparokṣa rūpasya darśanāt tathā iti ced na viruddha jāti samāveśa abhāvāt bhāve vā karambita karbura eva kārye dvayoḥ api śaktiḥ abhyupagantavyā darśana balāt  na hi niyata viṣayeṇa sāmarthyena karbura kārya siddhiḥ anyatra api tathā prasaṅgāt  nanu ubhayoḥ api ubhayatra sāmarthye kor athaḥ mithas sannidhānena iti ced na tad sahitasya eva tasya tatra sāmarthyāt iti etena surabhi candanam ityādayaḥ  vyākhyātāḥ tathā ca abhāva viṣaye api indriya sāmarthyasya durapahnava tvāt alam asat graheṇa iti syāt etad  na agṛhīte viśeṣaṇe viśaṣṭa buddhiḥ udā iti tad kāryatvāt na ca viśiṣṭa sāmarthye kevala viśeṣaṇe api sāmarthyam kevala saurabhe api cakṣuṣaḥ  vṛtti prasaṅgāt  atas  abhāva viśeṣaṇa grahaṇāya māna antara sambhavaḥ api ca katham anālocitor atha indriyeṇa vikalpyeta na ca māna antarasya api eṣā rītiḥ anumāna ādibhiḥ anāla ucitasya api arthasya vikalpanāt  aprāpteḥ ca na hi abhāvena indriyasya saṃyoga ādiḥ sambhavati na ca viśeṣaṇa tvam sambandha antara pūrvaka tvāt tasya avaśya abhyupagantavya tvāt ca anupalabdheḥ na hi tad upalabdhau tasya abhāva upalambha iti ced  ucyate avaccheda graha dhrauvyāt adhrauvye siddha sādhanāt  prāpti antare anavasthāna atra ced anyaḥ  api durghaṭaḥ sa hi artha viśeṣaṇī bhaviṣyan kevalaḥ  api visphuret  yasya avacchedaka jñānam na vyañjakam sa ca vā vikalpayitavya ālocyate yaḥ  viśeṣaṇa jñāna nirapekṣeṇa indriyeṇa vijñāpyate yaḥ tu tad puraḥsara eva prakāśate tatra tasya vikalpa sāmagrī samavadhānavata eva sāmarthyāt na ayam vidhiḥ svabhāva prāptau satyām api adhikā prāptiḥ pratipatti balena rūpa ādau  abhyupagatā iha tu anavasthāt ustha tayā na tad abhyupagamaḥ na tu svabhāva pratyāsattiḥ etāvatā eva viphalāyate na ced evam pramāṇa antare api sarvam etad durghaṭam syāt  tathā hi sarvam eva mānam sākṣāt paramparayā vā nirvikalpaka viśrāntam na hi anumāna ādikam api anālocana pūrvakam tatas  anāla ucitaḥ  abhāvaḥ katham anupalabdhyā api vikalpyeta na ca tayā tad ālocanam eva janyate pratiyogi anavacchinnasya tasya nirūpayitum aśakyatvāt  śakya tve vā kim aparāddham indriyeṇa tathā sambandha antara garbhatva niyamena viśeṣaṇa tvasya māna antare api kaḥ pratīkāraḥ tad abhāvasya tadānīm apisamāna tvāt  parasya tādātmyam asti iti ced  nanu yadi asau  asti asti eva na ced  na eva na hi abhyupagamena arthāḥ kriyante anabhyupagamena vā nivartante iti avaśya abhyupagantavya tve kāraṇa tvam siddhayet  na tu māna antara tvam anyathā bhāva upalambhe api abhāva anupalabdhiḥ eva pramāṇam syāt  na indriyam abhāva upalambhe bhāva anupalambhavat bhāva upalambhe abhāvānupalambhasya api vajra lepāya māna tvāt iti pratyakṣa ādibhiḥ ebhiḥ evam adharaḥ  dūre virodha udayaḥ prāyaḥ yad mukha vīkṣaṇa eka vidhuraiḥ ātmā api na āsādyate tam sarva anuvidheyam ekam asama svacchanda līla utsavam devānām api devam udbhavat ati śraddhāḥ prapadyāmahe nanu sat api īśvara jñānam na pramāṇam tad lakṣaṇā yogāt anadhigata artha gantuḥ tathā abhāvāt anyathā smṛteḥ api prāmāṇya prasaṅgāt  na ca nityasya sarva viṣasya cān adhigata artha tā vyāghātāt  atra ucyate avyāpteḥ adhika vyāpteḥ alakṣaṇam apūrva dṛś  yathārtha anubhavaḥ mānam anapekṣatayā iṣyate na hi adhigater athe adhigatiḥ eva na utpadyate kāraṇānām apratibandhāt  na ca utpadyamānā api pramātuḥ anapekṣitā iti na pramā prāmāṇyasya ātad adhīna tvāt na api pūrva aviśiṣṭa tā mātreṇa aprāmāṇyam uttara aviśiṣṭa tayā pūrvasya api aprāmāṇya prasaṅgāt  tad anapekṣa tvena tu tasya pramāṇye tad uttarasya api tathā eva syāt  aviśeṣāt  chinne kuṭhāra ādīnām iva paricchinne nayana ādīnām sādhakatama tvam eva na asti iti api na asti phala utpāda anutpādābhyām viśeṣāt  tad  phalam pramā eva na bhavati gṛhīta mātra gocara tvāt smṛtivat iti ced na yathārtha anubhava tu niṣedhe sādhye bādhita tvāt  anadhigata arthatva niṣedhe siddha sādhanāt  sādhya sama tvāt ca vyavahāra niṣedhe tad nimitta viraha upādhika tvāt  bādhita tvāt ca nacān adhigata artha tvam eva tad nimittam viparyayepi pramāvī avahāra prasaṅgāt  na api yathārthatva viśiṣṭam etad eva dhārāvahana buddhi avyāpteḥ na ca tad tad kāla kalā viśiṣṭa tayā tatra api anadhigata arthar thagantṛ tvam upapādanīyam kṣaṇa upādhīnām anākalanāt naca ajñāteṣu api viśeṣaṇeṣu tad janita viśiṣṭa tā prakāśata iti kalpanīyam sva rūpeṇa tad janane anāgata ādi viśiṣṭa tā anubhava virodhāt tad jñānena tu tad janane sūrya gati ādīnām ajñāne tad viśiṣṭa tā anutpādāt  na ca etasyām pramāṇam asti nanu anupakārya anupakārakayoḥ viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāve katham atiprasaṅgaḥ  vāraṇīyaḥ vyavacchitti pratyāyanena vyavacchittau svabhāvena anyathā tatra vā vyanavasthānāt iti jñāta tā eva upādhiḥ iti ced na nirākariṣyamāṇa tvāt  tad sadbhāvepi vā smṛteḥ api tathā eva prāmāṇya prasaṅgāt  janaka agocara tvepi uttarottarasmṛtau pūrva pūrva smaraṇa janita jñāta tāvabhāsanāt astu vā pratyakṣe yathā tathā gṛhīta vismṛta artha śrutau kā vārtā apramā eva asau  iti ced  gatam idānīm veda prāmāṇya pratyāśayā na hi anādau saṃsāre  svarga kāmaḥ  yajete ati vākya arthaḥ kenacid na avagataḥ sandehe api prāmāṇya sandehāt na ca tatra api kāla kalā viśeṣāḥ parisphuranti na ca eka janma avaccheda paribhāṣayet am lakṣaṇam tatra api anubhūta vismṛta veda artham pratyaprāmāṇya prasaṅgāt  katham tarhi smṛteḥ vyavacchedaḥ ananubhava tvena eva yathā arthohi anubhavaḥ pramā iti prāmāṇikāḥ paśya ṭha nti  tatva jñānā aditi sūtraṇāt   avyabhicāri jñāna am iti ca nanu smṛtiḥ pramā eva kim na syāt  yathā artha jñāna tvāt pratyakṣa ādi anubhūtivat iti ced na siddhe vyavahāre nimitta anusaraṇāt  na ca sva icchā kalpitena nimittena loka vyavahāra niyamanam avyavasthayā loka vyavahāra viplava prasaṅgāt  na ca smṛti hetau pramāṇa abhiyuktānām prāmāṇa vyavahāra abhiyuktānām mahā ṛṣīṇām pramāṇa vyavahāraḥ  asti pṛthak anupadeśāt  ukteṣu anantarbhāvāt anupadeśa iti ced na pratyakṣasya asākṣāt kāri phalatva anupapatteḥ liṅga śabda ādeḥ ca sattā mātreṇa pratītya sādhana tvāt iti evam vyavasthite tarkyate api yad  iyam anubhava eka viṣayā satī tad mukha nirīkṣaṇena tad yathārthatva ayatha artha tve anuvidhīyamānā tad prāmāṇyam avya na vasthāpya na yathārtha tayā vyavahartum śakyata iti vyavahāre api pūrva anubhava eva pramitiḥ anapekṣa tvāt  na tu smṛtiḥ nityam tad apekṣaṇāt  asamī cīne hi anubhave smṛtiḥ api tathā eva nanu evam anumānam api apramāṇam āpadyeta mūla pratyakṣa anuvidhānāt na viṣaya bhedāt  āgamaḥ tarhi na pramāṇam tad viṣaya māna antara anuvidhānāt na pramātṛ bhedāt  dhārāvāhika buddhayaḥ tarhi na pramāṇam ādya pramāṇa anuvidhānāt na kāraṇa viśuddhi mātra apekṣayā prathamavat uttarāsām api pūrva mukha nirīkṣaṇa abhāvāt kāraṇa bala āyātam kākatālīyam paurvāparyam iti yadi hi yadi tarhi smṛtiḥ na pramitiḥ pūrva anubhave kim pramāṇam smṛti anyathā anupapattiḥ iti ced na tayā kāraṇa mātra siddheḥ na tu tena anubhavena eva bhavitavyam iti niyāmakam asti ananubhūtepi tarhi smaraṇam syāt iti ced  kim na syāt  na hi atra pramāṇam asti pūrva anaubhava ākāraḥ  bhavaḥ  llekhaḥ smṛteḥ dṛśyate saḥ  anyathā na syāt iti ced  tad  kim bauddhavat  viṣaya ākārāni atha anupapattyā viṣaya siddhiḥ tvayā āpi iṣyate tathābhūtam jñānam eva vā tad siddhiḥ ādye tadvat eva anaikāntika tvam na hi yad ākāram jñānam tad pūrvaka tvam tasya iti niyamaḥ anāgata jñāne vibhrame ca vyabhicārāt  dvitīye ca tu smṛti prāmāṇyam avarjanīyam mā bhūt  pūrva anubhava siddhiḥ kim naḥ chinnam iti ced  na tarhi smṛti anubhavayoḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāva siddhiḥ iti na tad aprāmāṇye api pūrva apara avasthāvat ātma pratyabhijñāna prāmāṇyāt eva tad upapatteḥ yaḥ  aham anvabhavam amum artham saḥ  aham smarāmi iti mānasa pratyakṣam asti iti na ca gṛhīta grāhi tvam īśvara jñānasya tadīya jñāna antara agocara tvāt  viśvasya na ca tad eva jñānam kāla bhedena apramāṇam anapekṣa tvasya aparāvṛtteḥ tathā api vā prāmāṇye atiprasaṅgāt iti syāt etad  anupakārakam viṣayasya tadīyam etadīyam vā na bhavitum arhati aviśeṣāt  na ca tasya iti aniyatam tatra pramāṇam atiprasaṅgāt  na ca tad abhijñāna bhijña mantareṇa tad upakārasya utpattiḥ tathā anabhyupagamāt  abhyupagame vā kāryatvasya anaikāntika tvāt  atra ucyate svabhāva niyama abhāvāt upakāraḥ  api durghaṭaḥ su ghaṭa tve api sati arthe asati kā gatiḥ anyathā viśeṣa abhāvāt tatra eva phalam na anyatra iti asya api niyamasya anupapatteḥ svabhāva niyamena ca upapattau tathā eva viṣaya vyavasthā upapatteḥ avaśyañca etad anuma bhyupaga ntavyam atīta ādi viṣaya tvā yā nurodhāt  na hi tatra jñānena kiñcid  kriyate iti śakyam avagantum asatvāt  na ca tad dharma sāmāni ādhāram kiñcid  kriyate iti yuktam tena tasya eva viṣayatva prāpteḥ tādātmyāt viśeṣasya api sā eva jñāta tā iti ced  tad  kim cakṣuṣā ghaṭe jñāyamāne rasaḥ  api jñāyate tādātmyāt  ghaṭa ākāreṇa jñāyata eva asau rasaḥ iti ced  atha rasa ākāreṇa kim na jñāyate tena rūpeṇa jñāta tānādhāra tvāt iti ced  na tarhi vartamāna sāmānya jñāne api atīta anāgata ādi jñānam tena ākāreṇa prākaṭya ana ādhāra tvāt iti nanu kriyayā karmaṇi kiñcid  karttavyam iti vyāpteraḥ tu anumānam na anaikāntyā anekāntāt asiddheḥ vā na ca liṅgam iha kriyā tad vaiśiṣṭya prakāśa tvāt na adhyakṣa anubhavaḥ  adhike dhātu artha mātra abhiprāyeṇ  prayoge saṃyoga ādibhiḥ aneka antāt na hi śara saṃyogena gagane kiñcid  kriyate antya śabda abhivyaktyā vā śabde spanda abhiprāyeṇa asiddheḥ vyāpāra abhiprāyeṇa śabda liṅga indriya vyāpāraiḥ vyabhicārāt  na hi taiḥ prameye kiñcid  kriyate api tu pramātari eva phala abhiprāyeṇa api tathā antatas tena eva anekāntāt anavasthānāt ca āśu vināśi dharma abhiprāyeṇa dvitva ādibhiḥ aniyamāt  āśu kāraka abhiprāyeṇa karmaṇi asiddheḥ karmaṇi āśu kārakam jñānam iti eva hi sādhyam kartari āśu kāraka tvasya karma upakāraka tvena avyāpteḥ śabda ādi vyāpāraiḥ eva anekāntāt syāt etad  anubhava siddham eva prākaṭyam tathā hi jñātaḥ  ayam artha iti sāmānyatas  sākṣātkṛtaḥ  ayam artha iti viśeṣataḥ  viṣaya viśeṣaṇam eva kiñcid  parisphurati iti ced  tad asat  yathā hi   arthena eva viśeṣaḥ  hi nirākāra tayā adhiyām  tathā kriyayā eva viśeṣaḥ  hi vyavahāreṣu karmaṇām kim na paśyasi ghaṭa kriyā paṭa kriyā itivat  kṛtaḥ  ghaṭaḥ kariṣyate ghaṭa ityādi tathā eva gṛhāṇa ghaṭa jñānam paṭa jñānam itivat  jñātaḥ  ghaṭaḥ  jñāsyate jñāyate iti katham asambaddhayoḥ dharma dharmi bhāva iti ced  dhvastaḥ  ghaṭa iti yathā etad api katham iti ced  nūnam dhvaṃsena api ghaṭe kiñcid  kriyate iti vaktu madhya vasitaḥ  asi tad nirūpaṇa adhīna nirūpaṇaḥ  dhvaṃsaḥ svabhāvāt eva tadīya iti kim atra sambandha antareṇa iti ced  prakṛte api evam eva etena phala anādhāra tvāt arthaḥ katham karma iti nirastam vināśyavat  karaṇa vyāpāra viṣaya tvena tad upapatteḥ svābhāvika phala nirūpaka tvañca tulyam nanu jñānam atīndriya tvāt asādhāraṇa kārya anumeyam tad abhāve katham anumīyeta apratītañca katham vyavahāra patham avataret iti jñāna vyavahārāni atha anupapattyā jñāta tā kalpanam tad api asat paraspara āśraya prasaṅgāt  jñāta tayā hi jñānam anumīyeta jñāte ca tad vyavahārāni atha anupapattiḥ tām jñāpayet  kutas ca jñānam atīndriyam indriyeṇa anupalabhyamāna tvāt iti ced  na anumāna upanyāse na pakṣe sādhya aviśiṣṭa tvāt nupalabdhi mātra upanyāse tu yogya tā viśeṣitā asau katham aindriyikā upalambha abhāvam gamayet  tad viśeṣaṇe tu katham atīndriyam jñānam iti tathāvidha jñāta tāna āśraya tvāt iti ced na āśraya asiddheḥ vyavahārāni atha anupapattyā eva siddha āśraya iti ced na jñāna hetunā eva tad upapatteḥ tasya ātma manaḥ saṃyoga ādi rūpasya sattve api suṣupti daśāyām artha vyavahāra abhāvāt na evam iti ced na tāvat mātrasya vyavahāra ahetu tvāt  anyathā jñāna svīkāre api tulya tvāt  smaraṇāni atha anupapatya iti ced na tasya api asiddheḥ asti tāvat vyavahāra nimittam kiñcid iti ced  kim atas  na hi etāvatā jñānam tad iti siddhyati tasya eva asiddheḥ tathā api niyatasya kartuḥ pravṛtteḥ kartṛ dharmeṇa eva kenacid  pravṛtti hetunā bhavitavyam iti ced  astu icchā pratyakṣa siddhā na tu jñānam sā eva katham niyata adhikaraṇe ṇa utpadyatām iti ced na jñāna abhyupagame api tulya tvāt  sva hetoḥ kutaścid iti ced  tatas  eva icchāstu kim jñāna kalpanayā iti syāt etad  prakāśamāne khalu arthe tad upāditsādiḥ upajāyate na tu suṣupti avasthāyām prakāśa māne api arthe iti anubhava siddham tatas  icchāyāḥ kāraṇam vilakṣaṇam eva kiñcid  parikalpanīyam yasmin sati susvāpa lakṣaṇam audasīnyam artha viṣayam ātmanaḥ  nivartate iti ced  hantā evam susvāpa nivṛttim anubhava niddhām pratijānānena jñānam eva aparokṣyam iṣyante acetayan  eva hi suṣupta iti ucyate acaitanya nivṛttiḥ eva hi caitanyam jñānam iti tathā ca kāla atyaya apadiṣṭaḥ  hetuḥ etena kṣaṇika tvāt iti nistam apica kim idam kṣaṇika tvam nāma yadi āśutara vināśi tvam tadā anaikāntikam atha ekakṣaṇa avasthāyi tvam tad asiddham pramāṇa abhāvāt  nanu sthāyi vijñānam yādṛśam artha kṣaṇam gṛhṇat utpadyate dvitīye api kṣaṇe kim tādṛśam eva gṛṇhāti anyādṛśam vā na vā kam api iti na prathamaḥ tasya kṣaṇasya atīta tvāt  pratyakṣa jñānasya ca vartamānā abhava tvāt na ca atītam eva vartamāna tayā ullikhati bhrāntatva prasaṅgāt  na dvitīyaḥ viramya vyāpāra ayogāt prathamatas  api tathā abhyupagame anāgata avekṣaṇa prasaṅgāt  na tṛtīyaḥ jñānatva hāneḥ iti mahāvratīyāḥ tad asat  jñānam gṛṇhāti iti asya eva ār athasya anabhyupagamāt api tu tad eva grahaṇam iti abhyupagamaḥ tathā ca jñānam prathame yam artham ālambya jātam dvitīye api kṣaṇe tad ālambanam eva tad nava iti praśna arthaḥ tatra tad ālambanam eva tad iti parama arthaḥ na ca evam bhrānta tvam viparīta anavagāhanāt tathā api jñeya nivṛttau katham jñāna anuvṛttiḥ tad anuvṛttau vā katham jñeya nivṛttiḥ iti ced  kim asmin  anupapannam na hi jñānam arthaḥ ca iti ekam tattvam eka āyuṣkam vā iti sati api vā kṣaṇika tve katham apratyakṣam ittham yathā ucyate na sva prakāśam vastutva āditara vastuvat  na ca jñāna antara grāhyam jñāna yaugapadya niṣedhena samāna kālasya tasya abhāvāt  grāhaka kāle grāhyasya atīta tvena vartamāna abhatva anupapatteḥ grāhya kāle ca grāhakasya anāgata tvāt iti ced  nanu evam jñāta tā api na pratyakṣā syāt  kṣaṇika tvāt  katham ittham na sva prakāśā vastu tvāt  na janaka grāhyā anāgata tvāt  viramya vyāpāra ayogāt ca na sama samaya jñāna grāhyā jñāna janaka indriya sambandhān anubhavāt  na ca tad uttara jñāna grāhyā tadānīm atīta tvāt  iti kṣaṇika tvam eva tasyāḥ kuta iti ced  tvad ukta yukteḥ eva tathā hi yam kṣaṇam āśritya jātā tatas  param api tam eva āśrayante anyam vā na vā kam api iti tatra na prathamaḥ tasya tadānīm asattvāt na dvitīyaḥ apratisaṅkramāt  eka kṣaṇa avagāhini ca jñāne tad anyakṣaṇa āśraya jñāta tā phala tvena bhrāntatva prasaṅgāt  rajata avagāhini puras varti vṛtti jñāta tā phala iva na ca anyam api kṣaṇam jñānam avagāhate tadānīm tasya asattvāt na tṛtīyaḥ niḥsvabhāvatā prasaṅgāt  na hi asau tadānīm tadīyāni adīyā vā iti atītena api tena eva kṣaṇena upalakṣita anuvartate iti ced  evam tarhi vartamāna artha tā prakāśasya na syāt  anyathā jñānasya api tathā anuvṛtteḥ kaḥ  doṣaḥ na hi vartamāna artha prakāśa sambandham antareṇa jñānasya anyā vartamāna avabhāsa tā nāma artha nirapekṣa prakāśana anuvṛtti mātreṇa tathā tve bhūta bhāvi viṣayasya api jñānasya tathā abhāva prasaṅgāt  atha mā bhūdayam doṣa iti sthūla eva vartamānaḥ prakāśena āśrīyate iti abhyupagamaḥ tadā tad jñānasya api sa eva viṣaya iti tasya api na kṣaṇika tvam iti nanu jñānam aindriyakam ced  viṣaya sañcāraḥ  na syāt  sañjāta sambandha tvāt  na ca jijñāsā niyamān niyamaḥ tasyāḥ saṃśaya pūrvaka tvāt  tasya ca dharmi jñāna pūrvaka tvāt  dharmiṇaḥ ca sannidhi mātreṇa jñāne jijñāsā apekṣaṇe vā ubhayathā api anavasthānāt iti tad na jñāta tā pakṣe api tulya tvāt  tasyāḥ  api hi jñeya tve tad paramparā jñāna āpātāt  jijñāsā niyamasya ca tadvat anupapatteḥ naca indriya sambandha vicchedāt virāma iti yuktam ātma prākaṭyā vyāpanāt  svabhāvata eva kācid asau  ajijñāsitā api jñāyate na tu sarva iti ced  tulyam prāk utpanna jñāta tā smaraṇa janita jijñāsaḥ samunmīlita nayanaḥ sañjāta jñāna samutpādita prākaṭyam jijñāsuḥ eva pratipadyate iti atas  na anavasthā iti ced  tulyam etad  nanu jñānam na sa vikalpaka grāhyam tasya nirvikalpaka pūrvaka tvāt  nirvikalpaka gṛgītasya tāvat kālānavasthānāt tasya tena eva vināśāt  na api kevala nirvikalpaka vedyam tasya sa vikalpa ka unneya tvena tad abhāve pramāṇa abhāvāt  na ca samavāya abhāvavat nirvikalpaka nirapekṣa sa vikalpaka gocara tvam jñānasya iti sāmpratam tayoḥ viśeṣaṇa aṃśasya prāk grahaṇāt anumāna ādivat tad upapatteḥ prakṛte tu jñānatva ādeḥ anupalabdheḥ agṛhīta viśeṣaṇāyāḥ ca buddheḥ viśeṣya anupasaṅkramāt katham evam syāt  na utpanna mātrasya eva bāhya viṣaya jñānasya ālocanāt  tatas tad puraḥsaram prathamata eva tad jātīyasya jñāna antarasya vikalpanāt  indriya sannikarṣasya tadā eva viśeṣaṇa grahaṇa lakṣaṇa sahakāri sampatteḥ vyakti antara samavetam api hi sāmānyam gṛhītam tad eva iti upayujyate anyathā anumāna ādi vikalpānām anutpāda prasaṅgaḥ tad gatasya viśeṣaṇasya agrahaṇāt anya gatasya ca anupayogāt kim liṅga grahaṇa sahakāri syāt iti etena śabda ādi pratyakṣam vyākhyātam iti syāt etad  viṣaya nirūpyam hi jñānam iṣyate na ca atīndriyasya paramāṇu ādeḥ manasā vedanam asti na ca agṛhītasya viśeṣaṇa tvam na ca nitya parokṣasya aparokṣa viśiṣṭa buddhi viṣaya tvam vyāghātāt iti na bāhya indriya grāhyasya agrāhyasya vā pūrva jñāna upanītasya eva manasā vedanāt  anyathā atīndriya smaraṇasya api anutpatti prasaṅgāt  iyān  tu viśeṣaḥ tasmin sati tad balāt eva asati tu tad janita vāsanā balāt na ca evam sati smaraṇam etad  agṛhīta jñāna gocara tvāt na ca viṣaya aṃśe tad tathā syāt iti yuktam avacchedaka tayā prāc avasthāvat avabhāsanāt  na ca pratyabhijñānam api grahaṇa smaraṇa ākāram virodhāt  atha grahaṇa smaraṇayoḥ kiyatī sāmagrī adhikor atha sannikarṣaḥ  grahaṇasya saṃskāra mātram sannikarṣaḥ smaraṇasya atha grahaṇa tve api kuta etad aparokṣa ākāram kāraṇa antara nirapekṣeṇa saṃskāra adhika  sannikarṣavata indriyeṇa janita tvāt  atha kaḥsannikarṣaḥ jñānena saṃyukta samavāyaḥ tad arthena saṃyukta samaveta viśeṣaṇa tvam iti manasaḥ  nirapekṣasya bahis vyāpāre andha badhira ādi abhāva prasaṅga iti ced  jñāna avacchedakam prati na ayam doṣaḥ na ca jñāna apekṣayā bahis iti asti na api tad viṣaya apekṣayā nirapekṣa tvam tasya eva jñānasya apekṣaṇāt atha api jñānam pratyakṣam iti atra kim pramāṇam pratyakṣam eva yad asūtrayat  jñāna vikalpānām bhāva abhāva saṃvedanāt adhyātmam  nyāya  iti nanu na īśvara jñānam pramā nitya tvena aphala tvāt  na api pramāṇam akāraka tvāt  ata eva ca na tad aśrayaḥ pramātā iti ucyate mitiḥ samyak  paricchittiḥ tadvat tā ca pramātṛ tā tad ayoga vyavacchedaḥ pramāṇyam gautame mate samīcīn  aḥ  hi anubhavaḥ pramā iti vyavastathitam tathā ca anitya tvena viśeṣaṇam anarthakam nitya anubhava siddhau tad vyavacchedabhyā aniṣṭa tvāt asiddhau ca vyavacchedya abhāvāt  na ca idam anumānam āśraya asiddhi bādhayoḥ anyatara ākrānta tvāt  na tad  pramākaraṇam iti tviṣyata eva pramayā sambandha abhāvāt tad āśrayasya tu pramātṛ tvam etad eva yad  tad samavāyaḥ kāraka tve sati iti tu viśeṣaṇam pūrvavat nirarthakam anusandheyam yadi evam  āpta prāmāṇyāt   nyāya  iti sūtra virodhaḥ tena hi īśvarasya prāmāṇyam pratipādyate na tu pramātṛ tvam iti ced  na nimitta samāveśena vyavahāra samāveśa avirodhāt  pramāsam avāyaḥ  hi pramātṛ vyavahāra nimittam pramayā tvayā ayoga vyavacchedena sambandhaḥ pramāṇa vyavahāra nimittam tad ubhayañceśvare atra api kāryayā iti viśeṣaṇam pūrvavat anarthakam ūhanīyam syāt etad  pramīyate anena iti pramāṇam pramiṇoti iti pramātā iti kāraka śabda tvam anayoḥ tathā ca katham akārakam artha iti ced  na etasya vyutpatti mātra nimitta tvāt pravṛtti nimittam tu yathā upadarśitam eva vyavasthāpanāt  anyathā asmad ādiṣu na pramātṛ vyavahāraḥ syāt  sarvatra svātantrya abhāvāt karaṇa vyavahāraḥ tu anyatra yadi api anya nimitta kaḥ  api tathā api iha ukta nimitta vivakṣayā eva iti evantarhi pañcama pramāṇa abhyupagame apasiddhāntaḥ na hi tad  pratyakṣam anumānam āgamaḥ  vā anindriya liṅga śabda karaṇa tvāt na sākṣātkāri pramāvat tayā pratyakṣa antar bhāvāt indriya artha sannikarṣa utpanna tvasya ca laukika mātra viṣaya tvāt syāt etad  tathā api īśvara jñānam na pramā viparyaya tvāt  yadā khalu etad asmad ādi vibhramānālambate tadā etasya viṣayam aspṛśataḥ  na jñāna avagāhana sambhava iti tad arthaḥ  api ālambanam abhyupeyam tathā ca tad api viparyayaḥ viparīta artha ālambana tvāt tad anavagāhane vā asmad ādeḥ vibhramān aviduṣaḥ tad upaśamāya upadeśānām asarvajña pūrvakatvam iti na vibhramasya aprāmāṇye api tad viṣayasya tattvam ullikhataḥ  abhrānta tvāt  anyathā bhrānti samuccheda prasaṅgaḥ pramāṇa abhāvāt  tathā api āropita artha vacchinna jñāna ālambana tvena katham na bhrānta tvam iti ced  na yad  yatra na asti tatra tasya avagatiḥ iti bhrānti artha tvāt etad ālambanaḥ ta ca evam ullakhataḥ sarvatra yathārtha tvāt  na hi na tad rajatam na api tatra asat  na api tad na avagatam iti sākṣāt  kāriṇi nitya yogini para dvāra anapekṣa sthitau bhūta artha anubhave niviṣṭa nikhila prastā rivastukramaḥ leśa adṛṣṭi nimitta duṣṭi vigama prabhraṣṭa śaṅkā tuṣaḥ śaṅkā unmeṣa kalaṅkibhiḥ kim aparaiḥ tad me pramāṇam śivaḥ nanu īśvare pramāṇa upapattau satyām sarvam etad evam syāt  tad eva tu na paśyāma iti ced  na hi eṣa sthāṇoḥ aparādhaḥ yad enam andhaḥ  na paśyati tathā hi kāryā ayojana dhṛtya ādeḥ padāt  pratyayataḥ śruteḥ vākyāt  saṅkhyā viśeṣāt ca sādhyaḥ  viśva vid avyayaḥ kṣiti ādi kartṛ pūrvakam kārya tvāt iti na bādhaḥ  asya upajīvya tvāt pratibandhaḥ  na durbalaiḥ siddhi asiddhyoḥ virodhaḥ  naḥ na asiddhiḥ anibandhanā tathā hi atra ye śarīra prasaṅgam udghāṭayanti kaḥ teṣām āśayaḥ kim īśvaram pakṣayitvā kartṛ tvāt śarīri tvam tatas  atha śarīra vyāvṛtteḥ akartṛ tvam atha kṣiti ādikam eva pakṣayitvā kāryatvāt śarīri kartṛka tvam yad vā śarīra ajanya tvāt akārya tvam tatas  eva vākartṛka tvam para vyāpti stambhana artham viparīta vyāpti upadarśana mātram vā iti tatra prathama dvitīyayoḥ āśraya asiddhi bādhāpa siddhānta pratijñā virodhāḥ tṛtīye tu vyāptau satyām na idam aniṣṭam asatya antu na prasaṅgaḥ caturthe bādhānekāntau pañcametu asamartha viśeṣaṇa tvam ṣaṣṭhe apinā gṛhyamāṇa viśeṣayā vyāptyā bādhaḥ na ca agṛhyamāṇā viśeṣayā vyāptyā gṛhyamāṇa viśeṣāyāḥ sat pratipakṣa tvam asti ca kāryatva vyāpteḥ pakṣa dharma tā parigrahaḥ  viśeṣaḥ kartāśarīrī viparītaḥ  na kartā iti ca anayoḥ tad virahaḥ nanu yad  buddhimat hetukam tad śarī hetukam iti niyame yad śarīra hetukam na bhavati tad  buddhimat hetukam api na bhavati iti viryaya niyamopi syāt  tathā ca pakṣa dharma tā api labhyata iti ced na gagana ādeḥ sa pakṣa bhāgasya api sambhavāt kevala vyatirekitva anupapatteḥ anvaye tu viśeṣaṇā sāmarthyāt  hetu vyāvṛtti mātram eva hi tatra kartṛ vyāvṛtti vyāptam na tu śarīra rūpa hetu vyāvṛttiḥ iti uktam vyāptaḥ ca pakṣa dharma upayujyate na tu anyaḥ  ati prasaṅgāt  etena tad vyāpaka rahita tvāt iti sāmānya upasaṃhārasya asiddha tvam uktam veditavyam na hi yad vyāvṛttiḥ yad abhāve anvaya vyatirekābhyām upasaṃhartum aśakyā tad tasya vyāpakam nāma iti viśeṣa virodhaḥ tu viśeṣa siddhau saha upalambhena tad asiddhau mithas dharmi parihāra anupalambhena nirastaḥ  na āśaṅkām api adhirohati iti syāt etad  asti tāvat  kāryasya avāntara viśeṣaḥ yatas śarīri kartṛka tvam anumīyate tathā ca tad prayuktām eva vyāptam upajīvet kāryatva sāmānyam iti syāt  na syāt  na hi viśeṣa usti iti sāmānyam aprayojakam tathā asati saurabha kaṭutva nīlim ādi viśeṣe sati na dhūma sāmānyam agniṅgamayet kim nāma sādhaka sāmānye sādhya sāmānyam āśritya pravartamāne tad viśeṣaḥ sādhya viśeṣa vyāptim āśrayet na tu viśeṣe sati sāmānyam akiñcitkaram tasya api viśeṣa antara apekṣayā kiñcid karatva prasaṅgāt  saurabha ādi viśeṣam vihāya api dhūme vanhiḥ dṛṣṭaḥ na tu viśeṣam vihāya kārye karteticed na kārya viśeṣaḥ kāraṇa viśeṣe vyavatiṣṭhate na tu kārya kāraṇa sāmānyayoḥ pratibandham anyathākuryāt iti kim na dṛṣṭam kāryam kāraṇa mātre aṅkuraḥ bīje tad viśeṣaḥ  dhānye tad viśeṣaḥ śālau tad viśeṣaḥ kalame ityādi bahulam loke kva vā dṛṣṭa maṇu dravya ārabhyam dravyam nitya rūpa ādi ārabdham rūpa ādi tathā api sāmānya vyāpteḥ avirodhāt siddhi ati eva avaśyañca etad evam aṅgīkartavyam anyathā kāryatvasya akasmikatva prasaṅgāt  syāt etad  anvayayvatireki tāvat idam kāryatvam iti parama arthaḥ tatra ākāśa ādeḥ vipakṣāt  kim kartṛ vyāvṛtteḥ kāryatva vyāvṛttiḥ āhosvit kāraṇa mātra vyāvṛtteḥ iti sandihyate tad asat  kartuḥ api kāraṇa tvāt  kāraṇeṣu ca anyatama vyatirekasya api kārya anutpattim prati prayojaka tvāt  anyathā kāraṇatva vyāghātāt karaṇa ādi viśeṣa vyatireka sandeha prasaṅgāt ca katham hi niścīyate kim ākāśāt  kāraṇa vyāvṛttyā kāryatva vyāvṛttiḥ uta karaṇa vyāvṛttyā evam kim upādāna vyāvṛttyā kim asamavāyi vyāvṛttyā kim nimitta vyāvṛttyā iti kāryatvāt  karaṇam upādānam asamavāyi nimittam vā buddhi ādiṣu na siddhyet  kartuḥ kāraṇa tve siddhe sarvam etad ucitam tad eva tu asiddham iti ced  kim paṭa ādau kuvinda ādiḥ akāraṇam eva kartā prastute vā udāsīna eva sādhayitum upakrāntaḥ tasmāt  yad kiñcid etad api iti nanu kartā kāraṇānām adhiṣṭa ātā sākṣāt vā śarītavat  sādhya paramparayā vā daṇḍa ādivat  tatra na pūrvaḥ paramāṇu ādīnām śarīratva prasaṅgāt  na dvatīyaḥ dvāra abhāvāt na hi kasyacid sākṣāt adhiṣṭeyasya abhāve paramparayā adhiṣṭānam sambhavati tad ayam pramāṇa arthaḥ paramāṇu ādayaḥna sākṣāt cetana adhiṣṭheyāḥ śarīra itara tvāt  yad punar  sākṣāt adhiṣṭheyam na tad evam yathā asmad śarīram iti na api paramparayā adhiṣṭheyāḥ sva vyāpāre śarīra anapekṣa tvāt sva ceṣṭāyām asmad śarīravat vyatirekeṇa vā daṇḍa ādi udāharaṇam evañca evam kṣiti ādi na cetana adhiṣṭhita hetukam śarīra itara hetuka tvāt iti atipīḍayā sat pratipakṣa tvam apica paṭa ādau kuvinda ādeḥ kim kāraka adhiṣṭhāna artham apekṣā teṣām acetanānām svatas  apravṛtteḥ āhaḥ kāraka tvena na pūrvaḥ teṣām parameśvareṇa eva adhiṣṭhānāt na hi asya jñānam icchā prayatnaḥ  vā vema ādīn na vyāpnoti iti sambhavati na ca adhiṣṭhitānām adhiṣṭhātṛ antara apekṣā tad artham eva tathā asatyanavasthānāt eva aviśeṣāt na dvitīyaḥ
