adhiṣṭhātṛ tvasya anaṅgatva prasaṅge dṛṣṭāntasya sādhya vikalatva āpatteḥ na ca hetu tvena eva tasya apekṣāḥ tu iti vācyam evam tarhi yad  kāryam tad sa hetukam iti vyāptiḥ na tu sa kartṛkam iti tathā ca tayai tathā e va prayoge siddha sādhanāt  kiñca anitya prayatna pūrvakatva prayuktām vyāptim upajīvat  kāryatvam na buddhimat pūrvaka tvena svabhāva pratibaddham na hi anitya prayatnaḥ  api buddhyā śarīravat  kāraṇa tvena apekṣyate yena tad nivṛttau  api akāryā r ya buddhiḥ na nivartata iti tad etad prāk eva nirasta prāyam na uttarāntaram apekṣate tathā hi sākṣāt adhiṣṭhātari sādhye paramāṇu ādīnām śarīratva prasaṅga iti kim idam śarīra tvam yad  prasajyate yadi sākṣāt prayatnavat adhiṣṭheya tvam tad iṣyata eva na ca tatas  anyat  prasañjakam api atha indriya āśraya tvam tad na tad avacchinna jñāna janana dvāreṇa indriyāṇām upayogāt  anavacchinne prayatne na ayam vidhiḥ nitya tvāt  ata eva na artha āśraya tvam na hi nitya jñānam bhoga rūpam abhoga rūpam vā yatnam apekṣate tasya kāraṇa viśeṣa tvāt  na ca nitya sarvajñasya bhoga sambhāvanā api viśeṣa adarśana abhāve mithyājñāna anavakāśe doṣa an utpattau dharma adharmayoḥ asattvāt tasmāt  sākṣāt prayatnān adhiṣṭheya tvāt  sva vyāpāre tad anapekṣa tvāt ca iti dvayam sādhya aviśiṣṭam anindriya āśraya tvāt abhoga āyatana tvāt  sva vyāpāre tad anapekṣa tvāt ca iti trayam api anyathā siddham abhoga āyatana tvāt anindriya āśrayaḥ  api bhoktṛ karma anupagrahāt abhoga āyatanam api sparśavat vegavat dravya antara nudyatvāt ta danapekṣam api syāt  acetana tvāt cetanā adhiṣṭhatam api syāt iti kaḥ  virodhaḥ tathā ca sākṣāt prayatna adhiṣṭhita itara janya tvāt iti sādhya samaḥ indriya āśrayeta rajanyatvāt bhoga āyatana itara janya tvāt iti dvayam api anyathā siddham kārya jñāna ādi avapekṣa tvāt śarīretara janyam api syāt  acetana hetuka tvāt cetana adhiṣṭhituka mapi iti kaḥ  virodhaḥ aprasiddha viśeṣaṇaḥ capakṣaḥ na hi cetanā anadhiṣṭhata hetuka tvam kvacid  pramāṇa siddham na ca cetanā adhiṣṭhita hetukatva niṣedhaḥ sādhyaḥ hetoḥ asādha araṇya prasaṅgāt  gagana ādeḥ api sa pakṣāt vyāvṛtteḥ yad punaruktam kuvinda ādeḥ paṭa ādau katham apekṣā iti tatra kārakatayā iti kaḥsandehaḥ kintu kāraka tvam eva tasya jñāna cikīrṣā prayatnavataḥ na svarūpavataḥ tad eva ca adhiṣṭhātṛ tvam yad tu adhiṣṭhite kim adhiṣṭhānena iti tad kim kuvinda udvāryate īśvaraḥ  vā anavasthā vā apādyate na prathamaḥ anvaya vyatireka siddha tvāt na dvatīyaḥ paramāṇu adṛṣṭa adhiṣṭhātṛtva siddhau jñāna ādīnām sarva viṣaya tve vema ādi adhiṣṭhānasya api nyāya prāpta tvāt  na tu tad adhiṣṭhāna artham eva īśvara siddhiḥ na tṛtīyaḥ tasmin pramāṇa abhāvāt  tathā api eka adhiṣṭhitam aparaḥ kimartham adhitiṣṭhati iti praśne kim uttaram iti ced  hetu praśnaḥ  ayam prayojana praśnaḥ  vā na ādyaḥ īśvara adhiṣṭhānasya nitya tvāt  kuvinda ādi adhiṣṭhānasya sva hetu adhīna tvāt  na dvitīyaḥ kārya niṣpādanena bhoga siddheḥ spaṣṭa tvāt  eka adhiṣṭhānena eva kāryam syāt iti ced  syāt eva tathā api na sambhede anyatara vaiyarthyam parimāṇam prati saṅkhyā parimāṇa pracayavat pratyekam sāmarthya upalabdhau sambhūya kāritva upapatteḥ asti tatra vaijātyam iti ced  iha api kiñcid bhaviṣyati iti na ca akurvataḥ kulāla ādeḥ kāya saṅkṣobha ādi sādhyaḥ  bhogaḥ siddhyet iti tad artham asya kartṛ tvam īśvaraḥ  anumanyate tad artha mātra tvāt aiśvaryasya iti yatu anitya prayatna ityādi bhavet api evam yadi anitya prayatna nivṛttau  eva buddhiḥ api nivarteta na tu etad asti udāsīnasya prayatna abhāve api buddhi sadbhāvāt  hetu bhūtā buddhiḥ nivattate ithi ced na udāsīna buddheḥ api saṃskāram prati hetu tvāt  kāraka viṣayā buddhiḥ nivartate iti ced na udāsīnasya api kāraka boddhṛ tvāt  na hi ghaṭa ādikam akurvantaḥ cakra ādikam na īkṣāmahe hetu bhūtā kāraka buddhiḥ nivartate iti ced na cakrā dibuddheḥ api saṃskāram prati hetu tvāt  kāraka phala hetu bhūtā kāraka buddhiḥ nivartata iti ced na ayatamānasya api duḥkha hetu bhūtāyā api tad hetu kaṇṭaka sparśa buddheḥ bhāvāt cikīrṣā hetu bhūtaḥ  anubhavaḥ  nivartata iti ced na kenacid nimittena akurvataḥ  api cikīrṣā tad hetu buddhi sambhava ātat anapekṣa kṛti hetu ci kīrṣā kāraṇam buddhiḥ nivartate iti ced  na tarhi buddhi mātram tathā ca anitya prayatna hetukatva prayuktam viśiṣṭa prayatna cikīrṣā hetu buddhimat pūrvakatvam iti tad nivṛttau tad eva nivartatām na tu buddhimat pūrvakatva mātram tatra tasya aprayojaka tvāt iti buddhimat pūrvakatva miti sādhya pakṣe parīhāraḥ sa kartṛkam iti prayatna pradhāna pakṣe śaṅkā eva na asti tasya eva tatra anupādhi tvāt  etena śarīra sambandhe buddhi gata kāryatvavat  buddhi sambandhe prayatna gata kārya tvam upādhiḥ iti nirastam yaḥ  hi buddhyā śarīravat śarīra nivṛttyā buddhi nivṛttivat vā prayatnena buddhim buddhi nivṛttyā prayatna nivṛttim vā sādhayet  sa evam kadācid upālabhyaḥ vayantu avagata hetu bhāvam kalita śakti sakala kāraka prayoktāram kāryāt eva anumimānā na evam āskandanīyāḥ tatra tasya anupādhi tvāt na ca prayatna ātma lābha artham eva matim apekṣate viṣaya lābha artham api apekṣaṇāt  tatas  prayatnāt buddhiḥ tad nivṛtteḥ ca prayatna nivṛttiḥ siddhyā iti vistṛtam anyatra kārya buddhi nivṛttyā tu kārya eva prayatnaḥ  nivartate na nityaḥ nitye ca prayatne nityā eva buddhiḥ pravartate na anityā na hi tayā tasya viṣaya lābha sambhavaḥ śarīra ādeḥ prāk  tad asambhave deha anutpattau sarvadā anutpatteḥ śarīra ajanya tvavat ca anitya prayatna ajanya tvam iti saṅkṣepaḥ tarka ābhāsatayā anyeṣām tarka aśuddhiḥ adūṣaṇam anukūlaḥ tu tarkaḥ  atra kārya lopaḥ  vibhūṣaṇam kāraka vyāpāra vigam e hi kārya anutpatti prasaṅgaḥ cetana acetana vyāpārayoḥ hetu phala bhāva avadhāraṇāt kāraṇa antara abhāva iva kartṛ abhāve kārya anutpatti prasaṅgaḥ kartuḥ apikāraṇa tvāt  yaḥ tu āha pratyakṣa anupalambhābhyām tad utpatti niścayaḥ  dṛśyayoḥ eva na tu adṛśyayoḥ pratyakṣasya anupalambhasya ca tāvat mātra vidhi niṣedha samartha tvāt dhūma agnivat  kampa mārutavat ca na hi dhūmaḥ kāryaḥ  analasya iti udaryasya api na hi śākhā kampaḥ  mātariśvana iti stimitasya api syāt  kintu bhauma spṛśyayoḥ eva tathā iha api śarīra vata eva kāraṇa tvam avagantum ucitam na anyasya iti tad asat  pratyakṣa anupalambhau hi dṛśya viṣayau  upāyaḥ tad utpatti niścaye na tu dṛśyatā eva tatra upeyā kinnāma dṛśya āśritam sāmānya dvayam tad ālīḍhasya hi tad utpatti niścaye dṛśyam adṛśyam vā sarvam eva tad jātīyam tad utpattimat tayā niścitam bhavati yathā sparśa rūpa rasa gandhānām uttarottara nimitta tāyām tava asmākañcā atīndriya samavāya ādi siddhau naced evam udāhṛtayoḥ eva dahana pavanayoḥ āloka rūpavatoḥ tad utpatti niścaye kathana āloka nirasta rūpayoḥ siddhiḥ yad  udari stimita sādhāraṇī siddhiḥsyāt iti tad bhavet api evam yadi śarīra ādikam vinā kāryam iva bhaumam sparśavat vegavan tañca vinā agni mātrāt  pavana mātrāt vā dhūma kampau syātām na tu evam na ca evam cetana vyabhicāraḥ  api śakya abhidhāna iti alam bāla pralāpānām samādhānaiḥ tad utpatteḥ asiddhau  api tad tad upādhi vidhūnanena svābhāvikatva sthitau yadi kartāram atipatya kāryam syāt  svabhāvam eva atipatet iti kārya vilopa prasaṅga iti etad ca sarvam ātma tattva viveke nipuṇataram upapāditam iti na iha pratanyate evañca siddhe pratibandhe na pratibandya ādeḥ pratibandya ādeḥ kṣudra upadravasya avakāśaḥ pratibandha siddha āviṣṭa āpādanāt  tad asiddhau tatas  eva tad siddheḥ aprasaṅgāt iti nanu tasya sarvadā sarvatra aviśeṣe kāryasya sarvadā utpatti prasaṅga  iti nirapekṣa īśvara pakṣe doṣaḥ sa apekṣe upekṣaṇīya eva astu iti bālasya pradīpa kalikā krīḍayā eva nagara dāhaḥ tad na sthema bhājaḥ  jagata eva akāraṇatva prasaṅgāt om iti bruvataḥ saugatasya dattam uttaram prāk   ārṣam dharma upadeśañca veda śāstra avirodhinā yaḥ tarkeṇa anusandhatte sa dharmam veda na itaraḥ manu    tam imam artham āgamaḥ saṃvadati visaṃvadati tu pareṣām vicāram  viśvatas cakṣuḥ uta viśvatomukhaḥ  viśvatobāhuḥ uta viśvataspāt  saṃ bāhubhyām dhamati saṃ patatraiḥ dyāvābhūmī janayan deva ekaḥ  atra prathamena sarvajña tvam cakṣuṣā dṛṣṭeḥ upalakṣaṇāt  dvitīyena sarva vaktṛ tvam mukhena vāc upalakṣaṇāt  tṛtīyena sarva sahakāri tvam bāhunā sahakāritvaḥ  mattvaḥ  palakṣaṇāt  caturthena vyāpaka tvam padā vyāpteḥ upalakṣaṇāt  pañcamena dharma adharma lakṣaṇa pradhāna kāraṇa tvam tau hi lokayātrā vahanāt  bāhū ṣaṣṭhena paramāṇu rūpa pradhāna adhiṣṭheya tvam te hi gati śīla tvāt patatra vyapadeśāḥ patanti iti sandhamati sañjanayan  iti ca vyavahita upasarga sambandhaḥ tena saṃyojayati samutpādayan  iti arthaḥ dyāvā iti ūrdhva sapta loka upalakṣaṇam bhūmi iti adhastāt eka iti anāditā iti smṛtiḥ api  aham sarvasya prabhavaḥ  mattaḥ sarvam pravartate  gītā    ityādiḥ etena brahma ādi pratipādakā āgamā boddhavyāḥ āyojanāt  khalu api svātantrye jaḍa tā ha aniḥ na adṛṣṭam dṛṣṭa ghātakam hetu abhāve phala abhāvaḥ  viśeṣaḥ tu viśeṣavān paramāṇu ādayaḥ  hi cetanā ayojitāḥ pravartante acetana tvāt  vā asya ādivat  anyathā kāraṇam vinā kārya anutpatti prasaṅgaḥ acetana kriyāyāḥ cetana adhiṣṭhāna kāryatva avadhāraṇāt kriyā viśeṣa viśrāntaḥ  ayam arthaḥ na tu tanmātra gocaraḥ ceṣṭā hi cetana adhiṣṭhānam apekṣata iti ced  atha kā iyam ceṣṭā nāma yadi prayatnavat ātma saṃyoga asamavāyi kāraṇikā kriyā prayatna mātra kāraṇikā iti vā vivakṣitam tad na tasya eva tatra anupādhi tvāt  atha hita ahita prāpti parihāra phala tvam tattvam tad na viṣa bhakṣaṇa udbandhana ādya vyāpanāt  iṣṭa aniṣṭa prāpti parihāra phala tvam iti ced  kartāram prati anyam vā ubhayathā api paramāṇu ādi kriyā sādha araṇyāt aviśeṣaḥ bhrānta samīhāyā atathābhūtāyāḥ  api cetana vyāpāra apekṣaṇāt ca śarīra sama vāyi kriyā tvam tad iti ced na mṛta śarīra kriyāyāḥ  api cetana pūrvakatva prasakteḥ jīvata iti ced na netra spanda ādeḥ cetana adhiṣṭhāna abhyupagama prasaṅgāt sparśavat dravya antara aprayoge sati iti ced na jvalana pavana ādau tathā abhāva abhyupagama āpatteḥ śarīrasya sparśavat dravya antara aprayuktasya iti ced na ceṣṭayā eva śarīrasyalakṣyamāṇa tvāt sāmānya viśeṣaḥ ceṣṭā tvam yata unnīyate prayatna pūrvikā iyam kriyā iti ced na kriyā mātreṇa eva tad unnayanāt  bhoktṛ buddhimat pūrvaka tvam yata iti ced  tarhi tad viśrānta tvam eva tasya na ca etāvatā eva kriyā mātram prayatna cetana mātrasya cetana adhiṣṭhānena vyāptiḥ apasāryate viśeṣasya viśeṣam prati prayojaka tayā sāmānya vyāptim pratyavirodhaka tvāt  anyathā sarva sāmānya vyāpteḥ ucchedāt iti uktam etena aśarīratva ādinā sat pratipakṣa tvam apāstam atra api āgama saṃvādaḥ  yadā sa devaḥ  jāgarti tadā idam ceṣṭate jagat  yadā svapiti śānta ātmā tadā sarvam nimīlati   ajñaḥ  jantuḥ anīśaḥ  ayam ātmanaḥ sukha duḥkhayoḥ īśvara preritaḥ  gacchet  svargam vā śvabhram eva vā   mayā adhyakṣeṇ prakṛtiḥ sūyate sacarācaram gī  tapāmi aham aham varṣam nigṛṇhāmi utsṛjāmi ca  gī  ityādi atra jāgara svāpau sahakāri lābha alābhau īśvara preraṇāya āma jña tvam aprayata māna tvañca hetū darśitau paramāṇu ādi sādhāraṇau svarga śvabhre ca iṣṭa aniṣṭa upalakṣaṇe etad eva sarva adhiṣṭhānam uttaratra vibhāvyate mayā ityādinā na kevalam preraṇāyām aham adhiṣṭhātā api tu pratirodhe api yaḥ  hi yatra prabhavati sa tasya preraṇāvat  dhāraṇe api samarthaḥ yathār avācīraḥ śarīra prāṇa preraṇa dhāraṇayoḥ iti darśitam tapāmi ityādinā dhṛteḥ khalu api kṣiti ādi brahmāṇḍa paryantam hi jagat  sākṣāt  paramparayā vā vidhāraka prayatna adhiṣṭhitam guru tve satya patana dharmaka tvāt  viyati vihaṅgama śarīravat  tad saṃyukta dravyavat ca etena indra agni yama ādi lokapāla pratipādakā api āgamā vyākhyātāḥ sarva āveśa nibandhanaḥ ca sarva tādātmya vyavahāraḥ ātmā eva idam sarvam iti yathā eka eva māyāvī  aśvaḥ varāhaḥ  vyāghraḥ  vānaraḥ kinnaraḥ  bhikṣuḥ tāpasaḥ  vipra  ityādiḥ adṛṣṭāt eva tad upapatteḥ anyathāsidhdham idam iti ced  na tad bhāvepi prayatna anvaya vyatireka anuvidhānena tasya api sthitim prati kāraṇa tvāt  kāraṇa eka deśasya ca kāraṇa antaram pratyanupādhi tvāt  upādhi tve vā sarveṣām akāraṇatva prasaṅgāt  śarīra sthitiḥ evam na tu anya sthitiḥ iti ced na prāṇa indriyayoḥ sthiteḥ avyāpanāt  prāc nyāyena apāsta tvāt ca atra api āgamaḥ  etasya vā akṣarasya praśāsane gārgi dyāvāpṛthivyau vidhṛte tiṣṭhataḥ  bṛ u  iti praśāsanam daṇḍa bhūtaḥ prayatnaḥ  uttamaḥ puruṣaḥ tu anyaḥ paramātmā iti udāhṛtaḥ yaḥ  lokatrayam āviśya vibharti avyaya īśvaraḥ  gī  iti smṛtiḥ atra uttama tvam asaṃsāri tvam sarvajñatva ādi ca parama tvam sarva upāsyatā lokatrayam iti sarva upalakṣaṇam āveśaḥ  jñāna cikīrṣā prayatnavataḥ saṃyogaḥ bharaṇam dhāraṇam avyaya tvam āgantuka viśeṣa guṇa śūnya tvam aiśvaryam saṅkalpa apratighāta iti etena kūrma ādi viṣayā api āgamā vyākhyātāḥ saṃharaṇāt  khalu api brahmāṇḍa ādi dvi aṇuka paryantam jagat  prayatnavat vināśyam vināśya tvāt  pāṭyamāna paṭavat  atra api āgamaḥ  eṣa sarvāṇi bhūtāni sva abhivyāpya mūrtibhiḥ janma vṛddhi kṣayaiḥ nityam sambhrāmayati cakravat   sarva bhūtān  i kaunteya prakṛtim yānti māmikām kalpa kṣaye punar tāni kalpa ādau visṛjāmi aham  gī  ityādiḥ etena raudram aṃśam pratipādayanta upya āgamā vyākhyātāḥ padāt  khalu api kāryatvāt nirūpa adhi tvam evam dhṛti vināśayoḥ vicchedena padasya api pratyaya ādeḥ ca pūrvavat  pada śabdena atra padyate gamyate vyavahāra aṅgam arthaḥ  anena iti vṛddha vyavahāra eva ucyate atas  api īśvara siddhiḥ tathā hi yad etad  paṭa ādi nirmāṇa naipuṇyam kuvinda ādīnām vāc vyavahāraḥ ca vyakta vācām lipitat krama vyavahāraḥ ca bālānām sa sarvaḥ svatantra puruṣa viśrāntaḥ vyavahāra tvāt  nipuṇatara śilpi nirmitā pūrva ghaṭa ghaṭanā naipuṇyavat  caitra maitra ādi padavat  patra akṣaravat  pāṇinīya varṇa nirdeśa kramavat ca iti ādimān vyavahāra evam ayantu anīdiranyathā api bhaviṣyati iticed na tad asiddheḥ ādimattām eva sādhayitum ayam ārambhaḥ na ca evam saṃsārasya anāditva bhaṅga prasaṅgaḥ tathā api tasya avirodhāt na hi caitra ādi vyavahāraḥ  ayam ādimān iti bhavasya api anāditā na asti tad anādi tve vā na caitra ādi pada vyavaha āra upyāt imān iti astu arvāgdarśī kaścid eva atra mūlam iti ced na tena aśakya tvāt kalpa ādau  ādarśa ābhāsasya api asiddheḥ sādhitau ca sarga pralayau nanu vyavahārayitṛ vṛddhaḥ śarīrī samadhigataḥ naceśvaraḥ tathā tad katham evam syāt  na śarīra anvaya vyatireka anuvidhāyini kārye tasya apita dvat tvāt gṛṇhāti hi īśvaropi kārya vaśāt śarīram antarā antarā darśayati ca vibhūtim iti atra api āgamaḥ pitā aham asya jagataḥ  mātā dhātā pitāmahaḥ gī  tathā yadi hi ayam na varteyam ya jātu karmaṇi atandritaḥ mama vartma anuvartante manuṣyāḥ pārtha sarvaśas  utsīdeyuḥ ime lokā na kuryām karma ced aham iti gī  etena  namaḥ kulālebhyaḥ karmārebhya  ityādi yajūṃṣi boddhavyāni pratyayaḥ api yāt api pratyaya śabdena atra samāśvāsa viṣaya prāmāṇyam ucyate tathā ca prayogaḥ āgama sampradāya u ayam kāraṇa guṇa pūrvakaḥ pramāṇa tvāt  pratyakṣa ādivat  na hi prāmāṇya pratyayam vinā kvacid  samāśvāsaḥ naca asiddhasya prāmāṇyasya pratītiḥ na ca svatas  pramāṇyam iti āveditam na ca na idam pramāṇam mahā jana parigrahāt iti uktam na ca asarvajñaḥ  dharma adharmayoḥ svātantryeṇa prabhavati nacā sarva jñasya guṇavat tā iti niḥśaṅkam etad  śruteḥ khalu api tathā hi sarvajña praṇītā vedāḥ veda tvāt  yad  punar na sarvajña praṇītam na asau vedaḥ  yathā itara vākyam nanu kim idam veda tvam nāma vākya tvasya adṛṣṭa viṣaya vākya tvasya ca viruddha tvāt  adṛṣṭa viṣaya pramāṇa vākya tvasya ca asiddheḥ manu ādi vākye gata tvena virodhāt ceticed na anupalabhyamāna mūla antara tve sati mahā jana parigṛhīta vākya tvasya tattvāt  na hi aramat ādīnām pratyakṣa ādi mūlam na api bhrama vipralipse mahā jana parigrahāt iti uktam na api paramparā eva mūlam mahāpralaye vicchedāt iti uktam anvayataḥ  vā veda vākyāni pauruṣeyāṇi vākya tvāt asmad ādi vākyavat  asmaryamāṇa kartṛka tvāt na evam iti ced na asiddheḥ  anantarañca vaktrebhyaḥ  vedāḥ tasya viniḥsṛtāḥ   pratimanvantarañcā eṣā śrutiḥ anyā vidhīyate   vedānta kṛt veda vid eva ca aham  iti smṛteḥ  tasmāt yajñāt  sarva hutaḥ ṛcaḥ sāmāni jajñire  ityādi śruti pāṭhaka smṛteḥ ca arthavāda mātram idam iticed na karta smaraṇasya sarvatrāvidhi artha tvāt tathā ca asmaraṇe kālidāsa ādeḥ asmaraṇāt  evañca kumāra sambhava ādeḥ akartṛkatva prasaṅgaḥ anaikāntika tvam vā hetoḥ pramāṇa antara agocara arthatva asat sat pratipakṣa tvam iti ced na praṇetāram pratyasiddheḥ anyam pratyanaikāntika tvāt  ākasmika smita bīja sukha anusmṛteḥ kāraṇa viśeṣasya anyam prati pramāṇa antara agocarasya api tena eva vaktrā pratipādyamāna tvāt  vaktā eva prakṛte na sambhavati hetu abhāve phala abhāvāt cakṣuḥ ādīnām tatra asāmarthyāt  asmad ādi indriyavat  manasaḥ  bahis asvātantryāt  na cetanasya jñānasya indriyasya manasaḥ  vā pakṣīkaraṇe āśraya asiddheḥ prāk eva prapañcanāt  nitya nirākaraṇe ca asāmarthyāt  paramāṇu ādayaḥ  na kasyacid  pratyakṣāḥ tad sāmagrī rahita tvāt iti ced na draṣṭāram pratyasiddheḥ anyam prati siddha sādhanāt  tathā api vākya tvam na pramāṇam aprayojaka tvāt  pramāṇa antara gocara arthatva prayuktam tatra pauruṣeya tvam na tu vākyatva prayuktam na sugata ādi āgamānām apauruṣeyatva prasaṅgāt  pramāṇa vākyasya sata iti ced na praṇetṛ pramāṇa antara gocara artha tvasya sādhya anupravośāt svatantra puruṣa praṇīta tvam hi pauruṣeya tvam artha prati iti eka viṣayau hi vivakṣā prayatnau svātantryam manu ādi vākyasya apauruṣeyatva prasaṅgāt ca tad arthasya śabda itara pramāṇa agocara tvāt prayujyamāna vākya itara gocara arthatva mātram iti ced na tasya vede api satvāt  ekasya api arthasya śākhā bhedena bahubhiḥ vākyaiḥ pratipādanāt  astu evam na tu teṣā mithas mūla mūli bhāva iti ced na ukta uttara tvāt  saṅkhyā viśeṣāt khalu api dvi aṇuka tri aṇuke tāvat  paramāṇavatī dravya tvāt  tad ca parimāṇam kāryam kārya guṇa tvāt  na ca tasya paramāṇu parimāṇam dvi aṇuka parimāṇam vā kāraṇam nitya parimāṇa tvāt  aṇu parimāṇa tvāt ca anyathā anāśraya kārya utpatti prasaṅgāt  dvi aṇukasya mahattva prasaṅgāt ca tri aṇukavat aṇu ārabhyatva aviśeṣāt tatra kāraṇa bahu tvena mahat tve aṇu parimāṇasya anārambhakatva sthiteḥ aṇu tvam eva mahat ārambhe viśeṣa iti api na yuktam mahataḥ  mahat anārambha prasaṅgāt  aṇutva mahat tvayoḥ viruddha tayā eka jātīya kārya anārambhakatva prasaṅgāt  bahubhiḥ api paramāṇubhiḥ dvābhyām api dvi aṇukābhyām ārambha prasaṅgāt ca evam sati kaḥ  doṣa iti ced  paramāṇu kāryasya mahattva prasaṅgaḥ kāraṇa bahutvasya tad hetu tvāt  anyathā dvābhyām tribhiḥ caturbhiḥ iti aniyamena api aṇvārambhe tad vaiyarthya prasaṅgāt  aṇuna eva tāratamya abhyupagamaḥ tu saṅkhyām avadhīrya na syāt  astu mahat ārambha eva tribhiḥ iti ced na mahataḥ kāryasya kārya dravya ārambhatva niyamāt tathā api vā tāratamye saṅkhyā eva prayojikā iti na ca pracayaḥ apekṣaṇīyaḥ avayava saṃyogasya abhāvāt  tasmāt  parimāṇa pracayau mahata eva ārambhakau  iti sthitiḥ atas  aneka saṅkhyā pariśiṣyate sā apekṣā buddhi janyā aneka saṅkhyā tvāt na ca asmad ādīnām apekṣā buddhiḥ paramāṇuṣu sambhavati tad  yasya asau sa sarvajñaḥ anyathā apekṣā buddheḥ abhāvāt  saṅkhyā anutpattau tad gata parimāṇa an utpāde aparimitasya dravyasya anārambhaka tvāt tri aṇuka an utpattau viśva anutpatti prasaṅgaḥ asmāt ādīnām evā anumānikī apekṣā buddhiḥ astu iti ced na itaretara āśraya prasaṅgāt  jāte hi sthūla kārye tena paramāṇu ādi anumānam tasmin sati dvi aṇuka ādi krameṇa sthūla utpattiḥ astu adṛṣṭāt eva parimāṇam kṛtam apekṣā buddhyā iti ced na astu tatas  eva sarvam kim dṛṣṭa kāraṇena iti ādeḥ asamādheyatva prasaṅgāt iti athavā kāryā iti ādikam anyathā vyakhyāyate uddeśa eva tātparyam vyākhyā viśvadṛśaḥ satī īśvara ādi padam sārtham loka vṛtta anusārataḥ āmnāyasya hi bhāvya arthasya kārye puruṣa pravṛtti nivṛttī bhūta arthasya tu yadi api na ahatya pravartaka tvam nivartaka tvam vā tathā api tātparyataḥ tatra eva prāmāṇyam tathā hi vidhi śaktiḥ eva avasīdantī stuti ādibhiḥ uttabhyate praśaste hi sarvaḥ pravartate ninditāt ca nivartate iti sthitiḥ tatra pada śaktiḥ tāvat abhidhā tad bala āyātaḥ padārthaḥ ākāṅkṣa ādimattve sati ca anvaya śaktiḥ padānām padārthānām vā vākyam tad bala āyātaḥ vākya arthaḥ tātparya arthaḥ tu cintyate tad eva param sādhyam pratipādyam prayojanam uddeśyam vā yasya tad idam tad param tasya bhāvaḥ tattvam tad  yad viṣayam sa tātparyārtha iti syāt  tatra na prathamaḥ pramāṇena arthasya karmaṇaḥ  asādhya tvāt  phalasya ca tad pratipattitaḥ  anyasya abhāvāt  praśasta nindita sva artha pratipādana dvāreṇa pravṛtti nivṛtti rūpam sādhyam param ucyate iti ced na gaṅgāyām ghoṣa iti atra tīrasya apravṛtti nivṛtti rūpasya asādhyasya api paratvāt  tīra viṣaye pravṛtti nivṛttī sādhye iti tīrasya api paratvam iti ced na svarūpa ākhyāna mātreṇa api paryavasānāt  na dvitīyaḥ pada vākyayoḥ padārtha tad saṃsargau vihāya pratipādya antara abhāvāt pada śakti saṃsarga śaktī vinā sva artha āvina abhāvena pratipādyam param ucyate iti api na sāma pratam na hi yad  yad śabda arthau  inābhūtam tatra tatra tātparyam śabdasya ati prasaṅgāt  tadā hi gaṅgāyām jalam ityādi api tīra param syāt  avinābhā  asya tādavasthyāt  mukhye bādhake sati tad tathā syāt iti ced  na tasmin  asati api bhāvāt  tad  yathā  gaccha gacchasi ced  kānta panthānaḥ santu te śivāḥ mama api janma tatra eva bhūyāt  yatra gataḥ  bhavān  iti mukhya artha ābādhane api vāraṇe tātparyam na ca param vyāpakam eva avyāpake api tātparya darśanāt  tad  yathā mañcāḥ krośanti iti puruṣe tātparyam na ca mañca puruṣa yoḥ avinābhāvaḥ na api puruṣa krośanayoḥ na api tṛtīyaḥ tad hi pratipādya apekṣitam pratipādaka apekṣitam vā syāt  na ādyaḥ śabda prāmāṇyasya ātad adhīna tvāt tathā tve vā atiprasaṅgāt  yasya yad apekṣitam tam prati tasya paratva prasaṅgāt  tad artha sādhya tvena apekṣā niyama iti ced na kārya jñā api abhedena sādhyasya bahuvidha tve bhinna tātparyatayā vākya bheda prasaṅgāt  dhūmasya hi pradeśa śyāmala tāmaśaka nivṛtti ādi anekam kāryam ārda indhana dahana ādi anekam jñāpyam tathā āca iha pradeśe dhūma udgama iti abhihite tātparyataḥ kaḥ  vākya arthaḥ  bhavet  cetanā apekṣāya aniyantum aśakya tvāt na api pratipādaka upekṣitam vede tad abhāvāt caturthaḥ tu syāt  yad uddeśena yaḥ śabdaḥ pravṛttaḥ sa tad paraḥ tathā eva loka vyutpatteḥ tathā hi praśaṃsā vākyam upādānam uddiśya loke prayujyate tad upādāna param nindā vākyam hānam uddiśya prayujyate tad  hāna param evam anyatra api svayam ūhanīyam tasmāt loka anusāreṇa vede api evam svīkāraṇīyam anyathā artha vādānām sarvathā eva anarthakya prasaṅgāt sa ca uddeśaḥ  vyavasāyaḥ  adhikāraḥ  abhiprāyaḥ  bhāva āśaya iti anartha antaram iti tad ādhāra praṇetṛ puruṣa dhaureya siddhiḥ tathā ca prayogaḥ vaidikāni praśaṃsā vākyāni upādāna abhiprāya pūrvakāṇi praśaṃsā vākya tvāt  pariṇati surasam āmra phalam iti ādi loka vākyavat iti evam nindā vākyāni hāna abhiprāya pūrvakāṇi nindā vākya tvāt  pariṇati virasam panasa phalam ityādi vākyavat  anyathā nirarthakatva prasaṅgaḥ ca vipakṣe bādhakam uktam apica naḥ ced evam śruta arthāpattiḥ api hīyeta siddhaḥ  hi arthaḥ pramāṇa viṣayaḥ na tu tena eva kartavyaḥ na ca pīnaḥ  devadattaḥ  divā na bhuṅkte iti atra rātrau bhuṅkta iti vākya śeṣaḥ  asti anupalambha bādhita tvāt  utpatti abhivyakti sāmagrī tālu ādi vyāpāra virahāt  ayogyasya āśaṅkitum api aśakya tvāt tasmāt abhiprāya stha eva pariśiṣyate gati antara abhāvāt sa ced vede na asti na asti śruta arthāpattiḥ iti tad vyutpādana ānarthakya prasaṅgaḥ tasmāt  kāryāt tātparyāt api unnīyate asti praṇeta iti ayojanāt  khalu api na hi vedāt avyakhyātāt kaścid artham adhigacchati na ca eka deśa darśinaḥ  vyākhyānam ādaraṇīyam  paurva aparya aparāmṛṣṭaḥ śabdaḥ  anyām kurute matim  iti nyāyena anāśvāsāt tri caturapadakāt api vākyāt eka deśa śrāviṇaḥ  anyathā artha pratyayaḥ syāt  kim uta atīndriyāt antara antarā vākya sambheda duradhi gamāt  tatas sakala veda veda artha darśī kaścid eva abhyupeyaḥ anyathā andha paramparā prasaṅgāt  sa ca śruta adhīta avadhṛta smṛta sāṅga upāṅga veda arthaḥ tad viparītaḥ  vā na sarvajñāt anyaḥ sambhavati kohya pratyakṣīkṛta viśva tad anuṣṭhānaḥ etāvān eva ayam āmnāya iti niścinuyāt  kaḥ cārvāk dṛś  niḥśeṣāḥ śratīḥ granthator athatova adhīyīta adhyāpayet vā atra api prayogaḥ vedāḥ kadācid  sarva veda artha vid vyākhyātāḥ anuṣṭhātṛ mati calane api niścala artha anuṣṭhāna tvāt  yad evam tad sarvam tad artha vid vya ākhyātam yathā manu ādi saṃhitā iti anyathā tvan āśvāsena avyavasthānāt ananuṣṭhānam avyavasthā vā bhavet anādeśika tvāt  anuṣṭhātāra eva ādeṣṭāra iti ced na teṣām aniyata bodha tvāt  vedavat veda artha anuṣṭhānam api anādi iti ced na tad hi svatantram vā veda artha bodha tantram vā ādye nirmūlatva prasaṅgaḥ dvitīye tu aniyama āpattiḥ na hi asarva jñā viśeṣe pūrveṣām tad avabodhaḥ pramāṇam na tu idānīntanānām iti niyāmakam asti padāt  khalu upi śrūyate hi praṇava īśvara īśāna ādi padam tad ca sārthakam avigānena śruti smṛti itihāseṣu prayujyamāna tvāt  ghaṭa ādi padavat iti sānāsyataḥ siddheḥ kaḥ  asya arthaḥ iti vyutpatsoḥ vimarśe sati nirṇayaḥ svarga ādi padavat   uttamaḥ puruṣaḥ tu anyaḥ paramātmā iti udāhṛtaḥ yaḥ  lokatrayam āviśya bibhartti avyaya īśvaraḥ  iti artha vādāt  yava varāha ādivat vākya śeṣāt vā tad  yathā īśvara praṇidhānam upakramya śrūyate sarvajña tā tṛptiḥ anādi bodhaḥ svatantra tā nityam alupta śaktiḥ ananta śaktiḥ ca vibhoḥ vidhi jñāḥ ṣaṣ āhuḥ aṅgāni maheśvarasya  iti evam bhūtor athaḥ pramāṇa bādhita iti ced na prāk eva pratiṣedhāt  tathā api na tatra pramāṇam asti iti ced  svarge asti iti kā śraddhā na hi ukta viśeṣaṇe sukhe kiñcid  pramāṇam asti asmad ādīnām yājñika pravṛtti anyathā anupapatyā tathā eva tad iti avadhāryate iti ced na itaretara āśraya prasaṅgāt  avadhṛte hi svarga rūpe tatra pravṛttiḥ pravṛtti anyathā anupapattyā ca tad avadhāraṇam iti pūrva vṛddha pravṛttyā tad avadhāraṇe ayam adoṣa iti ced na andha paramparā prasaṅgāt  viśiṣṭa adṛṣṭa vaśāt kadācid  kasyacid evam vidham api sukham syāt iti na asti virodhaḥ tad niṣedhe pramāṇa abhāvāt iti ced  tulyam itaratra api atra api prayogaḥ yaḥ śabdaḥ  yatra vṛddhaiḥ asati vṛtti antare pyujyate sa tasya vācakaḥ yathā svarga śabdaḥ sukha viśeṣe prayujyamānaḥ tasya vācakaḥ prayujyate ca ayam jagatkartarī iti anyathā nirarthakatva prasaṅge sārthaka pada kadamba samabhivyāhāra anupapattiḥ iti etena rudra upendra mahā indra ādi devatā viśeṣa vācakā vyākhyātāḥ apica asmat padam lokavat vede api prayujyate tasya ca loke na acetaneṣu anyatamat arthaḥ tatra sarvathā eva aprayogāt  na api ātma mātram arthaḥ para ātmani api prayoga prasaṅgāt  api tu yaḥ tam svātantryeṇa uccārayati tam eva āha tathā eva anvaya vyatirekābhyām avasāyāt  tatas  loka vyutpattim anatikramya vede api anena sva prayoktā eva vaktavyaḥ anyathā prayoga prasaṅgāt  na ca yaḥ  yadā uccārayati vaidikam aham śabdam sa eva tadā tasya artha  iti yuktam tathā asati mām upāsīta ityādau sa eva upāsyaḥ syāt aham sarvasya prabhavaḥ  mattaḥ sarvam pravartate iti upādhyāya śiṣya paramparā eva ātmani aiśvaryam samadhigacchet  tathā ca upāsanām pratyunmatta keliḥ syāt  loka vyavahāraḥ ca ucchidyeta tasmanna anuvaktā asya vācyaḥ api tu vaktā eva iti sthite prayujyate vede asmad śabdaḥ sva prayoktṛ vacanaḥ asmad śabda tvāt lokavat iti evam anye api yaḥ kaḥ sa ityādi śabdā draṣṭavyāḥ teṣām buddhi upakrama praśna parāmarśa ādi upahita maryāda tvāt tasya ca vaktṛ dharma tvāt  buddhi apakramaḥ  hi prakṛta tvam jijñāsā aviṣkaraṇañca praśnaḥ pratisandhānañca parāmarśa iti evañca saṃśaya ādi vācaka api unneyāḥ na ca jijñāsā saṃśaya ādayaḥ sarvajñe pratiṣiddhā iti yuktam śiṣya pratibodhanāya āhārya tvena avirodhāt kaḥ  dharmaḥ katham lakṣaṇaka ityādi bhāṣyavat iti etena dhik ahaḥ bata hanta ityādayaḥ  nipātā vyākhyātāḥ pratyayāt api liṅga ādi pratyayā hi puruṣa dhaureya niyoga arthā bhavantaḥ tam prati pādayanti tathā hi pravṛttiḥ kṛtiḥ eva atra sā ca icchataḥ yatas ca sā tad jñānam viṣayaḥ tasya vidhiḥ tad jñāpakaḥ  athavā pravṛttiḥ khalu vidhi kāryā satī na tāvat kāya parispanda mātram ātmā jñātavya iti ādya vyāpanāt  na api icchā mātram tatas  eva phala siddhau karma anārambha prasaṅgāt  tatas  prayatnaḥ pariśiṣyate ātma jñāna bhūta dayā ādau  api tasyāḥ sya bhāvāt  tad uktam  pravṛttiḥ āramabhaḥ  iti sā iyam pravṛttiḥ yatas sattā mātra avasthitāt  na asau vidhiḥ tatra śāstra vaiyarthyāt  apratītāt eva kutaścid  pravṛtti siddhau tad pratyāyana artham tad abhyarthana abhāvāt na ca pravṛtti hetu janana artham tad upayogaḥ pravṛtti hetoḥ icchāyāḥ  jñāna yoni tvāt jñānam anutpādya tad utpādanasya aśakya tvāt tasya ca nirālambanasya anutpatteḥ apravartaka tvāt ca niyāmaka abhāvāt tasmāt  yasya jñānam prayatna jananīm icchām prasūte sortha viśeṣaḥ tad jñāpakaḥ  vār atha viśeṣaḥ  vidhiḥ preraṇā pravartanā niyuktiḥ niyoga upadeśa iti anartha antaram iti sthite vicāryate sa hi kartṛ dharmaḥ  vā syāt  karma dharmaḥ  vā karaṇa dharmaḥ  vā niyoktṛ dharmaḥ  vā iti na prathamaḥ iṣṭa hāneḥ aniṣṭa āpteḥ apravṛtteḥ virodhataḥ asattvāt  pratyayatyāgāt  kartṛ dharmaḥ  na saṅkarāt  sa hi na spanda eva ātmānam anupaśyet iti ādi avyāpteḥ grāmam gacchati iti ādau  ati vyāpteḥ ca na api tad kāraṇam prayatnaḥ tasya sarva ākhyāta sādhāraṇa tvāt nanu na sarvatra prayatna eva pratyaya arthaḥ karoti ityādau prakṛti artha atirekiṇaḥ tasya abhāvāt saṅkhyā mātra abhidhānena pratyayasya caritārtha tvāt tatas  liṅga ādi vāt ca eva prayatna iti na kuryāt iti atra api tulya tvāt  prayatna mātrasya prakṛti artha tve api tasya parā ṅgatā āpannasya pratyaya artha tvāt na tulya tvam iti ced  na tathā api tulya tvāt  na ca ekasya tad vācaka tve anyasya tad viparyaya āpadyeta ekaḥ  dvau bahava eṣiṣati ityādau vyabhicārāt  tatra dvitīya sṅkhya icchā ādi kalpane karoti prayatate iti ādau  api tathā syāt  pratyekam anyatra sāmarthya avadhṛtau sambhede tathā kalpanāyāḥ tulya tvāt rathaḥ  gacchati ityādau tad asambhave kā gatiḥ iti ced  tantavaḥ paṭam kurvanti iti atra yā loka upacāraḥ  ayam aparyanuyojya iti ced tulyam liṅaḥ kāryatve vṛddha vyavahārāt vyutpattau sarvam samañjasam ākhyāta mātrasya tu na tathā iti ced  na vivaraṇa ādeḥ api vyutpatteḥ asti ca tad iha kim karoti pacati pākam karoti iti artha ityādi darśanāt  tathā api phala anukūla tā āpanna dhātu artha mātra abhidhāne tad atirikta prayatna abhidhāna kalpanāyām kalpanā gauravam syāt  atas  vivaraṇam api tāvat mātra param iti ced  bhavet api evam yadi pākena iti vivṛṇuyāt  na tu etad asti dhātu arthasya eva pākam iti sādhya tvena nirdeśāt  tatas tam pratyeva kiñcid anukūla tā āpannam pratyayena abhidhānīyam iti yuktam tathā api tena prayatnena eva bhavitavyam na tu anyena iti kuta iti ced  niyamena tathā vivaraṇāt  bādhakam vinā tasya anyathā kartum aśakyatvāt anyathā ati prasaṅgāt  syāt etad  yasya kasyacid  phalam pratyanukūla tā āpatti mātram eva karoti arthaḥ na tu prayatna eva saḥ  api hi anena eva upādhinā pratyayena vaktavyaḥ na tu yatnatva mātreṇa prayatna padena aviśeṣa prasaṅgāt  tad varam tāvat mātram eva astu lāghavāya anyathā tu anukūlatva prayatna tve dvau  upādhī kalpanīyau acetaneṣu sarvatra gauṇa arthāḥ tiṅaḥ  asati bādhake kalpanīyā iti ced  atra ucyate kṛta akṛta vibhāgena kartṛ rūpa vyavasthayā yatna eva kṛtiḥ pūrvā parasmin sā eva bhavanā yatna pūrvakatva m hi pratisandhāya ghaṭa ādau kṛta iti vyavahārāt  hetu sattva pratisandhāne api yatna pūrvakatva pratisandhāna vidhurāṇām aṅkura ādau tad avyavahārāt karoti arthaḥ  yatna eva tāvat avasīyate anyathā hi yad kiñcit anukūla pūrvakatva aviśeṣāt  ghaṭa ādayaḥ kṛtāḥ na kṛtāḥ tu aṅkura ādaya  iti kutaḥ vyavahāra niyamaḥ tena ca sarvam ākhyāta padam vivriyate iti sarvatra sa eva artha iti nirṇayaḥ tathā ca samudite pravṛttam padam tad eka deśe api prayujyate viśuddhi mātram puraskṛtya brāhmaṇe śrotriya padavat  anyathā api madhyama uttama puruṣa gāminaḥ pratyayāḥ prathame puruṣe jānāti icchati prayatate adhyavasyati śete saṃśete ityādayaḥ ca gauṇa arthā eva acetaneṣu na ca vṛtti antareṇa api prayoga sambhave śakti kalpanā yuktā anyāyaḥ ca aneka artha tvam iti sthiteḥ ata eva anubhavaḥ  api yāvat uktam bhavati pāka anukūla vartamāna prayatnavān tāvat uktam bhavati pacati iti evam tathābhūta ativṛtta prayatnaḥ  apākṣīt iti evam tathā bhūta bhāvi prayatnaḥ pakṣyati iti na tu pacati iti pāka ānukūlayat kiñcidvān iti anyathā atithau  api para śrama śayāne pacati iti pratyaya prasaṅgāt  apica kartṛ vyāpāra eva kṛñarthaḥ cetanaḥ ca kartā anyathā tad vyavasthā anupapatteḥ na hi abhidhīyamāna vyāpāravat tvam kartṛ tvam anabhidhāna daśāyām kurvataḥ  api akartṛtva prasaṅgāt na api ākhyāta pratyaya abhidhāna yogya vyāpāra śāli tvam kartṛ tvam yogyatāyā eva anirūpaṇāt phala anuguṇa mātrasya sarvakāra kavya apāra sādhāraṇa tvāt na api vivakṣātaḥ  niyamaḥ avivakṣā daśa āyāma niyama prasaṅgāt  sva vyāpāre na idam aniṣṭam iti ced  evam tarhi  sva vyāpāre ca kartṛ tvam sarvatra eva asti kārake  iti nyāyena karaṇa ādi vilopa prasaṅgaḥ na sva vyāpāra apekṣayā karaṇa ādi vyavahāraḥ kintu pradhāna kriyā apekṣayā asti hi kāñcid  kriyām uddiśya pravartamānānām kārakāṇām avāntara vyāpāra yogaḥ na tu avāntara vyāpāra artham eva teṣām pravṛttiḥ iti ced  tarhi tad apekṣayā eva kartṛ karma ādi vyavahāra viśeṣa niyame kim kāraṇam iti cintyatām svātantryāt iti ced  nanu tad eva kim anyat  prayatna ādi samavāyāt iti vivicya abhidhīyatām iti tasmāt  sarvatra samāna vyāpāra eva ākhyāta arthaḥ tathā api phala anuguṇa tā eva astu pratyayasya pravṛtti nimittam prayatnaḥ tu ākṣepataḥ  lapsyate iti ced na bhāvanā eva hi yatna ātmā sarvatra ākhyāta gocaraḥ tayā vivaraṇa dhrauvyāt ākṣepa anupapattitaḥ kena hi tad ā ākṣipyeta natāvat anukūlatva mātreṇa tasya prayatna tvena avyāpanāt na hi yatnatva eka artha sama vāyi eva anukūla tvam ata eva na saṅkhyayā tasyāḥ saṅkhyeya mātra paryavasāyi tvāt kartrā iti ced  na dravya mātrasya akartṛ tvāt vyāpāravataḥ ca abhidhāne vyāpāra abhidhānasya avaśya abhyupagamanīya tvāt na api dhātu arthena tad ākṣepaḥ vidyate iti ādau tad asambhavāt  na hi atri dhātu arthaḥ  bhāvanā apekṣī sat tayā nitya tvāt  tatra na bhaviṣyati iti ced  na pūrva aparībhūta bhāvanā anubhavasya aviśeṣāt bhāvanā uparāgeṇa hi atathābhūtaḥ  api arthaḥ tathā bhāsate iti na ca pada antara labdhayā bhāvanayā anukūla tāyāḥ pratyaya arthasya anvayaḥ tad asambhavāt  na khalu prakṛtyā eva sā abhidhīyate dhātūnām kriyā phala mātra abhidhāyi tvāt  anyathā pāka iti ādau  api bhāvanā anubhava prasaṅgāt  na api caitra ityādinā pada antareṇa prakṛti pratyayayoḥ ubhayoḥ api akāraka artha tvāt odanam iti ādeḥ kāraka pada tvāt  tasya ca kriyā upahita tvāt tena abhidhānam ākṣepaḥ  vā katham anyathā odanam iti ukte kim bhuṅkte pacati vā iti viśeṣa ākāṅkṣa iti ced  na pacati iti ukte kim odanam temanam vā iti viśeṣa ākāṅkṣā darśanāt  sā cākṣepa abhidhānayoḥ anyataram antareṇa na syāt  tasyām daśāyām na ced ākṣepaḥ nūnam abhidhānam eva iti syāt etad  abhidhīyatām tarhi kartā api tad anabhidhāne hi saṅkhyeya mātram ākṣipya saṅkhyā katham kartāram anviyāt  na tu karma ādikam api śāka sūpau pacati śāka sūpa odanān pacati ityādau virodha nirastā saṅkhyā caitra iti kartāram aviruddham anugacchati iti ced  caitra odanam pacati iti atrakā gatiḥ ekatra nirṇītaḥ śāstra arthaḥ  aparatra api tathā yava varāha ādivat iti ced na pacyate iti ādau  api tathā abhāva prasaṅgāt  caitrābhyām caitraiḥ iti virodha nirastā sūpa iti aviruddham karma samanukrāmati iti ced  caitra maitrābhyām pāka sūpau pacyete iti atra kā gatiḥ anyatra nirṇītena arthena vyavahāra iti ced na pacati iti ādau  api tathā abhāva prasaṅgāt  tatra pūrvaka eva nirṇayaḥ pacyate iti atratva para iti ced na viśeṣa abhāvāt ātmanepada parasma epadābhyām viśeṣa iti ced na pacyate pacate pakṣyate iti ādau viplava prasaṅgāt iti dṛśyate ca samāna pratyaya abhihitena anvayaḥ saṅkhyāyāḥ tad  yathā bhūyate supyate iti ādau na hi tatra kartrā karmaṇā vā anyena eva vā kenacid anvayaḥ kintu bhāvena eva ananvaye tad abhidhāyinaḥ  anarthakatva prasaṅgāt  ākṣiptena ca anvaye tatra api kartṛ eva anvaya āpatteḥ kaḥ  hisupyate svapiti iti anayoḥ kartṛ ākṣepam prati viśeṣaḥ syāt etad  bhāva karmaṇoḥ iti ādi anuśāsana balāt tāvat  bhāva karmaṇī pratyaya vācye tatas tad abhihitā saṅkhyā tābhyām anvīyate yaḥ tu pratyayaḥ na tatra utpannaḥ tad abhihitā saṅkhyā  mukhyam vā pūrva codanān lokavat mī  iti nyāyena kartāram eva āśrayate iti niyamaḥ na viparyyaya prasaṅgāt   śeṣāt  kartari parasmaipadam   kartari śapa  iti anuśāsana balāt bhāva kartārau pratyaya vācyau tatas tad abhihitā saṅkhyā api tābhyām anvīyate yaḥ tu pratyayaḥ na tatra utpannaḥ tad abhihitā saṅkhyā tena eva nyāyena karma eva samāśrayet iti niyama upapatteḥ tasmāt mati kardamam apahāya yathā anuśāsanam eva gṛhyate iti prāptam evam prāpte abhidhīyate ākṣepa labhye saṅkhyeye na abhidhānasya kalpanā saṅkhyeya mātra lābhe api sa ākāṅkṣeṇa vyavasthitiḥ saṅkhyā ap i tāvat iyam bhāvanā anugāminī yam yam bhāvanā anveti tam tam saṅkhyā api iti sthiteḥ eka pratyaya vācyatva niyamāt bhāvanā ca śuddham prātipadikā artha mātram ākāṅkṣati na hi vyāpāravantam vyāpāra āśrayate ātma āśrayāt samavāyam prati tad anupayogāt vijātīya vyāpāravataḥ  akartṛ tvāt ca na ca dvitīya ādyāḥ prātipadika vibhaktayaḥ tatas  prathama anirdiṣṭena eva bhāvanā anvīyate iti tasya anvaya yogya tā niyamāt saṅkhyā api tad anugāminī tena eva anvīyate iti na ati prasaṅgaḥ nañarthavat  yathā hi caitraḥ  na brāhmaṇaḥ  na gauraḥ na spandate na kuṇḍalī ityādau viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya samabhivyāhāra viśeṣe api nañā tad anabhidhāna aviśeṣe api nañarthasya viśeṣaṇa aṃśaiḥ eva anvayaḥ na viśeṣya aṃśena nanu bādhāt tatra tathā na hi viśeṣyeṇa tad anvaye viśeṣaṇa upādānam arthavat bhavet  tad niṣedhena eva viśeṣaṇa niṣedha upalabdheḥ ubha niṣedhe ca āvṛttau vākya bhedāt  anāvṛttau nirākāṅkṣa tvāt iti ced  tulya tvāt  samāna pratyaya upātta bhāvanā kṣipta anvaya upapattau bādhakam vinā sannihita tyāgena vyavahita parigrahasya guru tvāt  bhāvanāyāḥ ca sāmānya ākṣepe api sa ākāṅkṣa parityāge nirākāṅkṣa anvaya anupapatteḥ na hi anyatara ākāṅkṣā anvaya hetuḥ apitu ubhayā kāṅkṣā prātipadikā arthaḥ  hi phalena anvayam alabhamānaḥ kriyā sambandham apekṣate bhāvanā api vyāpāra bhūtā satī vyāpāriṇam iti ubhaya ākāṅkṣā anvaya hetuḥ kaṭam kaṭena ityādi tu kāraka tayā eva phala samanvitam na vyāpāra antaram apekṣate iti nirākāṅkṣam iti ata eva āsyate supyate iti ādau na ākṣiptena anvayaḥ na hi caitreṇa iti tṛtīyānta śabdasya bhāvanāyām ākāṅkṣā asti bhāvya ākāṅkṣā asti iti ced  na phalena śayana ādi dhātu arthena anvayāt phala sambandhinaḥ ca atra kartṛ anatiḥ ekāt  na hi śayanāt ayaḥ  dhātu arthāḥ kartṛ atiḥ eki sambaddhāḥ na ca phala tad sambandhi vyatirekeṇa anyaḥ  bhāvyaḥ  nāma yam apekṣeta syāt etad  kim iti na prayujyate kaṭaḥ karoti caitram ityādi abhihita anabhihita vyavasthā bhāvāt iti ced  na cetram iti prathama antasya asādhu tvāt dvitīya antasya tu karma vacana tvena tad sambandhāt  bhāvya anapekṣiṇī bhāvanā bhāvaka mātram apekṣeta na ca kaṭasya caitram pratibhāvaka tvam viryayāt  anāptena tu vivakṣāyām prayujyata eva prayujyatām tarhi kaṭaḥ karoti caitra ityādi na nitya sandigdha tvena vākya artha asamarpaka tvāt  tatas tad upapattaye viśeṣasya vyañjanīya tvāt vyajyatām tarhi tṛtīyayā caitreṇa iti evam devadattaḥ kriyate kaṭam iti vyajyatām dvitīyayā iti ced  na aprayogāt  na hi anāptena api evam prāyāṇi prayujyante lakṣaṇa avirodhena kuta etad eva iti ced  lokasya aparyanuyojya tvāt na hi gārgikayā iti padam sādhu iti ślāghā abhidhāyi pada sannidhim anapekṣya prayujyate tasya tad upādhinā eva vihita tvāt iti ced  etad eva kutas  loke tathā eva prayoga darśanāt iti ced  tulyam karoti ityādi karma vibhakti samabhivyāhāreṇa eva prayujyate kriyate iti kartṛ vibhakti sama bhavya āhāreṇa eva iti kim atra kriyatām imam eva viśeṣa murarīkṛtya anabhihita adhikāra anuśāsanena hi etāvān parāmarśaḥ sarveṣām hṛdi padam ādadhāti iti abhidhāna an abhidhāna vibhāga eva vyutpādana daśāyām peśala iti syāt etad  bhavatu sarva ākhyāta sādhāraṇī bhāvanā kāla viśeṣa sambandhinī sā laḍa ādi arthaḥ kāla traya aparāmṛṣṭā liṅā artha iti ced  na yatna padena samāna arthatva prasaṅgāt  viṣaya uparāgān uparāgābhyām viśeṣa iti ced na yāga yatna iti anena paryāyata āpatteḥ kartṛ saṅkhyā abhidhānānabhidhānābhyām viśeṣa iti ced na yāgayatnavān iti anena sāmya āpatteḥ iṣṭa eva ayam artha iti ced na itas  vatsara śatena api apravṛtteḥ phala samabhivyāhāra abhāvāt na pravarttate iti ced na svarga kāmaḥ  yāga yatna vān iti atas api apravṛtteḥ tad  kasya hetoḥ na hi yatnaḥ  yatnasya hetuḥ yatna pratītiḥ vā yatnasya kāraṇam api tu icchā na ca sā api pratītā yatna jananī yena sā eva vidhi artha iti anugamyatām api tu sat tayā na ca liṅaḥ śruti kāle sā satī na ca liṅā iva tām janayati artha viśeṣam apratyāyayantyāḥ tasyāḥ tad janaka tve vyutpatti grahaṇa vaiyarthyāt  anupalabdha liṅāñca icchā anutpatti prasaṅgāt iti etena vṛddha vyavahārāt vyutpattiḥ bhavantī bālasya ātmani pravṛtti hetuḥ yaḥ  avagataḥ tam eva āśrayet svayañca kuryām iti saṅkalpāt eva ayam pravṛttaḥ tatas sa eva liṅā artha iti nirastam kuryām iti prayatnaḥ  vā syāt icchā vā na ādyaḥ sva ātmani vṛtti virodhāt  na dvitīyaḥ sā hi sat tayā eva prayatna utpādinī na ca liṅaḥ śruti kāle sā sati iti uktam phala icchā tu nisarga vāhi tayā sati api na prayatnam prati hetuḥ anya viṣaya tvāt  tad arthañca śāstra vaiyarthyāt  tasyāḥ kāraṇa antarata eva siddheḥ tad prati iti artham api śāstra anapekṣaṇāt  tasyāḥ manaḥ vedya tvāt  aprāpte ca śāstram arthavat  prāpte ca śāstra anavakāśāt tad abhidhāne ca svarga kāma  iti kartṛ viśeṣaṇa paunaruktyāt  tadā hi yajeta iti asya eva yāga kartā svarga kāma  iti arthaḥ syāt yadica phala viṣayā eva sādhana viṣayam prayatnam janayet  anyatra api prasuvīta niyāmaka abhāvāt hetu phala bhāva eva niyāmaka iti ced na ajñātasya tasya niyāmaka tve liṅam vinā api svarga icchātaḥ  yāge pravṛtti prasaṅgāt  jñātasya tu tad sādhana tvasya niyāmaka tve tad icchā eva tatra pravartayatuḥ yaḥ  yad kāmayate sa tad sādhanam api kāmayata eva iti niyamāt  na ca sā tadānīm satī na ca tad jñānam eva prayatna janakam tad ca liṅā kriyate iti yuktam svarga kāmaḥ  yāga cikīrṣāva aniti atas  api pravṛtti prasaṅgāt  liṅaḥ  vā icchām pratītya anicchan  api sarvaḥ pravarteta sva sambandhi tayā tad avagamaḥ tathā na tu sāmānyata iti ced na prathama puruṣeṇa tad anabhidhāne tasya avidhi arthatva prasaṅgāt  odana kāmaḥ tvam pāka cikīrṣā vānityatas  api pravṛtti āpatteḥ ca tteḥ apica saṅkalpa jñānāt yadi prayatnaḥ  jāyeta tathā api saṅkalpasya kutaḥ janma kimarthañca saṅkalpa jñānāt eva prayatna arthañcā iti ced  nanu icchā viśeṣaḥ saṅkalpaḥ sa tāvat sukhe svabhāvataḥ tad sādhane caupa adhikaḥ saṅkalpa viṣayaḥ tu katham tad sādhana tvāt eva iti ced  tarhi tad sādhanatva ajñānāt na tu saṅkalpa svarūpa jñānāt bhavitum arhati iti anyathā iṣṭa sādhana tā jñānam api anarthakam āpadyeta tasmāt  saṅkalpaḥ pravartaka iti abhyupeyate kintu sattā mātreṇa na tu jñāta iti na asau vidhiḥ jñānañca viṣaya upahāreṇa eva vyavahārayati iti tad viṣaya eva avaśiṣyate iti kartṛ dharma vyudāsaḥ astu tarhi karma dharmaḥ na iti ucyate atiprasaṅgāt na phalam na apūrvam tatva hānitaḥ tad alābhāt na kāryañca na kriyā api apravṛttitaḥ   karma hi phalam vā syāt  tad kāraṇam apūrvam vā tad kāraṇam kriyā vā na prathamaḥ phala icchāyāḥ pravṛttim pratyahetutvāt  atiprasaṅgāt iti ukta tvāt  na dvitīyaḥ avyutpatteḥ liṅaḥ  hi pravṛtti nimittam apūrva tvam vā syāt  kāryatvam vā syāt  ubhayam vā na prathamaḥ śabda pravṛtti nimittasya apūrva tvasya pramāṇa antarāt avagatau  apūrvatva vyāghātāt anavagatau  avyutpatteḥ sambandhanaḥ  anavagame sambandhasya pratyetum aśakyatvāt  tatas  eva avagatau  itaretara āśraya doṣāt na ca gandhava tvena upanītāyām pṛthivyām pṛthivī śabdavat  adūra viprakarṣeṇa kāryatvena upanītena apūrva tvena nimittena apūrve pravartate liṅiti yuktam tatra ubhayoḥ api pratīyamāna tvena sandehe kalpanā gaurava puraskāreṇa pṛthivītva eva saṅgati viśrānteḥ upapatteḥ na tu atra apūrvatva pratītiḥ syāt etad  kāryatvam upalakṣaṇīkṛtya tāvat eṣā liṅ pravṛttā tad upalakṣitaḥ ca yāgaḥ  vā yatnaḥ  vā anyaḥ  vā śabda itara pramāṇa gocaraḥ  na adhikāri viśeṣaṇa svarga sādhana samarthaḥ na ca akāmya phale kāmī niyoktum śakyate tatas  anyat eva alaukikam kiñcid anena upalakṣyate yaḥ  liṅā ādi pravṛtti gocara iti kim anupapannim iti ced  na upalakṣaṇam hi smaraṇam anumānam vā ubhayam api anavagata sambandhena aśakyam na hi saṃskāravat manaḥvat dṛṣṭavat vā kāryatvam apūrva tvam upalakṣayati jñāna apekṣaṇāt  tatas  hastī iva hastipakam dhūma iva dhūmadhvajam tad sambandha jñānāt upalakṣayet  na tu anyathā tathā ca nyāya sampādana api araṇyeḥ uditam na hi yukti sahasraiḥ api avidite saṅgatigrahaḥ  avidita saṅgatiḥ vā śabdaḥ pravartate iti etena bheda agrahāt kriyā kārye vyutpattiḥ iti nirastam na hi ajñāte bheda āgrahaḥ vyavahāra aṅgam atiprasaṅgāt  kiñca apūrva tve pravṛtti nimitte kalpyamāne laukikī liṅanarthikā prasajyeta tatra upalakṣaṇīya abhāvāt tatra kāryatvam eva pravṛtti nimittam iti yadi prakṛte api tathā eva astu kḷpta tvāta sambhavāt ca iti astu tarhi tad eva pravṛtti nimittam tarka sampādanayātu pūrva vyakti lābha iti ced na nitya niṣedha āpūrvayoḥ alābha prasaṅgāt  naca asmin pakṣe ekatra nirṇītena śāstra arthena anyatra tathā eva vyavahāra iti sambhavati kāryatvasya eva pravṛtti nimitta tvena nirṇīta tvāt  na tu apūrva tvasya nyāya sampādanāyāḥ ca tatra asambhavāt  phala anuguṇyena hi vyakti viśeṣaḥ  labhyate na ca tad tatra śrūyate na ca aśrutam api kalpayitum śakyate bīja abhāvāt tad hi vidhi anyathā anupapatyā kalpyeta kāryyatva pratyayāni atha anupapatyā vā lokavat  na prathamaḥ bhavatām darśane tasya upeya rūpa tvāt yatas  śruta svarga phala tve api sādhya vivṛddhiḥ ucyate na dvitīyaḥ śabda balena tad pratyaye tad anapekṣaṇāt  loke hi tad pratyaya iṣṭa abhyupāyata adhīnaḥ na tu vede iti abhyupagamāt  anyathā iṣṭa abhyupāyata eva prathamam vedāt avagantavyā pramāṇa antara abhāvāt tatas  kāryyata iti ānumānikaḥ  vidhiḥsyāt  na śābdaḥ ānumānikam phalam astu yad kartavyam tad iṣṭa abhyupāya iti vyāpteḥ iti api na yuktam sukhena vyabhicārāt  anya tve sati iti ced na duḥkha abhāvena vyabhicārāt  phalam vihāya iti ced  tad eva kim uktam syāt  iṣṭam svabhāvata iti ced  tarhi tatas  anyat aniṣṭam syāt  tad ca kartavyam iti vyāghātaḥ tad sādhanam iti ced  tad sādhana tve sati iti sādhya aviśiṣṭam viśeṣaṇam  svabhāvataḥ  na idam iṣṭam kartavyañca tatas  nūnam iṣṭa sādhanam iti sādhana artha iti ced na svabhāvataḥ  na idam iṣṭam iti asiddheḥ ananya uddeśa pravṛtta kṛti vyāpta tvāt  anyathā tad asiddheḥ tatas  vyāghātāt anyatara apāya iti astu nitya niṣedha apūrvayoḥ alābhaḥ kim naḥ chinnam iti ced  kim naḥ chinnam yadā kāma adhikāre api tad alābhaḥ na hi liṅā kāryam svarga sādhanam uktam na api svarga kāma pada samabhivyāhārāni atha anupapatyā tad labdham brāhmaṇatva āt ivat adhi kāryavat cheda mātreṇa eva upapatteḥ naca idam anumānam yasya yad icchātaḥ  yad kartavyam tad tasya iṣṭa sādhanam iti anya icchayā svābhāvika kartavyatva asiddheḥ tad icchayā eva tad kartavya tāyāḥ sukhena anaikāntika tvāt  aupādhika kartavyatāyāḥ ca iṣṭa sādhana tvam apratītya pratyetum aśakya tvāt kim anayā viśeṣa cintayā pratīyate tāvat śabdāt anyat icchataḥ  anyat kāryam iti etāvatā eva anumānam iti ced  nanu anvitam abhidhānīyam yogyañcā anvīyate anyat icchataḥ ca anyat  kartavyam anvaya ayogyam tad katham abhidhīyatām tatas  eva tad sādhanatva siddhiḥ iti ced  evam tarhi iṣṭa sā adhana tā eka artha samavāyi kartavyatva abhidhānāt anumāna anavakāśaḥ naca anvitā abhidhāne āpi tad sādhanatva siddhiḥ adhikārya vaccheda mātreṇa api anvaya yogyata upapatteḥ na ca kārya tvam apūrve sambhavati tad hi kṛti vyāpya tā ced  vrīhi ādiṣu eva siddha tvāt  kṛti phala tvam ced  yāgasya eva tatas tasya eva ahatya utpatteḥ kṛtī uddeśya tā ced  svargasya eva nisarga sundara tvāt  na tu apūrvasya tad viparīta tvāt stana pāna ādivat aupādhikī iti ced  sā api yāgasya eva svargasya sādhyatva sthitau yāgasya eva sādhana tvena anvayāt kāla vyavadhānāt na etad nirvahati iti ced  yathā nirvahati śruta anurodhena tathā kalpyatām  vyāpāra dvārā kathañcid  syāt  na tu bhinna kālayoḥ vyāpāra vyāpāribhāvaḥ kāraṇatvañca vyāpāreṇa yujyate avyavadhānena pūrva kāla niyamḥ ca tattvam anyathā ati prasaṅgā aditi ced  na pūrva bhāva niyama mātrasya kāraṇa tvāt  kārya anuguṇa avāntara kāryasya eva vyāpāra tvāt  kṛṣi cikitsā ādau bahulam tathā vyavahārāt  lākṣaṇikaḥ  asau  iti ced na mukhya artha tve virodha abhāvāt astu tarhi putreṇa hate brahmaṇi ciradhvastasya pituḥ tam avāntara vyāpārīkṛtya kartṛ tvam tathā ca lokayātrā viplava iti ced  na sati api sute kadācid tad akaraṇāt tasmin  asati api kadācid kāraṇāt anirvāhaka tayā tasya vyāpāratva ayogāt yam janayitvā eva hi yam prati yasya pūrva bhāva nirvāhaḥ sa eva tam prati tasya vyāpāraḥ  na aparaḥ yathā anubhavasya smaraṇam prati saṃskāraḥ tasya hi anvaya vyatireka anuvidhāne siddhe tad anyathā anupapatyā saṃskāraḥ kalpyate na tu anyathā tathā iha api na ced evam tava api brahma bhidura śara vimoka sama samaya hatasya hantṛ tvam na syāt  syāt ca sva niveśana śayānasya tad pituḥ iti etena ubhayam na iti nirastam astu tarhi kriyā dharma eva kāryatvam vidhiḥ sarvaḥ hi kartavyam etad iti pratyeti tatas  kuryām iti saṅkalpya pravartate iti ced  na kartavyam mayā iti kṛtī adhyavasāya arthaḥ  vā syāt  kartavyam mayā iti ucita arthaḥ  vā syāta tatra prathamaḥ saṅkalpān na bhidyate vyavahita kārya saṅkalpaḥ  hi kartavyaḥ  mayā iti sannihita kārya saṅkalpaḥ tu kuryām iti sa ca na liṅā arthaḥ sattā mātreṇa pravartanāt iti uktam tad etad kartavyatāyām jātāyām pravartate iti vastu sthitau bhrāntaiḥ jñātāyām iti gṛhītam aucityantu kriyā dharmaḥ prāgabhāvavat tvam tasmin sati śakya tvam vā tasmin sati kartāram pratyupakāraka tvam vā prathame kutaścid api na nivarteta dvitīye duḥkhe api tathāvidhe pravarteta tṛtīye tu vakṣyate astu tarhi karaṇa dharmaḥ na karaṇam hi śabdaḥ tad dharmaḥ  abhidhā vā syāt  tad arthaḥ  bhāvanā ādiḥ vā tad dharma iṣṭa sādhana tā vā na prathamaḥ asattvāt apravṛtteḥ ca na abhidhā api garīyasī bādhakasya samāna tvāt  pariśeṣaḥ  api durlabhaḥ saṅgati pratisandhāna adhikāyā m tasyām pramāṇa abhāvāt  anya samavetasya apūrvavat anya vyāpāra tvena api upapatteḥ viṣaya tayā api viṣaya tāyām api ca sva vyāpāram pratiliṅgavat hetu bhāva avirodhāta adhikattve api tatas  apravṛtteḥ bālānām tad abhāve api tad bhāvāt śabda antareṇa tad śrāviṇām api apravṛtteḥ na ca vilakṣaṇā eva sā liṅaḥ  viṣayaḥ tad vailakṣyaṇyam pratītim pratipattim prati ced  artha viśeṣaḥ  api syāt  pravṛtti mātram prati ced  abhidhā samavetam tad iti kutas  tad sannidhānāt iti ca id naḥ aniyamāt  anyasya sarvasya niṣedhāt iti ced na pravṛtti hetuttva niṣedhasya tulya tvāt  tad sannidhi niṣeṣasya ca aśakya tvāt śabda eka vedya tve ca avyutpatteḥ  pravṛtti anyathā anupapatti siddhe vyutpatti ariti api vārtam na hi pravṛtti hetuḥ kaścid asti iti pravartate iṣṭa sādhana tā tu syāt  sarvaḥ  hi mayā kriyamāṇam etad mama samīhitam sādhayiṣyati iti pratisandhatte tatas  icchati kuryām iti tatas  karoti iti sarva anubhava siddham tad ayam vyutpitsuḥ yad jñānāt  prayatna jananīm icchām avāptavān tad jñānam eva liṅśrāviṇaḥ pravṛtti kāraṇam anuminoti tatas ca kartavyatā eka artha samavāyinī iṣṭa sādhana tā āliṅā artha iti avadhārayati na ca vācyam evañcet  varam kartavyatā eva astu avaśya abhyupagamanīya tvāt kṛtam iṣṭa sādhanatayā iti yathā hi na iṣṭa sādhana tā mātram pratītya pravartate asādhyeṣu vyabhicārāt  tathā prayatna viṣaya sama vāyinīm iṣṭa sādhana tām adhigamya adhikārī pravartate iti anubhavaḥ tatra viṣayaḥ  dhātunā bhāvanā akhyāta mātreṇa śeṣantu tad viśeṣeṇa liṅā iti evam iṣṭa abhyupāya tāyām adhigatāyām anvaya balāt tad viṣayasya iṣṭa sādhanatva avagatiḥ iti kartavyatā eka artha samavāyini iṣṭa abhyupāya tāta liṅāḥ pravṛtti nimittam iti uktam karaṇasya iṣṭa sā adhana tā abhidhāne jyotiṣṭomena iti tṛtīyayā na bhavitavyam iti tu deśyam avaiyākaraṇasya avadhīraṇīyam eva tad saṅkhyā abhidhānam hi tad abhidhānam ākhyātena na ca tad  prakṛte na ca yāga iṣṭa sādhana tā abhidhānam liṅā kintu anvaya balāt talābha iti uktam yad tu siddhā ddhaḥ  padeśāt api pratīyate iṣṭa sādhana tā na ca atas  saṅkalpa ātmā pravṛttiḥ asti iti deśyam tatra samutkaṭa phala abhilāṣasya samarthasya tad sādhana tau  ahame api na pravṛttiḥ iti kaḥ pratīyāt  sarva pakṣa samānañca etad  samāna parīhārañca iti kim tena atra abhidhīyate astu prayatna viṣaya samavāyini iṣṭa sādhana tā pravṛtti hetuḥ tathā api na asau liṅā arthaḥ sandehāt  sā hi kim sākṣāt eva liṅā avagamyate stana pāna ādau  anu mānāt iva bālena kim vā tad pratipāditāt kutaścid arthāt anumīyate ceṣṭā viśeṣa anumita āt iva abhipraya viśeṣāt samayā abhijñena iti sandihyate evañca sati sā na abhidhīyate iti eva nirṇayaḥ hetu tvāt anumānāt ca madhyamādau viyogataḥ anyatra kḷpta sāmarthyāt niṣedha anupapattitaḥ tathā hi agni kāmaḥ  dāruṇī mathnīyāt iti śrutvā kuta iti ukte vaktāraḥ  vadanti yatas tad manthanāt agniḥ arasya sidhyati iti tarati mṛtyum tarati brahmahatyām yaḥ  aśvamedhena yajate iti ādā  iṣṭa abhyupāya tāyām eva avagatāyām anumimate tāntrikāḥ yad   aśvamedhena yajeta mṛtyu brahma hatyā taraṇa kāma  ityādi vidhim nindayā ca niṣedham tad yathā  andham tamaḥ praviśanti ye ke ca ātma hanaḥ  janāḥ  iti atas  na ātmānam hanyāt iti kuryyāḥ kuryyām iti atra vidhi vihitā eva liṅ na iṣṭā abhyupāyatām āha kintu vaktṛ saṅkalpam na hi iṣṭa abhyupāyaḥ  mama ayam iti kuryām iti padārthaḥ kintu tad pratipatteḥ anantaram yaḥ  asya saṅkalpaḥ kuryām iti sa eva sarvatra ca anyatra vaktuḥ eva icchā abhidhīyate liṅā iti avadhṛtam tathā hi ājñādhyeṣaṇa anujñā sampraśna prārthanā āśaṃsā liṅinā an yad cakāsti yām vaktuḥ icchām ananu vidadhānaḥ tad kṣobhāt bibheti sā ājñā yā tu śrotuḥ pūjā saṃmāna vyañjikā sā adhyeṣaṇā vāraṇa abhāva vyañjikā anujñā abhidhāna prayojanā sampraśnaḥ lobha icchā prārthanā śubha āśaṃsanam āśīḥ iti na ca vidhi vikalpeṣu niṣedha upapadyate tathā hi yadā abhidhā vidhiḥ tadā na hanyāt  hanana bhāvanā na abhidhīyata iti vākya arthaḥ  vyāghātāt nirastaḥ yadā kāla traya aparāmṛṣṭā bhāvanā tadā na iti sambandhe atyanta abhāvaḥ  mithyā yadā kāryam tadā na hanyāt  na hananam kāryam iti anubhava viruddham kriyata eva yatas  na hananena kāryam hanana kāraṇakam kāryam na asti iti artha iti api na asti duḥkha nivṛtti sukha āptyoḥ anyatarasya tatra sadbhāvāt  hanana kāraṇakam adṛṣṭam mapūrvam na asti iti artha iti tu nirātaṅkam dṛṣṭa arthinam pravartayet eva iti sādhu śāstra arthaḥ ahananena apūrvam bhāvayet iti tu aśakyam kāraṇasya anādi tvena kāryasya api tathā abhāva prasaṅgāt  bhāvanāyāḥ ca tad aviṣaya tvāt ahanana saṅkalpena iti yāvat jīvam avicchinni tad saṅkalpaḥ syāt sakṛt kṛtvā evavā nivṛttiḥ paścāt hanyāt eva avirodhāt  sampāditaḥ  hi anena niyoga arthaḥ  yāvat yāvat dhanana saṅkalpavān tāvat tāvat viparīta saṅkalpena apūrvam bhāvayet iti vākya arthaḥ tathābhūtasya adhikāritvā aditi api vārtam tad aśruteḥ prasaktam hi pratiṣidhyate na aprasaktam iti ced  na vai kiñcid iha pratiṣidhyate tad abhāvaḥ pratipādyate iti niṣedha arthaḥ ahanana saṅkalpa karaṇa kamapūrvam vākya arthaḥ kiñca na hanyāt iti ahananena apūrvasya kartavya tā pratyayaḥ  jātaḥ  vedāt  jātaḥ ca hanana kriyāyām rāgāt  niṣphalāt ca kāryāt apekṣita phalaṅgarīya iti nyāyena hanyāt eva iti ahaḥ veda vyākhyā kauśalam āstikya abhimāninaḥ  mīmāṃsaka durdurūṭasya iṣṭa sādhana tā pakṣe api na hanyāt  na hanana bhāvanā iṣṭa abhyupāya iti vākya arthaḥ tathā ca aniṣṭa sādhantvam kutaḥ labhyate na hi iṣṭa sādhanam yad na bhavati tad avaśyam aniṣṭa sādhanam dṛṣṭam upekṣaṇīyasya api bhāvāt   yad  rāga ādi prasaktam pratiṣidhyate tad avaśyam aniṣṭa sādhanam dṛṣṭam yathāsaviṣam annam na bhuñjīthā iti tena vede api anumāsyate  iti api na sādhīyaḥ pratiṣedha arthasya eva cintyamāna tvāt  na hi kartavya tvasya iṣṭa sā adhana tvasya bhāvanāyāḥ  vābhāvaḥ pratipādayitum śakyate laukikānām laukika pramāṇa siddha tvāt  tathā api pratipādyate tāvat iti ced na pāṣaṇḍa āgama niṣedhena anekāntāt  na asau pramāṇam iti ced na artha viparyaya pratipādana aviśeṣe asya api tathā abhāvāt tātparyyataḥ prāmāṇyam iti ced na vidhi niṣedhayoḥ ananya paratvāt na vidhau paraḥ śabda artha iti vacanāt  tathā api niṣedhe tathā bhaviṣyati iti ced na avinā abhāva tad uddeśa pravṛttyoḥ abhāvāt na api asurā vidyā ādi vadasya nañaḥ  virodhi vacana tvam kriyā saṅgata tvāt asamasta tvāt ca tasmāt  vidhiḥ vaktuḥ abhiprāyaḥ pravṛtti ādau liṅā ādibhiḥ abhidheyaḥ  anumeyā tu kartariṣṭa abhyupāya tā tatra svayaṅkartṛka kriyā icchā abhidhānam kuryām iti sambodhya kartṛka kriyā icchā abhidhānam kuryā iti śeṣa kartṛka kriyā icchā abhidhānam kurvīta iti tathā ca agni kāmaḥ  dāruṇī mathnīya ādityasya laukika vākyasi ayam arthaḥ sampadyate agni kāmasya dāru mathane pravṛttiḥ mama iṣṭa iti tatas  śrotā anum inoti nūnam kārumathana yatnaḥ  agneḥ upāya iti yad viṣayaḥ  hi prayatnaḥ  yasya āptena iṣyate sa tasya apekṣita hetu tathā tena avagataḥ ca yathā mama e yai va putra ādeḥ bhojana viṣayaḥ iti vyāpteḥ viṣam na bhakṣayet iti asya tu viṣa bhakṣaṇa gocarā pravṛttiḥ mama na iṣṭā iti arthaḥ tatas  api śrotā anum inoti nūnam viṣa bhakṣaṇa bhāvanā aniṣṭa sādhanam yad viṣayaḥ  hi prayatnaḥ kartuḥ abhimata sādhaka upya āptena na iṣyate sa tatas  adhikatara anartha hetuḥ tathā tena avagataḥ ca yathā mama e yai va putra ādeḥ krīḍā kardama viṣa bhakṣaṇa ādi viṣaya iti vyāpteḥ laukika eva vākye ayam prakāraḥ kadācid buddhim adhirohati na tu vedikeṣu teṣu puruṣasya nirasta tvāt iti ced na nirāsa hetoḥ abhāvāt  tad astitve api pramāṇam na asti iti ced  mā bhūt anyat  vidhiḥ eva tāvat  garbha iva puṃyoge pramāṇam śruti kumāryāḥ kim atra kriyatām liṅaḥ  vā laukika artha atikrame   ya eva laukikāḥ ta eva vaidikāḥ ta eva ca eṣām arthā  iti viplaveta tathā ca jabagaḍa daśa ādivat anarthakatva prasaṅga iti bhava susthaḥ syāt etad  tathā api vaktṝṇām upādhyāyānām eva abhiprāyaḥ  vede vidhiḥ astu kṛtam svatantreṇa vaktrā parameśvareṇa iti ced  na teṣām anuvaktṛtayā abhyāsa abhiprāya mātreṇa pravṛtteḥ śuka ādivat  tathāvidha abhiprāya abhāvāt bhāve vā na rāja śāsana anuvādinaḥ  abhiprāya ājñā kim nāma rājña eva iti laukikaḥ  anubhavaḥ śruteḥ khalu api kṛtsna eva hi vedaḥ  ayam parameśvara gocaraḥ sva artha dvārā evatāt paryyam tasya svarga ādivat vidhau na santi eva hi veda bhāgāḥ yatra parameśvaraḥ  na gīyate tathā hi sraṣṭṛ tvena puruṣasūkteṣu vibhūtyā rudreṣu śabdabrahma tvena maṇḍala brāhmaṇeṣu pravañcam puraskṛtya niṣprapañca tayā upaniṣatsu yajñapuruṣa tvena mantra vidhiṣu deha āviḥ bhāvaiḥ upākhyāneṣu upāsya tvena ca sarvatra iti siddhārtha tayā na te pramāṇam iti ced na tad hetu toḥ kāraṇa doṣa śaṅkā nirāsasya bhāvya bhūta artha sādhāraṇa tvāt anyatra amīṣām tātparyam iti ced  sva artha pratipādana dvārā śabda mātra tayā vā prathame sva arthe api pramāṇyameṣitavyam tasya arthasya ananya pramāṇaka tvāt  ata eva tatra tasya smāraka tvam iti api mithyā tad pratipādaka tve api na tatra tātparyam iti ced  sva artha aparityāge gena jyotiḥśāstravat anyatra api tātparye kaḥ  doṣaḥ anyathā svarga naraka vrātya śrotriya ādi svarūpa pratipādakānām aprāmāṇye bahu viplaveta tatra ābādhanāt tathā iti ced  tulyam na tādṛśaḥ  gar thaḥ kvacid  dṛṣṭa iti ced  svargāt ayaḥ  api tathā tad mithyātvetad arthi nām apravṛttau vidhāna ānarthakya prasaṅga iti ced  iha api tad upāsana avidhāna ānarthakya prasaṅgaḥ tad mithyā tve hi sālokya sāyujya ādi phala mithyā tve kaḥ prekṣāvān  tam upāsīta iti tulyam iti vākyāt api saṃsarga bheda viśeṣa pratipādaka tvam hi atra vākya tvam abhipretam tathā ca yad pada kadambakam yad saṃsarga bheda pratipādakam tad  tad anapekṣa saṃsarga jñāna pūrvakam yathā laukikam tathā ca vaidikam iti prayogaḥ vipakṣe ca bādhakam uktam saṅkhyā viśeṣāt api syām abhūvam bhaviṣyāmi ityādi saṅkhyā ca vaktṛ gā samākhyā api na śākhānām ādya pravacanāt ṛte kārya tayā hi prāk  saṅkhyā uktā samprati tu pratipādyatayā ucyate tathā hi uttama puruṣa abhihitā saṅkhyā vaktāram anveti iti su prasiddham asti ca tad prayogaḥ prāyaśas  vede tatas tad abhihitayā tayā api sa eva anugantavyaḥ anyathā ananvaya prasaṅgāt  athavā samākhyā viśeṣaḥ saṅkhyā viśeṣa ucyate kāṭhakam kālāpakam ityādayaḥ  hi samākhyā viśeṣāḥ śākhā viśeṣāṇām anusmaryante te ca na pravacana mātra nibandhanāḥ pravaktṝṇām ananta tvāt  na api prakṛṣṭa vacana nimittāḥ upādhyāyebhyaḥ  api prakarṣe pratyutānyathā karaṇa doṣāt tad pāṭhā anukaraṇe ca prakarṣa abhāvāt kati ca anādau saṃsāre prakṛṣṭāḥ pravaktāra iti kaḥ  niyāmaka iti na api ādyasya vaktuḥ samākhyā iti yuktam bhavadbhiḥ tad anabhyupagamāt  abhyupagame vā sa eva asmākam vedakāra iti vṛthā vipratipattiḥ syāt etad  brāhmaṇa tve satyavāntara jāti bhedā eva kaṭhatva ādayaḥ tad adhyeyā tad anuṣṭheya arthā ca śākhā tad samākhyayā vpapadiśyate iti kim anupapannam na kṣatriya ādeḥ api tatra eva adhikārāt na ca yaḥ  brāhmaṇasya viśeṣaḥ sa kṣatriya ādau sambhavati na ca kṣatriya ādeḥ anyaḥ  veda iti asti na ca kaṭhāḥ kāṭhakam eva ādhīyate tad artham eva anutiṣṭhanti iti niyamaḥ śākhā sañcārasya api prāyaśas  darśanāt  prāk evam vāyam niyama āsīt  idānī mayam viplavate iti ced  viplava eva tarhi sarvadā kaṭhādi avāntara jāti viplava āditya gatiḥ eva iyam tasmāt ādya pravaktṛ vacana nimitta eva ayam samākhyā viśeṣa sambandha iti eva sādhyiti śrīḥ sa evam bhagavān śrutaḥ  anumitaḥ ca kaiścid  sākṣāt api dṛścate prameya tvādergha tvāt  gha ṭavat  nanu tad sāmagrī rahitaḥ katham draṣṭavyaḥ sā hi bahis indriya garbha manaḥ garbhā vā tatra na sambhavati cakṣuḥ ādeḥ niyata viṣaya tvāt manasaḥ  bahis asvātantryāt  tad uktam  hetu abhāve phala abhāvā adityādi na kāryā eka vyaṅgyāyāḥ sāmagryā niṣeddhum aśakyatvāt  apica dṛśyate tāvat bahis indriya uparame api asat nihita deśa kāla artha sākṣātkāraḥ na ca smṛtiḥ eva asau paṭīyasī  smarāmi   smṛtam  vā iti svapna anusandhāna abhāvāt  paśyāmi    dṛṣṭa  miti anuvyavasāyāt  naca āropitam tatra anubhava tvam abādhanāt  ananubhūtasya api sva śira  chedana ādeḥ avabhāsanāt ca smṛti viparyāsaḥ  asau  iti ced  yadi smṛti viṣaye viparyāsa iti arthaḥ tadā anumanyāmahe atha smṛtau  eva anubhavatu viparyāsaḥ iti tadā prāk eva nirastaḥ na ca sambhavati api na hi anyena ākāreṇa adhyavasitaḥ  anyena jñāna avacchedakatayā adhyavasīyate tathā ca sa ghaṭa iti utpannāyām smṛtau bhrāmyataḥ tam ghaṭam anubhavāmi iti syāt  na tu imam ghaṭam iti na hi ayam ghaṭa iti smṛteḥ ākāraḥ tasmāt anubhava eva asau svīkartavyaḥ asti ca svapna anubhavasya api kasyacid  satya tvam saṃvādāt  tad ca kākatālīyam api na nirnimittam sarva svapna jñānānām api tathātva prasaṅgāt  hetuḥ ca atra dharma eva sa ca karma javat  yoga jaḥ  api yoga vidheḥ avaseyaḥ karma yoga vidhyoḥ tulya yogakṣema tvāt  tasmāt  yoginām anubhavaḥ  dharmaja tvāt  pramā sākṣātkāri tvāt  pratyakṣa phalam dharmān anugṛhīta bhāvanā mātra prabhavaḥ tu na pramā iti vibhāga iti atas tad sāmagrī virahaḥ  asiddhaḥ tathā api vipakṣe kim bādhakam iti ced   dve brahmaṇī veditavye  ityādi yoga vidhi vaiyarthya prasaṅgaḥ aśakya anuṣṭhāna upāya upadeśaka tvāt  na ca asākṣātkāri jñāna vidhānam etad  artha jñāna avadhinā adhyayana vidhinā eva tasya gata artha tvāt iti etena paramāṇu ādayaḥ  vyākhyātā iti tad enam evam bhūtam adhikṛtya śrūyate  na draṣṭuḥ dṛṣṭeḥ viparilopaḥ  vidyate  iti  ekam eva ādvitīya am iti  paśyati acakṣuḥ sa śṛṇoti akarṇa  iti  dve brahmaṇī veditavye parañca aparam eva ce ati  yajñena yajñam ayajanta devā  iti yajñaḥ  vai devāḥ  iti  yajñaḥ  vai viṣṇu aratyādi smaryate ca gī   sarva dharmān parityajya mām ekam śaraṇam vraja  iti  mad artham karma kaunteya mukta saṅgaḥ samācara  iti  yajña arthāt  karmaṇaḥ  anyatra lokaḥ  ayam karma bandhana  iti  yajñāya ācarataḥ karma samagram pravilīyate  ityādi anuśiṣyate ca sāṅkhya pravacane īśvara praṇidhānam tam imam jyotiṣṭoma ādi bhiḥ iṣṭaiḥ prāsāda ādinā pūrtena śīta ātapa sahana ādinā tapasā ahiṃsā ādibhiḥ yamaiḥ śauca santoṣa ādibhiḥ niyamaiḥ āsana prāṇāyāma ādinā yogena mahā ṛṣa yaḥ  api vividiṣanti tasmin jñāte sarvam idam jñātam bhavati iti evam vijñāya śrutvā ekatānaḥ tad paraḥ  bhavet  yad tedam gīyate  mad manāḥ  bhava mad bhaktaḥ  mad yājī mām namaskuru mām eva eṣyasi yuktvā evam ātmānam mad parāyaṇaḥ   bhoktāram yajña tapasām sarva loka maheśvaram suhṛdam sarva bhūtānām jñātvā mām śāntim ṛcchati  iti iti evam śruti nīti samplava jalaiḥ bhūyobhiḥ ākṣālite yeṣām na āspadam ādadhā asi hṛdaye te śaula sāra āśayāḥ kint u prastuta vipratīpavidhayaḥ  api uccais bhavat cintakāḥ kāle kāruṇika tvayā eva kṛpayā te bhāvanīyā narāḥ asmākam tu nisarga sundara cirāt cetaḥ  nimagnam tvayī tyaddhā ananda nidhe tathā api taralam na adya api santṛpyate tad nātha tvaritam vidhehi karuṇām yena tvad ekāgra tām yāte cetasi na āpnuvāma śataśas  yāmyāḥ punar yātanāḥ iti eṣa nīti kusuma añjaliḥ ujjvala śrīḥ yad vāsayet api ca dakṣiṇa vāmakau gau dvau naḥ vā tatas  kim amara īśa guroḥ guruḥ tu prītaḥ  astu anena pada pīṭha samarpitena r
